February 03, 2026

LangMap: A Hierarchical Benchmark for Open-Vocabulary Goal Navigation

Abstract (English): The relationships between objects and language are fundamental to meaningful communication between humans and AI, and to practically useful embodied intelligence. We introduce HieraNav, a multi-granularity, open-vocabulary goal navigation task where agents interpret natural language instructions to reach targets at four semantic levels: scene, room, region, and instance. To this end, we present Language as a Map (LangMap), a large-scale benchmark built on real-world 3D indoor scans with comprehensive human-verified annotations and tasks spanning these levels. LangMap provides region labels, discriminative region descriptions, discriminative instance descriptions covering 414 object categories, and over 18K navigation tasks. Each target features both concise and detailed descriptions, enabling evaluation across different instruction styles. LangMap achieves superior annotation quality, outperforming GOAT-Bench by 23.8% in discriminative accuracy using four times fewer words. Comprehensive evaluations of zero-shot and supervised models on LangMap reveal that richer context and memory improve success, while long-tailed, small, context-dependent, and distant goals, as well as multi-goal completion, remain challenging. HieraNav and LangMap establish a rigorous testbed for advancing language-driven embodied navigation. Project: https://bo-miao.github.io/LangMap

摘要（中文）: 对象和语言之间的关系对于人类和人工智能之间有意义的沟通，以及在实践中具有实用性的具身智能至关重要。我们引入了HieraNav，这是一个多粒度、开放词汇的目标导航任务，其中智能体解释自然语言指令，以达到四个语义级别的目标：场景、房间、区域和实例。为此，我们提出了Language as a Map (LangMap)，这是一个基于真实3D室内扫描构建的大规模基准，具有全面的人工验证标注和跨越这些级别的任务。LangMap提供区域标签、可区分的区域描述、涵盖414个对象类别的可区分的实例描述，以及超过18K个导航任务。每个目标都具有简洁和详细的描述，从而可以评估不同指令风格的表现。LangMap实现了卓越的标注质量，在使用四分之一单词的情况下，其区分准确率比GOAT-Bench高出23.8%。通过对LangMap上的零样本和监督模型进行全面评估，发现更丰富的上下文和记忆有助于提高成功率，而长尾、小、上下文相关和远距离目标，以及多目标完成仍然具有挑战性。HieraNav和LangMap为推进语言驱动的具身导航建立了一个严格的测试平台。项目地址：https://bo-miao.github.io/LangMap

TLDR: The paper introduces LangMap, a large-scale benchmark for open-vocabulary goal navigation with multi-granularity targets and human-verified annotations, designed to advance language-driven embodied navigation.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了LangMap，一个用于开放词汇目标导航的大规模基准，具有多粒度目标和人工验证的注释，旨在推进语言驱动的具身导航。

Authors: Bo Miao, Weijia Liu, Jun Luo, Lachlan Shinnick, Jian Liu, Thomas Hamilton-Smith, Yuhe Yang, Zijie Wu, Vanja Videnovic, Feras Dayoub, Anton van den Hengel

Concept-Based Dictionary Learning for Inference-Time Safety in Vision Language Action Models

Abstract (English): Vision Language Action (VLA) models close the perception action loop by translating multimodal instructions into executable behaviors, but this very capability magnifies safety risks: jailbreaks that merely yield toxic text in LLMs can trigger unsafe physical actions in embodied systems. Existing defenses alignment, filtering, or prompt hardening intervene too late or at the wrong modality, leaving fused representations exploitable. We introduce a concept-based dictionary learning framework for inference-time safety control. By constructing sparse, interpretable dictionaries from hidden activations, our method identifies harmful concept directions and applies threshold-based interventions to suppress or block unsafe activations. Experiments on Libero-Harm, BadRobot, RoboPair, and IS-Bench show that our approach achieves state-of-the-art defense performance, cutting attack success rates by over 70\% while maintaining task success. Crucially, the framework is plug-in and model-agnostic, requiring no retraining and integrating seamlessly with diverse VLAs. To our knowledge, this is the first inference-time concept-based safety method for embodied systems, advancing both interpretability and safe deployment of VLA models.

摘要（中文）: 视觉语言动作（VLA）模型通过将多模态指令转换为可执行的行为来闭合感知-动作环路，但这种能力也放大了安全风险：仅在LLM中产生有害文本的越狱攻击就能在具身系统中触发不安全的物理动作。现有的防御措施，如对齐、过滤或提示强化，干预时间太晚或模态错误，使融合的表示仍可被利用。我们引入了一种基于概念的字典学习框架，用于推理时安全控制。通过从隐藏层激活中构建稀疏、可解释的字典，我们的方法识别有害的概念方向，并应用基于阈值的干预措施来抑制或阻止不安全的激活。在Libero-Harm、BadRobot、RoboPair和IS-Bench上的实验表明，我们的方法实现了最先进的防御性能，将攻击成功率降低了70%以上，同时保持了任务成功率。 关键是，该框架是即插即用的且与模型无关，无需重新训练，并可与各种VLA无缝集成。据我们所知，这是首个用于具身系统的推理时基于概念的安全方法，提升了VLA模型的可解释性和安全部署。

TLDR: This paper introduces a concept-based dictionary learning framework for inference-time safety control in Vision Language Action models, achieving state-of-the-art defense performance against attacks without requiring retraining.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种基于概念的字典学习框架，用于在视觉语言行动模型中进行推理时安全控制，在不需要重新训练的情况下实现了针对攻击的最先进的防御性能。

Authors: Siqi Wen, Shu Yang, Shaopeng Fu, Jingfeng Zhang, Lijie Hu, Di Wang

DDP-WM: Disentangled Dynamics Prediction for Efficient World Models

Abstract (English): World models are essential for autonomous robotic planning. However, the substantial computational overhead of existing dense Transformerbased models significantly hinders real-time deployment. To address this efficiency-performance bottleneck, we introduce DDP-WM, a novel world model centered on the principle of Disentangled Dynamics Prediction (DDP). We hypothesize that latent state evolution in observed scenes is heterogeneous and can be decomposed into sparse primary dynamics driven by physical interactions and secondary context-driven background updates. DDP-WM realizes this decomposition through an architecture that integrates efficient historical processing with dynamic localization to isolate primary dynamics. By employing a crossattention mechanism for background updates, the framework optimizes resource allocation and provides a smooth optimization landscape for planners. Extensive experiments demonstrate that DDP-WM achieves significant efficiency and performance across diverse tasks, including navigation, precise tabletop manipulation, and complex deformable or multi-body interactions. Specifically, on the challenging Push-T task, DDP-WM achieves an approximately 9 times inference speedup and improves the MPC success rate from 90% to98% compared to state-of-the-art dense models. The results establish a promising path for developing efficient, high-fidelity world models. Codes will be available at https://github.com/HCPLab-SYSU/DDP-WM.

摘要（中文）: 世界模型对于自主机器人规划至关重要。然而，现有基于稠密Transformer模型的巨大计算开销显著阻碍了实时部署。为了解决这种效率与性能的瓶颈，我们提出了一种新颖的世界模型DDP-WM，其核心原则是解耦动力学预测（DDP）。我们假设观测场景中的隐状态演化是异构的，并且可以分解为由物理交互驱动的稀疏主动力学和由上下文驱动的次要背景更新。DDP-WM通过集成高效历史处理和动态定位的架构来实现这种分解，从而隔离主动力学。该框架通过采用交叉注意力机制进行背景更新，优化了资源分配，并为规划器提供了平滑的优化空间。大量实验表明，DDP-WM在各种任务中实现了显著的效率和性能提升，包括导航、精确的桌面操作，以及复杂的形变或多体交互。特别是在具有挑战性的Push-T任务中，与最先进的稠密模型相比，DDP-WM实现了大约9倍的推理速度提升，并将MPC成功率从90%提高到98%。结果表明，这为开发高效、高保真的世界模型提供了一条有希望的途径。代码将在https://github.com/HCPLab-SYSU/DDP-WM上提供。

TLDR: The paper introduces DDP-WM, a novel world model based on disentangled dynamics prediction, which achieves significant efficiency and performance improvements in robotic tasks by decomposing latent state evolution into sparse primary and secondary dynamics.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了DDP-WM，一种基于解耦动态预测的新型世界模型，通过将潜在状态演化分解为稀疏的主要和次要动态，在机器人任务中实现了显著的效率和性能提升。

Authors: Shicheng Yin, Kaixuan Yin, Weixing Chen, Yang Liu, Guanbin Li, Liang Lin

ProcMEM: Learning Reusable Procedural Memory from Experience via Non-Parametric PPO for LLM Agents

Abstract (English): LLM-driven agents demonstrate strong performance in sequential decision-making but often rely on on-the-fly reasoning, re-deriving solutions even in recurring scenarios. This insufficient experience reuse leads to computational redundancy and execution instability. To bridge this gap, we propose ProcMEM, a framework that enables agents to autonomously learn procedural memory from interaction experiences without parameter updates. By formalizing a Skill-MDP, ProcMEM transforms passive episodic narratives into executable Skills defined by activation, execution, and termination conditions to ensure executability. To achieve reliable reusability without capability degradation, we introduce Non-Parametric PPO, which leverages semantic gradients for high-quality candidate generation and a PPO Gate for robust Skill verification. Through score-based maintenance, ProcMEM sustains compact, high-quality procedural memory. Experimental results across in-domain, cross-task, and cross-agent scenarios demonstrate that ProcMEM achieves superior reuse rates and significant performance gains with extreme memory compression. Visualized evolutionary trajectories and Skill distributions further reveal how ProcMEM transparently accumulates, refines, and reuses procedural knowledge to facilitate long-term autonomy.

摘要（中文）: 由LLM驱动的智能体在序贯决策中表现出强大的性能，但通常依赖于即时推理，即使在重复出现的情况下也会重新推导解决方案。这种经验复用不足导致计算冗余和执行不稳定。为了弥合这一差距，我们提出了ProcMEM，一个框架，使智能体能够自主地从交互经验中学习程序性记忆，而无需参数更新。通过形式化Skill-MDP，ProcMEM将被动的片段叙述转化为可执行的技能，这些技能由激活、执行和终止条件定义，以确保可执行性。为了实现可靠的复用性而又不降低能力，我们引入了非参数化PPO，它利用语义梯度生成高质量的候选技能，并使用PPO门进行稳健的技能验证。通过基于分数的维护，ProcMEM保持紧凑且高质量的程序性记忆。在领域内、跨任务和跨智能体场景下的实验结果表明，ProcMEM实现了卓越的复用率，并通过极端的记忆压缩实现了显著的性能提升。可视化的演化轨迹和技能分布进一步揭示了ProcMEM如何透明地积累、提炼和复用程序性知识，从而促进长期自主性。

TLDR: The paper introduces ProcMEM, a framework that enables LLM-driven agents to learn and reuse procedural memory from interaction experiences for improved efficiency and stability in sequential decision-making, using a Non-Parametric PPO approach.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了ProcMEM，一个能使LLM驱动的智能体从交互经验中学习和重用程序性记忆的框架，通过使用非参数PPO方法，提升连续决策过程中的效率和稳定性。

Authors: Qirui Mi, Zhijian Ma, Mengyue Yang, Haoxuan Li, Yisen Wang, Haifeng Zhang, Jun Wang

Generative Visual Code Mobile World Models

Abstract (English): Mobile Graphical User Interface (GUI) World Models (WMs) offer a promising path for improving mobile GUI agent performance at train- and inference-time. However, current approaches face a critical trade-off: text-based WMs sacrifice visual fidelity, while the inability of visual WMs in precise text rendering led to their reliance on slow, complex pipelines dependent on numerous external models. We propose a novel paradigm: visual world modeling via renderable code generation, where a single Vision-Language Model (VLM) predicts the next GUI state as executable web code that renders to pixels, rather than generating pixels directly. This combines the strengths of both approaches: VLMs retain their linguistic priors for precise text rendering while their pre-training on structured web code enables high-fidelity visual generation. We introduce gWorld (8B, 32B), the first open-weight visual mobile GUI WMs built on this paradigm, along with a data generation framework (gWorld) that automatically synthesizes code-based training data. In extensive evaluation across 4 in- and 2 out-of-distribution benchmarks, gWorld sets a new pareto frontier in accuracy versus model size, outperforming 8 frontier open-weight models over 50.25x larger. Further analyses show that (1) scaling training data via gWorld yields meaningful gains, (2) each component of our pipeline improves data quality, and (3) stronger world modeling improves downstream mobile GUI policy performance.

摘要（中文）: 移动图形用户界面（GUI）世界模型（WMs）为提升移动GUI代理在训练和推理时的性能提供了一条有前景的途径。然而，当前的方法面临着一个关键的权衡：基于文本的WMs牺牲了视觉保真度，而视觉WMs在精确文本渲染上的不足导致它们依赖于缓慢、复杂的流水线，并依赖于大量的外部模型。我们提出了一种新的范例：通过可渲染代码生成实现的视觉世界建模，其中单个视觉-语言模型（VLM）将下一个GUI状态预测为可执行的Web代码，该代码能够渲染成像素，而不是直接生成像素。这结合了两种方法的优势：VLMs保留了它们的语言先验知识，从而实现精确的文本渲染，同时它们在结构化Web代码上的预训练实现了高保真的视觉生成。我们推出了gWorld (8B, 32B)，这是首批基于这种范例构建的开源视觉移动GUI WMs， 以及一个自动合成基于代码的训练数据的数据生成框架（gWorld）。在跨4个分布内和2个分布外基准的广泛评估中，gWorld在准确率与模型大小之间设置了一个新的帕累托前沿，超过了8个规模超过其50.25倍的前沿开源模型。进一步的分析表明：（1）通过gWorld扩展训练数据会产生有意义的收益；（2）我们流水线的每个组件都提高了数据质量；（3）更强的世界建模能够提高下游移动GUI策略的性能。

TLDR: This paper introduces gWorld, a novel mobile GUI world model that generates executable web code representations of GUI states using a Vision-Language Model, achieving superior accuracy and size efficiency compared to existing methods.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种名为gWorld的新型移动GUI世界模型，该模型使用视觉-语言模型生成GUI状态的可执行Web代码表示，与现有方法相比，实现了更高的准确性和尺寸效率。

Authors: Woosung Koh, Sungjun Han, Segyu Lee, Se-Young Yun, Jamin Shin

MAIN-VLA: Modeling Abstraction of Intention and eNvironment for Vision-Language-Action Models

Abstract (English): Despite significant progress in Visual-Language-Action (VLA), in highly complex and dynamic environments that involve real-time unpredictable interactions (such as 3D open worlds and large-scale PvP games), existing approaches remain inefficient at extracting action-critical signals from redundant sensor streams. To tackle this, we introduce MAIN-VLA, a framework that explicitly Models the Abstraction of Intention and eNvironment to ground decision-making in deep semantic alignment rather than superficial pattern matching. Specifically, our Intention Abstraction (IA) extracts verbose linguistic instructions and their associated reasoning into compact, explicit semantic primitives, while the Environment Semantics Abstraction (ESA) projects overwhelming visual streams into a structured, topological affordance representation. Furthermore, aligning these two abstract modalities induces an emergent attention-concentration effect, enabling a parameter-free token-pruning strategy that filters out perceptual redundancy without degrading performance. Extensive experiments in open-world Minecraft and large-scale PvP environments (Game for Peace and Valorant) demonstrate that MAIN-VLA sets a new state-of-the-art, which achieves superior decision quality, stronger generalization, and cutting-edge inference efficiency.

摘要（中文）: 尽管在视觉-语言-动作（VLA）领域取得了显著进展，但在涉及实时不可预测交互的高度复杂和动态环境中（例如3D开放世界和大规模玩家对战游戏），现有方法在从冗余传感器流中提取行动关键信号方面仍然效率低下。为了解决这个问题，我们引入了MAIN-VLA，一个显式地对意图和环境的抽象进行建模的框架，它将决策建立在深层语义对齐的基础上，而不是表面的模式匹配。具体而言，我们的意图抽象（IA）将冗长的语言指令及其相关的推理提取成紧凑、显式的语义原语，而环境语义抽象（ESA）将压倒性的视觉流投射成结构化的拓扑可供性表示。此外，对齐这两种抽象模态会产生一种新兴的注意力集中效应，从而实现一种无需参数的令牌裁剪策略，在不降低性能的情况下过滤掉感知冗余。在开放世界Minecraft和大规模玩家对战环境（和平精英和无畏契约）中的大量实验表明，MAIN-VLA创造了一个新的最先进水平，实现了卓越的决策质量、更强的泛化能力和最先进的推理效率。

TLDR: The paper introduces MAIN-VLA, a framework for Vision-Language-Action models that uses intention and environment abstraction to improve decision-making, generalization, and efficiency in complex environments like Minecraft and PvP games.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了MAIN-VLA，一个视觉-语言-动作模型框架，它使用意图和环境抽象来提高在复杂环境（如Minecraft和PvP游戏）中的决策、泛化和效率。

Authors: Zheyuan Zhou, Liang Du, Zixun Sun, Xiaoyu Zhou, Ruimin Ye, Qihao Chen, Yinda Chen, Lemiao Qiu

SoMA: A Real-to-Sim Neural Simulator for Robotic Soft-body Manipulation

Abstract (English): Simulating deformable objects under rich interactions remains a fundamental challenge for real-to-sim robot manipulation, with dynamics jointly driven by environmental effects and robot actions. Existing simulators rely on predefined physics or data-driven dynamics without robot-conditioned control, limiting accuracy, stability, and generalization. This paper presents SoMA, a 3D Gaussian Splat simulator for soft-body manipulation. SoMA couples deformable dynamics, environmental forces, and robot joint actions in a unified latent neural space for end-to-end real-to-sim simulation. Modeling interactions over learned Gaussian splats enables controllable, stable long-horizon manipulation and generalization beyond observed trajectories without predefined physical models. SoMA improves resimulation accuracy and generalization on real-world robot manipulation by 20%, enabling stable simulation of complex tasks such as long-horizon cloth folding.

摘要（中文）: 对富交互下的可变形物体进行模拟仍然是实物转化到模拟机器人操作中的一个基本挑战，其动力学jointly由环境影响和机器人动作驱动。现有的模拟器依赖于预定义的物理规律或数据驱动动力学，而没有机器人条件控制，这限制了准确性、稳定性和泛化能力。本文提出了SoMA，一种用于软体操作的3D高斯溅射模拟器。SoMA在一个统一的潜在神经空间中耦合了可变形动力学、环境力和机器人关节动作，用于端到端的实物到模拟的仿真。在学习到的高斯溅射上建模交互，实现了可控、稳定的长时程操作，以及超出观察到的轨迹的泛化，而无需预定义的物理模型。SoMA将真实机器人操作的重模拟准确性和泛化能力提高了20%，从而能够稳定地模拟复杂的任务，例如长时程的布料折叠。

TLDR: The paper introduces SoMA, a 3D Gaussian Splat simulator that unifies deformable dynamics, environmental forces, and robot joint actions in a latent neural space for real-to-sim robot manipulation, enhancing accuracy, stability, and generalization.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了SoMA，一个3D高斯溅射模拟器，它在潜在神经空间中统一了可变形动力学，环境力和机器人关节动作，用于真实到模拟的机器人操作，从而提高了准确性，稳定性和泛化能力。

Authors: Mu Huang, Hui Wang, Kerui Ren, Linning Xu, Yunsong Zhou, Mulin Yu, Bo Dai, Jiangmiao Pang

PRISM: Performer RS-IMLE for Single-pass Multisensory Imitation Learning

Abstract (English): Robotic imitation learning typically requires models that capture multimodal action distributions while operating at real-time control rates and accommodating multiple sensing modalities. Although recent generative approaches such as diffusion models, flow matching, and Implicit Maximum Likelihood Estimation (IMLE) have achieved promising results, they often satisfy only a subset of these requirements. To address this, we introduce PRISM, a single-pass policy based on a batch-global rejection-sampling variant of IMLE. PRISM couples a temporal multisensory encoder (integrating RGB, depth, tactile, audio, and proprioception) with a linear-attention generator using a Performer architecture. We demonstrate the efficacy of PRISM on a diverse real-world hardware suite, including loco-manipulation using a Unitree Go2 with a 7-DoF arm D1 and tabletop manipulation with a UR5 manipulator. Across challenging physical tasks such as pre-manipulation parking, high-precision insertion, and multi-object pick-and-place, PRISM outperforms state-of-the-art diffusion policies by 10-25% in success rate while maintaining high-frequency (30-50 Hz) closed-loop control. We further validate our approach on large-scale simulation benchmarks, including CALVIN, MetaWorld, and Robomimic. In CALVIN (10% data split), PRISM improves success rates by approximately 25% over diffusion and approximately 20% over flow matching, while simultaneously reducing trajectory jerk by 20x-50x. These results position PRISM as a fast, accurate, and multisensory imitation policy that retains multimodal action coverage without the latency of iterative sampling.

摘要（中文）: 机器人模仿学习通常需要能够捕捉多模态动作分布的模型，同时能够以实时控制速率运行并适应多种传感模式。虽然诸如扩散模型、流匹配和隐式极大似然估计 (IMLE) 等近期生成方法已经取得了可喜的成果，但它们往往只能满足其中一部分需求。为了解决这个问题，我们引入 PRISM，这是一种基于 IMLE 的批量全局拒绝采样变体的单次策略。PRISM 将时间多感官编码器（整合 RGB、深度、触觉、音频和本体感觉）与使用 Performer 架构的线性注意力生成器相结合。我们在一套多样化的真实世界硬件套件上验证了 PRISM 的有效性，包括使用配备 7 自由度 D1 机械臂的宇树 Go2 进行的移动操作，以及使用 UR5 机械臂进行的桌面操作。在诸如预操作停车、高精度插入和多物体抓取放置等具有挑战性的物理任务中，PRISM 的成功率比最先进的扩散策略高出 10-25%，同时保持了高频（30-50 Hz）闭环控制。我们进一步在大规模模拟基准测试中验证了我们的方法，包括 CALVIN、MetaWorld 和 Robomimic。在 CALVIN（10% 数据分割）中，PRISM 比扩散模型将成功率提高了约 25%，比流匹配提高了约 20%，同时将轨迹抖动降低了 20-50 倍。这些结果表明 PRISM 是一种快速、准确和多感官的模仿策略，它保留了多模态动作覆盖率，而没有迭代采样的延迟。

TLDR: The paper introduces PRISM, a single-pass imitation learning policy based on a batch-global rejection-sampling variant of IMLE, which outperforms state-of-the-art diffusion policies in real-world robotic tasks while maintaining high-frequency control and demonstrating strong performance on large-scale simulation benchmarks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了PRISM，一种基于IMLE的批量全局拒绝采样变体的单程模仿学习策略。PRISM在实际机器人任务中表现优于最先进的扩散策略，同时保持高频控制，并在大规模模拟基准测试中表现出强大的性能。

Authors: Amisha Bhaskar, Pratap Tokekar, Stefano Di Cairano, Alexander Schperberg

TTT-Parkour: Rapid Test-Time Training for Perceptive Robot Parkour

Abstract (English): Achieving highly dynamic humanoid parkour on unseen, complex terrains remains a challenge in robotics. Although general locomotion policies demonstrate capabilities across broad terrain distributions, they often struggle with arbitrary and highly challenging environments. To overcome this limitation, we propose a real-to-sim-to-real framework that leverages rapid test-time training (TTT) on novel terrains, significantly enhancing the robot's capability to traverse extremely difficult geometries. We adopt a two-stage end-to-end learning paradigm: a policy is first pre-trained on diverse procedurally generated terrains, followed by rapid fine-tuning on high-fidelity meshes reconstructed from real-world captures. Specifically, we develop a feed-forward, efficient, and high-fidelity geometry reconstruction pipeline using RGB-D inputs, ensuring both speed and quality during test-time training. We demonstrate that TTT-Parkour empowers humanoid robots to master complex obstacles, including wedges, stakes, boxes, trapezoids, and narrow beams. The whole pipeline of capturing, reconstructing, and test-time training requires less than 10 minutes on most tested terrains. Extensive experiments show that the policy after test-time training exhibits robust zero-shot sim-to-real transfer capability.

摘要（中文）: 在未见过的复杂地形上实现高度动态的类人机器人跑酷仍然是机器人领域的一项挑战。尽管通用运动策略在广泛的地形分布中展现了能力，但它们通常难以应对任意且极具挑战性的环境。为了克服这一局限，我们提出了一种真机到仿真到真机(Real-to-Sim-to-Real)的框架，该框架利用在新地形上的快速测试时训练(TTT)，显著增强了机器人穿越极端困难几何体的能力。我们采用了一种两阶段的端到端学习范式：首先在各种程序化生成的地形上预训练一个策略，然后在从真实世界捕获重建的高保真网格上进行快速微调。具体来说，我们开发了一个使用RGB-D输入的、前馈、高效且高保真度的几何重建管道，确保了测试时训练期间的速度和质量。我们证明TTT-Parkour能够使类人机器人掌握复杂的障碍物，包括楔形物、尖桩、箱子、梯形物和窄梁。在大多数测试地形上，捕获、重建和测试时训练的整个流程需要不到10分钟。大量实验表明，经过测试时训练的策略表现出强大的零样本仿真到真机迁移能力。

TLDR: This paper presents TTT-Parkour, a framework for rapidly fine-tuning humanoid robot locomotion policies on real-world terrains using RGB-D input and test-time training, enabling robust parkour on complex geometries.

简要说明: 这篇论文提出了TTT-Parkour，一个使用RGB-D输入和测试时训练来快速微调人形机器人运动策略的框架，使其能够在复杂地形上进行稳健的跑酷运动。

Authors: Shaoting Zhu, Baijun Ye, Jiaxuan Wang, Jiakang Chen, Ziwen Zhuang, Linzhan Mou, Runhan Huang, Hang Zhao

Online Fine-Tuning of Pretrained Controllers for Autonomous Driving via Real-Time Recurrent RL

Abstract (English): Deploying pretrained policies in real-world applications presents substantial challenges that fundamentally limit the practical applicability of learning-based control systems. When autonomous systems encounter environmental changes in system dynamics, sensor drift, or task objectives, fixed policies rapidly degrade in performance. We show that employing Real-Time Recurrent Reinforcement Learning (RTRRL), a biologically plausible algorithm for online adaptation, can effectively fine-tune a pretrained policy to improve autonomous agents' performance on driving tasks. We further show that RTRRL synergizes with a recent biologically inspired recurrent network model, the Liquid-Resistance Liquid-Capacitance RNN. We demonstrate the effectiveness of this closed-loop approach in a simulated CarRacing environment and in a real-world line-following task with a RoboRacer car equipped with an event camera.

摘要（中文）: 将预训练策略部署到实际应用中面临着巨大的挑战，这从根本上限制了基于学习的控制系统的实际应用性。当自主系统遇到系统动力学、传感器漂移或任务目标方面的环境变化时，固定策略的性能会迅速下降。我们证明，采用实时递归强化学习（RTRRL），一种生物可信的在线自适应算法，能够有效地微调预训练策略，从而提高自动驾驶智能体在驾驶任务中的性能。我们进一步表明，RTRRL与最近一种受生物启发的回顾型网络模型，即液态电阻-液态电容循环神经网络，具有协同效应。我们分别在模拟的CarRacing环境以及配备事件相机的RoboRacer汽车的真实世界循线任务中，展示了这种闭环方法的有效性。

TLDR: The paper presents a method for online fine-tuning of pretrained control policies for autonomous driving using Real-Time Recurrent Reinforcement Learning (RTRRL) and demonstrates its effectiveness in simulated and real-world environments.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种使用实时循环强化学习（RTRRL）在线微调自动驾驶预训练控制策略的方法，并在模拟和真实环境中证明了其有效性。

Authors: Julian Lemmel, Felix Resch, Mónika Farsang, Ramin Hasani, Daniela Rus, Radu Grosu

FD-VLA: Force-Distilled Vision-Language-Action Model for Contact-Rich Manipulation

Abstract (English): Force sensing is a crucial modality for Vision-Language-Action (VLA) frameworks, as it enables fine-grained perception and dexterous manipulation in contact-rich tasks. We present Force-Distilled VLA (FD-VLA), a novel framework that integrates force awareness into contact-rich manipulation without relying on physical force sensors. The core of our approach is a Force Distillation Module (FDM), which distills force by mapping a learnable query token, conditioned on visual observations and robot states, into a predicted force token aligned with the latent representation of actual force signals. During inference, this distilled force token is injected into the pretrained VLM, enabling force-aware reasoning while preserving the integrity of its vision-language semantics. This design provides two key benefits: first, it allows practical deployment across a wide range of robots that lack expensive or fragile force-torque sensors, thereby reducing hardware cost and complexity; second, the FDM introduces an additional force-vision-state fusion prior to the VLM, which improves cross-modal alignment and enhances perception-action robustness in contact-rich scenarios. Surprisingly, our physical experiments show that the distilled force token outperforms direct sensor force measurements as well as other baselines, which highlights the effectiveness of this force-distilled VLA approach.

摘要（中文）: 力感应是视觉-语言-动作（VLA）框架的关键模态，因为它能够在接触丰富的任务中实现精细感知和灵巧操作。我们提出了力蒸馏VLA（FD-VLA），这是一种新颖的框架，它将力感知集成到接触丰富操作中，而无需依赖物理力传感器。我们方法的核心是力蒸馏模块（FDM），它通过将可学习的查询令牌（以视觉观察和机器人状态为条件）映射到与实际力信号的潜在表示对齐的预测力令牌来蒸馏力。在推理过程中，这个蒸馏后的力令牌被注入到预训练的VLM中，从而在保留其视觉-语言语义完整性的同时，实现力感知推理。这种设计提供了两个关键好处：首先，它允许在缺乏昂贵或脆弱的力-扭矩传感器的各种机器人上进行实际部署，从而降低硬件成本和复杂性；其次，FDM在VLM之前引入了额外的力-视觉-状态融合先验，这改善了跨模态对齐，并增强了接触丰富场景中的感知-动作鲁棒性。令人惊讶的是，我们的物理实验表明，蒸馏后的力令牌优于直接传感器力测量以及其他基线，这突出了这种力蒸馏VLA方法的有效性。

TLDR: The paper introduces FD-VLA, a novel Vision-Language-Action framework that distills force information from visual observations and robot states to enable force-aware reasoning in contact-rich manipulation tasks, even without physical force sensors.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了FD-VLA，一种新颖的视觉-语言-动作框架，它从视觉观察和机器人状态中提取力信息，从而在接触丰富的操作任务中实现力感知推理，即使没有物理力传感器。

Authors: Ruiteng Zhao, Wenshuo Wang, Yicheng Ma, Xiaocong Li, Francis E. H. Tay, Marcelo H. Ang, Haiyue Zhu

Bandwidth-Efficient Multi-Agent Communication through Information Bottleneck and Vector Quantization

Abstract (English): Multi-agent reinforcement learning systems deployed in real-world robotics applications face severe communication constraints that significantly impact coordination effectiveness. We present a framework that combines information bottleneck theory with vector quantization to enable selective, bandwidth-efficient communication in multi-agent environments. Our approach learns to compress and discretize communication messages while preserving task-critical information through principled information-theoretic optimization. We introduce a gated communication mechanism that dynamically determines when communication is necessary based on environmental context and agent states. Experimental evaluation on challenging coordination tasks demonstrates that our method achieves 181.8% performance improvement over no-communication baselines while reducing bandwidth usage by 41.4%. Comprehensive Pareto frontier analysis shows dominance across the entire success-bandwidth spectrum with area-under-curve of 0.198 vs 0.142 for next-best methods. Our approach significantly outperforms existing communication strategies and establishes a theoretically grounded framework for deploying multi-agent systems in bandwidth-constrained environments such as robotic swarms, autonomous vehicle fleets, and distributed sensor networks.

摘要（中文）: 在现实世界机器人应用中部署的多智能体强化学习系统面临着严峻的通信约束，这会显著影响协同效率。我们提出了一种框架，该框架结合了信息瓶颈理论和向量量化，以在多智能体环境中实现选择性的、带宽高效的通信。我们的方法通过有原则的信息论优化，学习压缩和离散化通信消息，同时保留任务关键信息。我们引入了一种门控通信机制，可以根据环境上下文和智能体状态动态地确定何时需要通信。在具有挑战性的协同任务上的实验评估表明，我们的方法在不通信的基线基础上实现了 181.8% 的性能提升，同时减少了 41.4% 的带宽使用。全面的帕累托前沿分析表明，在整个成功率-带宽范围内都具有优势，曲线下面积为 0.198，而次优方法为 0.142。我们的方法显著优于现有的通信策略，并为在带宽受限的环境（例如机器人集群、自动驾驶车队和分布式传感器网络）中部署多智能体系统建立了一个理论基础坚实的框架。

TLDR: This paper presents a method for bandwidth-efficient multi-agent communication using information bottleneck and vector quantization, demonstrating improved performance and reduced bandwidth usage in challenging coordination tasks.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种利用信息瓶颈和矢量量化的带宽高效多智能体通信方法，在具有挑战性的协调任务中表现出更高的性能和更低的带宽使用率。

Authors: Ahmad Farooq, Kamran Iqbal

LIEREx: Language-Image Embeddings for Robotic Exploration

Abstract (English): Semantic maps allow a robot to reason about its surroundings to fulfill tasks such as navigating known environments, finding specific objects, and exploring unmapped areas. Traditional mapping approaches provide accurate geometric representations but are often constrained by pre-designed symbolic vocabularies. The reliance on fixed object classes makes it impractical to handle out-of-distribution knowledge not defined at design time. Recent advances in Vision-Language Foundation Models, such as CLIP, enable open-set mapping, where objects are encoded as high-dimensional embeddings rather than fixed labels. In LIEREx, we integrate these VLFMs with established 3D Semantic Scene Graphs to enable target-directed exploration by an autonomous agent in partially unknown environments.

摘要（中文）: 语义地图允许机器人推理其周围环境，以完成诸如导航已知环境、寻找特定物体以及探索未绘制区域等任务。传统的地图构建方法提供精确的几何表示，但通常受限于预先设计的符号词汇表。对固定物体类别的依赖使其难以处理设计时未定义的分布外知识。诸如CLIP等视觉-语言基础模型（VLFMs）的最新进展，实现了开放集映射，其中物体被编码为高维嵌入，而非固定标签。在LIEREx中，我们将这些VLFMs与已建立的3D语义场景图集成，从而能够使自主体在部分未知环境中进行目标导向的探索。

TLDR: LIEREx integrates Vision-Language Foundation Models (VLFMs) with 3D Semantic Scene Graphs for target-directed robotic exploration in partially unknown environments, enabling open-set mapping compared to traditional fixed-vocabulary methods.

简要说明: LIEREx集成了视觉-语言基础模型(VLFMs)与3D语义场景图，用于在部分未知的环境中进行目标导向的机器人探索。相比传统的固定词汇方法，能够实现开放集映射。

Multimodal Large Language Models for Real-Time Situated Reasoning

Abstract (English): In this work, we explore how multimodal large language models can support real-time context- and value-aware decision-making. To do so, we combine the GPT-4o language model with a TurtleBot 4 platform simulating a smart vacuum cleaning robot in a home. The model evaluates the environment through vision input and determines whether it is appropriate to initiate cleaning. The system highlights the ability of these models to reason about domestic activities, social norms, and user preferences and take nuanced decisions aligned with the values of the people involved, such as cleanliness, comfort, and safety. 摘要（中文）: 在这项工作中，我们探索了多模态大语言模型如何支持实时、上下文感知和价值取向的决策。为此，我们将 GPT-4o 语言模型与 TurtleBot 4 平台相结合，模拟家庭中的智能真空吸尘机器人。该模型通过视觉输入评估环境，并判断是否适合启动清洁。该系统突显了这些模型在推理家庭活动、社会规范和用户偏好方面的能力，并能做出与相关人员的价值观（如清洁、舒适和安全）相符的细致决策。我们在真实的家庭环境中演示了该系统，展示了其从有限的视觉输入中推断上下文和价值观的能力。我们的结果表明，多模态大语言模型在提升机器人自主性和情境感知方面具有前景，同时也强调了与一致性、偏见和实时性能相关的挑战。

Authors: Giulio Antonio Abbo, Senne Lenaerts, Tony Belpaeme

BTGenBot-2: Efficient Behavior Tree Generation with Small Language Models

Abstract (English): Recent advances in robot learning increasingly rely on LLM-based task planning, leveraging their ability to bridge natural language with executable actions. While prior works showcased great performances, the widespread adoption of these models in robotics has been challenging as 1) existing methods are often closed-source or computationally intensive, neglecting the actual deployment on real-world physical systems, and 2) there is no universally accepted, plug-and-play representation for robotic task generation. Addressing these challenges, we propose BTGenBot-2, a 1B-parameter open-source small language model that directly converts natural language task descriptions and a list of robot action primitives into executable behavior trees in XML. Unlike prior approaches, BTGenBot-2 enables zero-shot BT generation, error recovery at inference and runtime, while remaining lightweight enough for resource-constrained robots. We further introduce the first standardized benchmark for LLM-based BT generation, covering 52 navigation and manipulation tasks in NVIDIA Isaac Sim. Extensive evaluations demonstrate that BTGenBot-2 consistently outperforms GPT-5, Claude Opus 4.1, and larger open-source models across both functional and non-functional metrics, achieving average success rates of 90.38% in zero-shot and 98.07% in one-shot, while delivering up to 16x faster inference compared to the previous BTGenBot.

摘要（中文）: 机器人学习的最新进展越来越依赖于基于大型语言模型（LLM）的任务规划，利用它们的能力将自然语言与可执行动作联系起来。虽然先前的工作展现了出色的性能，但这些模型在机器人领域的广泛应用一直具有挑战性，因为1）现有方法通常是闭源的或计算密集型的，忽略了在真实物理系统上的实际部署，并且2）对于机器人任务生成，没有普遍接受的、即插即用的表示形式。为了解决这些挑战，我们提出了BTGenBot-2，一个拥有10亿参数的开源小型语言模型，它可以直接将自然语言任务描述和机器人动作原语列表转换为XML格式的可执行行为树。与先前的方法不同，BTGenBot-2能够实现零样本行为树生成，在推理和运行时进行错误恢复，同时保持足够轻量，可用于资源受限的机器人。我们进一步推出了首个基于LLM的行为树生成标准化基准，涵盖了NVIDIA Isaac Sim中的52个导航和操作任务。广泛的评估表明，BTGenBot-2在功能性和非功能性指标上均始终优于GPT-5、Claude Opus 4.1和更大的开源模型，在零样本情况下的平均成功率为90.38%，在单样本情况下的平均成功率为98.07%，并且与之前的BTGenBot相比，推理速度提高了高达16倍。

TLDR: The paper introduces BTGenBot-2, a lightweight, open-source small language model for generating executable behavior trees from natural language for robot task planning, outperforming larger models and establishing a new benchmark.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了BTGenBot-2，一个轻量级的开源小型语言模型，用于从自然语言生成可执行的行为树，用于机器人任务规划，性能优于更大的模型，并建立了一个新的基准。

Authors: Riccardo Andrea Izzo, Gianluca Bardaro, Matteo Matteucci

From Knowing to Doing Precisely: A General Self-Correction and Termination Framework for VLA models

Abstract (English): While vision-language-action (VLA) models for embodied agents integrate perception, reasoning, and control, they remain constrained by two critical weaknesses: first, during grasping tasks, the action tokens generated by the language model often exhibit subtle spatial deviations from the target object, resulting in grasp failures; second, they lack the ability to reliably recognize task completion, which leads to redundant actions and frequent timeout errors. To address these challenges and enhance robustness, we propose a lightweight, training-free framework, VLA-SCT. This framework operates as a self-correcting control loop, combining data-driven action refinement with conditional logic for termination. Consequently, compared to baseline approaches, our method achieves consistent improvements across all datasets in the LIBERO benchmark, significantly increasing the success rate of fine manipulation tasks and ensuring accurate task completion, thereby promoting the deployment of more reliable VLA agents in complex, unstructured environments.

摘要（中文）: 面向具身智能体的视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型集成了感知、推理和控制功能，但仍然受到两个关键弱点的制约：首先，在抓取任务中，语言模型生成的动作令牌常常表现出与目标物体存在细微的空间偏差，导致抓取失败；其次，它们缺乏可靠识别任务完成的能力，导致冗余动作和频繁的超时错误。为了应对这些挑战并提高鲁棒性，我们提出了一种轻量级的、无需训练的框架VLA-SCT。该框架作为一个自校正控制循环运行，将数据驱动的动作优化与用于终止的条件逻辑相结合。因此，与基线方法相比，我们的方法在LIBERO基准测试的所有数据集中都获得了持续的改进，显著提高了精细操作任务的成功率，并确保了准确的任务完成，从而促进了更可靠的VLA智能体在复杂、非结构化环境中的部署。

Authors: Wentao Zhang, Aolan Sun, Wentao Mo, Xiaoyang Qu, Yuxin Zheng, Jianzong Wang

RFS: Reinforcement learning with Residual flow steering for dexterous manipulation

Abstract (English): Imitation learning has emerged as an effective approach for bootstrapping sequential decision-making in robotics, achieving strong performance even in high-dimensional dexterous manipulation tasks. Recent behavior cloning methods further leverage expressive generative models, such as diffusion models and flow matching, to represent multimodal action distributions. However, policies pretrained in this manner often exhibit limited generalization and require additional fine-tuning to achieve robust performance at deployment time. Such adaptation must preserve the global exploration benefits of pretraining while enabling rapid correction of local execution errors. We propose Residual Flow Steering(RFS), a data-efficient reinforcement learning framework for adapting pretrained generative policies. RFS steers a pretrained flow-matching policy by jointly optimizing a residual action and a latent noise distribution, enabling complementary forms of exploration: local refinement through residual corrections and global exploration through latent-space modulation. This design allows efficient adaptation while retaining the expressive structure of the pretrained policy. We demonstrate the effectiveness of RFS on dexterous manipulation tasks, showing efficient fine-tuning in both simulation and real-world settings when adapting pretrained base policies. Project website:https://weirdlabuw.github.io/rfs.

摘要（中文）: 模仿学习已成为在机器人技术中引导序列决策的有效方法，即使在高维灵巧操作任务中也能实现强大的性能。最近的行为克隆方法进一步利用具有表现力的生成模型，如扩散模型和流匹配，来表示多模态动作分布。然而，以这种方式预训练的策略通常表现出有限的泛化能力，并且需要额外的微调，才能在部署时实现稳健的性能。这种适应必须保留预训练的全局探索优势，同时能够快速纠正局部执行错误。我们提出残差流引导（RFS），一种用于调整预训练生成策略的数据高效强化学习框架。RFS通过联合优化残差动作和潜在噪声分布来引导预训练的流匹配策略，从而实现互补形式的探索：通过残差校正进行局部细化，以及通过潜在空间调制进行全局探索。这种设计可以在保留预训练策略的表达结构的同时，实现高效的适应。我们在灵巧操作任务上证明了RFS的有效性，展示了当调整预训练的基础策略时，在模拟和真实世界环境中均能实现高效的微调。项目网站：https://weirdlabuw.github.io/rfs。

TLDR: The paper introduces Residual Flow Steering (RFS), a reinforcement learning framework that efficiently fine-tunes pretrained flow-matching policies for dexterous manipulation by jointly optimizing a residual action and a latent noise distribution, demonstrating strong performance in simulation and real-world settings.

Authors: Entong Su, Tyler Westenbroek, Anusha Nagabandi, Abhishek Gupta

Uncertainty-Aware Non-Prehensile Manipulation with Mobile Manipulators under Object-Induced Occlusion

Abstract (English): Non-prehensile manipulation using onboard sensing presents a fundamental challenge: the manipulated object occludes the sensor's field of view, creating occluded regions that can lead to collisions. We propose CURA-PPO, a reinforcement learning framework that addresses this challenge by explicitly modeling uncertainty under partial observability. By predicting collision possibility as a distribution, we extract both risk and uncertainty to guide the robot's actions. The uncertainty term encourages active perception, enabling simultaneous manipulation and information gathering to resolve occlusions. When combined with confidence maps that capture observation reliability, our approach enables safe navigation despite severe sensor occlusion. Extensive experiments across varying object sizes and obstacle configurations demonstrate that CURA-PPO achieves up to 3X higher success rates than the baselines, with learned behaviors that handle occlusions. Our method provides a practical solution for autonomous manipulation in cluttered environments using only onboard sensing.

摘要（中文）: 利用机载传感的非抓取式操作面临一个根本性挑战：被操作物体会遮挡传感器的视野，造成遮挡区域，从而可能导致碰撞。我们提出 CURA-PPO，一个强化学习框架，通过显式地对部分可观测性下的不确定性进行建模来解决这一挑战。通过将碰撞可能性预测为一个分布，我们提取风险和不确定性来引导机器人的动作。不确定性项鼓励主动感知，从而能够同时进行操作和信息收集以消除遮挡。当与捕捉观测可靠性的置信度图相结合时，我们的方法能够在严重的传感器遮挡下实现安全导航。在不同物体尺寸和障碍物配置下进行的大量实验表明，CURA-PPO 比基线方法实现了高达 3 倍的成功率，并学习到了能够处理遮挡的行为。我们的方法仅使用机载传感，为在杂乱环境中进行自主操作提供了一个实用的解决方案。

TLDR: The paper introduces CURA-PPO, a reinforcement learning framework that improves non-prehensile manipulation under object-induced occlusion by explicitly modeling uncertainty and risk in observations to enable active perception and safe navigation, achieving up to 3X higher success rates.

Authors: Jiwoo Hwang, Taegeun Yang, Jeil Jeong, Minsung Yoon, Sung-Eui Yoon

GSR: Learning Structured Reasoning for Embodied Manipulation

Abstract (English): Despite rapid progress, embodied agents still struggle with long-horizon manipulation that requires maintaining spatial consistency, causal dependencies, and goal constraints. A key limitation of existing approaches is that task reasoning is implicitly embedded in high-dimensional latent representations, making it challenging to separate task structure from perceptual variability. We introduce Grounded Scene-graph Reasoning (GSR), a structured reasoning paradigm that explicitly models world-state evolution as transitions over semantically grounded scene graphs. By reasoning step-wise over object states and spatial relations, rather than directly mapping perception to actions, GSR enables explicit reasoning about action preconditions, consequences, and goal satisfaction in a physically grounded space. To support learning such reasoning, we construct Manip-Cognition-1.6M, a large-scale dataset that jointly supervises world understanding, action planning, and goal interpretation. Extensive evaluations across RLBench, LIBERO, GSR-benchmark, and real-world robotic tasks show that GSR significantly improves zero-shot generalization and long-horizon task completion over prompting-based baselines. These results highlight explicit world-state representations as a key inductive bias for scalable embodied reasoning.

摘要（中文）: 尽管进展迅速，具身智能体仍然难以应对需要维持空间一致性、因果依赖性和目标约束的远距离操作任务。现有方法的一个关键限制在于，任务推理隐式地嵌入在高维潜在表示中，使得分离任务结构与感知变异性变得具有挑战性。 我们引入了基于场景图的推理（Grounded Scene-graph Reasoning，GSR），这是一种结构化的推理范式，它将世界状态演化显式地建模为在语义接地的场景图上的转换。 通过逐步推理对象状态和空间关系，而不是直接将感知映射到动作，GSR 能够在物理接地的空间中显式地推理动作先决条件、后果和目标满足情况。 为了支持这种推理的学习，我们构建了 Manip-Cognition-1.6M，这是一个大规模数据集，联合监督世界理解、动作规划和目标解释。 在 RLBench、LIBERO、GSR-benchmark 和真实世界机器人任务中的广泛评估表明，与基于提示的基线相比，GSR 显著提高了零样本泛化能力和远距离任务完成率。 这些结果强调了显式的世界状态表示是可扩展具身推理的关键归纳偏置。

TLDR: The paper introduces Grounded Scene-graph Reasoning (GSR), a structured reasoning paradigm for embodied manipulation that explicitly models world-state evolution, leading to improved zero-shot generalization and long-horizon task completion. They also introduce a large-scale dataset, Manip-Cognition-1.6M.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了Grounded Scene-graph Reasoning (GSR)，一种用于具身操作的结构化推理范式，它显式地建模世界状态的演变，从而提高了零样本泛化和长周期任务完成度。他们还介绍了大型数据集Manip-Cognition-1.6M。

Authors: Kewei Hu, Michael Zhang, Wei Ying, Tianhao Liu, Guoqiang Hao, Zimeng Li, Wanchan Yu, Jiajian Jing, Fangwen Chen, Hanwen Kang

AgenticLab: A Real-World Robot Agent Platform that Can See, Think, and Act

Abstract (English): Recent advances in large vision-language models (VLMs) have demonstrated generalizable open-vocabulary perception and reasoning, yet their real-robot manipulation capability remains unclear for long-horizon, closed-loop execution in unstructured, in-the-wild environments. Prior VLM-based manipulation pipelines are difficult to compare across different research groups' setups, and many evaluations rely on simulation, privileged state, or specially designed setups. We present AgenticLab, a model-agnostic robot agent platform and benchmark for open-world manipulation. AgenticLab provides a closed-loop agent pipeline for perception, task decomposition, online verification, and replanning. Using AgenticLab, we benchmark state-of-the-art VLM-based agents on real-robot tasks in unstructured environments. Our benchmark reveals several failure modes that offline vision-language tests (e.g., VQA and static image understanding) fail to capture, including breakdowns in multi-step grounding consistency, object grounding under occlusion and scene changes, and insufficient spatial reasoning for reliable manipulation. We will release the full hardware and software stack to support reproducible evaluation and accelerate research on general-purpose robot agents.

摘要（中文）: 大型视觉-语言模型（VLM）的最新进展已经展示了其具有泛化性的开放词汇感知和推理能力，但它们在非结构化、真实环境中进行长时程、闭环执行的真实机器人操作能力仍然不明确。先前的基于VLM的操作流程难以在不同研究团队的设置之间进行比较，并且许多评估依赖于仿真、特权状态或特殊设计的设置。我们提出了AgenticLab，一个模型无关的机器人代理平台和开放世界操作基准。AgenticLab提供了一个闭环代理流程，用于感知、任务分解、在线验证和重新规划。利用AgenticLab，我们在非结构化环境中的真实机器人任务上对最先进的基于VLM的代理进行基准测试。我们的基准测试揭示了离线视觉-语言测试（例如，视觉问答和静态图像理解）无法捕捉到的几种失效模式，包括多步基础一致性的崩溃、遮挡和场景变化下的物体基础失败，以及用于可靠操作的不足空间推理。我们将发布完整的硬件和软件堆栈，以支持可复现的评估并加速通用机器人代理的研究。

TLDR: The paper introduces AgenticLab, a real-world robot agent platform and benchmark for evaluating VLM-based agents in unstructured environments, highlighting failure modes not captured by offline VLM evaluations.

Authors: Pengyuan Guo, Zhonghao Mai, Zhengtong Xu, Kaidi Zhang, Heng Zhang, Zichen Miao, Arash Ajoudani, Zachary Kingston, Qiang Qiu, Yu She

From Perception to Action: Spatial AI Agents and World Models

Abstract (English): While large language models have become the prevailing approach for agentic reasoning and planning, their success in symbolic domains does not readily translate to the physical world. Spatial intelligence, the ability to perceive 3D structure, reason about object relationships, and act under physical constraints, is an orthogonal capability that proves important for embodied agents. Existing surveys address either agentic architectures or spatial domains in isolation. None provide a unified framework connecting these complementary capabilities. This paper bridges that gap. Through a thorough review of over 2,000 papers, citing 742 works from top-tier venues, we introduce a unified three-axis taxonomy connecting agentic capabilities with spatial tasks across scales. Crucially, we distinguish spatial grounding (metric understanding of geometry and physics) from symbolic grounding (associating images with text), arguing that perception alone does not confer agency. Our analysis reveals three key findings mapped to these axes: (1) hierarchical memory systems (Capability axis) are important for long-horizon spatial tasks. (2) GNN-LLM integration (Task axis) is a promising approach for structured spatial reasoning. (3) World models (Scale axis) are essential for safe deployment across micro-to-macro spatial scales. We conclude by identifying six grand challenges and outlining directions for future research, including the need for unified evaluation frameworks to standardize cross-domain assessment. This taxonomy provides a foundation for unifying fragmented research efforts and enabling the next generation of spatially-aware autonomous systems in robotics, autonomous vehicles, and geospatial intelligence.

摘要（中文）: 大型语言模型已成为智能体推理和规划的主流方法，但它们在符号领域取得的成功难以直接转化到物理世界。空间智能，即感知三维结构、推理对象关系并在物理约束下行动的能力，是一种正交能力，对于具身智能体至关重要。现有的综述要么孤立地探讨智能体架构，要么孤立地探讨空间领域，没有提供连接这些互补能力的统一框架。本文弥补了这一差距。通过对2000多篇论文的全面回顾，并引用顶级场所发表的742篇文献，我们提出了一个统一的三轴分类法，将智能体能力与不同尺度的空间任务联系起来。关键在于，我们将空间接地（对几何和物理的度量理解）与符号接地（将图像与文本相关联）区分开来，认为仅靠感知并不能赋予智能体行为能力。我们的分析揭示了映射到这些轴的三个关键发现：（1）分层记忆系统（能力轴）对于长时程空间任务至关重要。（2）GNN-LLM集成（任务轴）是结构化空间推理的一种有前景的方法。（3）世界模型（尺度轴）对于微观到宏观空间尺度上的安全部署至关重要。最后，我们确定了六大挑战，并概述了未来的研究方向，包括需要统一的评估框架来标准化跨领域评估。该分类法为统一分散的研究工作奠定了基础，并将在机器人、自动驾驶车辆和地理空间情报领域实现下一代具有空间感知能力的自主系统。

TLDR: This paper presents a unified taxonomy for Spatial AI agents, linking agentic capabilities with spatial tasks across different scales, and identifies key challenges and future research directions, especially focusing on the distinction between spatial grounding and symbolic grounding.

简要说明: 本文提出了空间人工智能代理的统一分类法，将代理能力与跨不同尺度的空间任务联系起来，并确定了关键挑战和未来研究方向，特别关注空间基准与符号基准之间的区别。

Authors: Gloria Felicia, Nolan Bryant, Handi Putra, Ayaan Gazali, Eliel Lobo, Esteban Rojas

A Closed-Form Geometric Retargeting Solver for Upper Body Humanoid Robot Teleoperation

Abstract (English): Retargeting human motion to robot poses is a practical approach for teleoperating bimanual humanoid robot arms, but existing methods can be suboptimal and slow, often causing undesirable motion or latency. This is due to optimizing to match robot end-effector to human hand position and orientation, which can also limit the robot's workspace to that of the human. Instead, this paper reframes retargeting as an orientation alignment problem, enabling a closed-form, geometric solution algorithm with an optimality guarantee. The key idea is to align a robot arm to a human's upper and lower arm orientations, as identified from shoulder, elbow, and wrist (SEW) keypoints; hence, the method is called SEW-Mimic. The method has fast inference (3 kHz) on standard commercial CPUs, leaving computational overhead for downstream applications; an example in this paper is a safety filter to avoid bimanual self-collision. The method suits most 7-degree-of-freedom robot arms and humanoids, and is agnostic to input keypoint source. Experiments show that SEW-Mimic outperforms other retargeting methods in computation time and accuracy. A pilot user study suggests that the method improves teleoperation task success. Preliminary analysis indicates that data collected with SEW-Mimic improves policy learning due to being smoother. SEW-Mimic is also shown to be a drop-in way to accelerate full-body humanoid retargeting. Finally, hardware demonstrations illustrate SEW-Mimic's practicality. The results emphasize the utility of SEW-Mimic as a fundamental building block for bimanual robot manipulation and humanoid robot teleoperation.

摘要（中文）: 将人类运动重定向到机器人姿态是遥操作双臂类人机器人的实用方法，但现有方法可能存在次优和缓慢的问题，经常导致不期望的运动或延迟。这是因为它们优化的是使机器人末端执行器匹配人类手的位置和方向，这也可能将机器人的工作空间限制在人类的工作空间范围内。与此不同，本文将重定向重新定义为一个姿态对齐问题，从而实现了一种具备最优性保证的闭式几何解算法。关键思想是将机器人手臂对齐到人类的上臂和下臂姿态，这些姿态由肩、肘和腕 (SEW) 关键点识别；因此，该方法被称为 SEW-Mimic。该方法在标准商用 CPU 上具有快速推理能力 (3 kHz)，为下游应用留出计算开销；本文中的一个例子是避免双手自碰撞的安全滤波器。该方法适用于大多数 7 自由度机器人手臂和类人机器人，并且与输入关键点的来源无关。实验表明，SEW-Mimic 在计算时间和精度方面均优于其他重定向方法。一项初步用户研究表明，该方法提高了遥操作任务的成功率。初步分析表明，使用 SEW-Mimic 收集的数据由于其更平滑的特性而提高了策略学习的效果。SEW-Mimic 也被证明是一种加速全身类人机器人重定向的即插即用方法。最后，硬件演示展示了 SEW-Mimic 的实用性。结果强调了 SEW-Mimic 作为双臂机器人操作和类人机器人遥操作的基本构建模块的效用。

TLDR: This paper presents SEW-Mimic, a fast, closed-form geometric solution for retargeting human upper body motion to humanoid robots by aligning arm orientations, improving teleoperation task success and potentially accelerating policy learning.

简要说明: 本文提出SEW-Mimic，一种快速的闭式几何解法，通过对齐手臂方向将人体上半身运动重新定位到人形机器人，从而提高遥操作任务的成功率，并有可能加速策略学习。

Authors: Chuizheng Kong, Yunho Cho, Wonsuhk Jung, Idris Wibowo, Parth Shinde, Sundhar Vinodh-Sangeetha, Long Kiu Chung, Zhenyang Chen, Andrew Mattei, Advaith Nidumukkala, Alexander Elias, Danfei Xu, Taylor Higgins, Shreyas Kousik

UniDWM: Towards a Unified Driving World Model via Multifaceted Representation Learning

Abstract (English): Achieving reliable and efficient planning in complex driving environments requires a model that can reason over the scene's geometry, appearance, and dynamics. We present UniDWM, a unified driving world model that advances autonomous driving through multifaceted representation learning. UniDWM constructs a structure- and dynamic-aware latent world representation that serves as a physically grounded state space, enabling consistent reasoning across perception, prediction, and planning. Specifically, a joint reconstruction pathway learns to recover the scene's structure, including geometry and visual texture, while a collaborative generation framework leverages a conditional diffusion transformer to forecast future world evolution within the latent space. Furthermore, we show that our UniDWM can be deemed as a variation of VAE, which provides theoretical guidance for the multifaceted representation learning. Extensive experiments demonstrate the effectiveness of UniDWM in trajectory planning, 4D reconstruction and generation, highlighting the potential of multifaceted world representations as a foundation for unified driving intelligence. The code will be publicly available at https://github.com/Say2L/UniDWM.

摘要（中文）: 在复杂的驾驶环境中实现可靠且高效的规划需要一个能够推理场景的几何、外观和动态特性的模型。我们提出了UniDWM，一个统一的驾驶世界模型，它通过多方面的表示学习推动自动驾驶技术的发展。UniDWM构建了一个结构和动态感知的潜在世界表示，作为物理基础的状态空间，从而能够对感知、预测和规划进行一致的推理。具体而言，联合重构通路学习恢复场景的结构，包括几何形状和视觉纹理，而协作生成框架则利用条件扩散Transformer在潜在空间中预测未来的世界演变。此外，我们证明了我们的UniDWM可以被视为一种VAE的变体，这为多方面的表示学习提供了理论指导。大量的实验表明了UniDWM在轨迹规划、4D重建和生成方面的有效性，突出了多方面的世界表示作为统一驾驶智能基础的潜力。代码将在https://github.com/Say2L/UniDWM上公开。

TLDR: UniDWM proposes a unified driving world model using multifaceted representation learning to improve autonomous driving by jointly reconstructing scene structure and predicting future world evolution with a conditional diffusion transformer.

简要说明: UniDWM提出了一个统一的驾驶世界模型，通过多方面的表征学习来改进自动驾驶，通过联合重建场景结构并使用条件扩散Transformer预测未来世界演化。

Authors: Shuai Liu, Siheng Ren, Xiaoyao Zhu, Quanmin Liang, Zefeng Li, Qiang Li, Xin Hu, Kai Huang

RAPT: Model-Predictive Out-of-Distribution Detection and Failure Diagnosis for Sim-to-Real Humanoid Robots

Abstract (English): Deploying learned control policies on humanoid robots is challenging: policies that appear robust in simulation can execute confidently in out-of-distribution (OOD) states after Sim-to-Real transfer, leading to silent failures that risk hardware damage. Although anomaly detection can mitigate these failures, prior methods are often incompatible with high-rate control, poorly calibrated at the extremely low false-positive rates required for practical deployment, or operate as black boxes that provide a binary stop signal without explaining why the robot drifted from nominal behavior. We present RAPT, a lightweight, self-supervised deployment-time monitor for 50Hz humanoid control. RAPT learns a probabilistic spatio-temporal manifold of nominal execution from simulation and evaluates execution-time predictive deviation as a calibrated, per-dimension signal. This yields (i) reliable online OOD detection under strict false-positive constraints and (ii) a continuous, interpretable measure of Sim-to-Real mismatch that can be tracked over time to quantify how far deployment has drifted from training. Beyond detection, we introduce an automated post-hoc root-cause analysis pipeline that combines gradient-based temporal saliency derived from RAPT's reconstruction objective with LLM-based reasoning conditioned on saliency and joint kinematics to produce semantic failure diagnoses in a zero-shot setting. We evaluate RAPT on a Unitree G1 humanoid across four complex tasks in simulation and on physical hardware. In large-scale simulation, RAPT improves True Positive Rate (TPR) by 37% over the strongest baseline at a fixed episode-level false positive rate of 0.5%. On real-world deployments, RAPT achieves a 12.5% TPR improvement and provides actionable interpretability, reaching 75% root-cause classification accuracy across 16 real-world failures using only proprioceptive data.

摘要（中文）: 在人形机器人上部署学习到的控制策略极具挑战：经过Sim-to-Real迁移后，在仿真中看似具有鲁棒性的策略在分布外(OOD)状态下可能会自信地执行，从而导致静默失效，进而造成硬件损坏的风险。虽然异常检测可以缓解这些失效，但先前的方法通常与高频率控制不兼容，在实际部署所需的极低假阳性率下校准不佳，或者作为黑盒运行，只提供二元停止信号，无法解释机器人为何偏离标称行为。我们提出了RAPT，一种轻量级的自监督部署时监控器，适用于50Hz的人形机器人控制。RAPT从仿真中学习标称执行的概率时空流形，并将执行时的预测偏差评估为校准过的、逐维度的信号。这产生了(i)在严格的假阳性约束下可靠的在线OOD检测，以及(ii)对Sim-to-Real不匹配程度进行连续、可解释的度量，可以随时间跟踪，以量化部署与训练的偏离程度。除了检测之外，我们还引入了一种自动化的事后根本原因分析流程，该流程将从RAPT的重构目标中导出的基于梯度的时序显著性与基于LLM的推理相结合，LLM的推理以显著性和关节运动学为条件，从而在零样本设置中产生语义失效诊断。我们在一台宇树G1人形机器人上，在仿真和物理硬件上评估了 RAPT 在四个复杂任务中的表现。在大规模仿真中，RAPT 在固定 эпизод 级别 0.5% 假阳性率下，真阳性率 (TPR) 比最强的基线提高了 37%。在真实世界的部署中，RAPT 实现了 12.5% 的 TPR 提升，并提供了可操作的可解释性，仅使用本体感觉数据在 16 个真实世界的失效中达到了 75% 的根本原因分类准确率。

TLDR: This paper introduces RAPT, a self-supervised method for OOD detection and failure diagnosis in humanoid robots, using model-predictive deviation and LLM-based root cause analysis, demonstrating improved performance on real-world deployments.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了RAPT，一种用于人形机器人中OOD检测和故障诊断的自监督方法，利用模型预测偏差和基于LLM的根本原因分析，并在真实部署中展示了改进的性能。

Authors: Humphrey Munn, Brendan Tidd, Peter Bohm, Marcus Gallagher, David Howard

Sem-NaVAE: Semantically-Guided Outdoor Mapless Navigation via Generative Trajectory Priors

Abstract (English): This work presents a mapless global navigation approach for outdoor applications. It combines the exploratory capacity of conditional variational autoencoders (CVAEs) to generate trajectories and the semantic segmentation capabilities of a lightweight visual language model (VLM) to select the trajectory to execute. Open-vocabulary segmentation is used to score and select the generated trajectories based on natural language, and a state-of-the-art local planner executes velocity commands. One of the key features of the proposed approach is its ability to generate a large variability of trajectories and to select them and navigate in real-time. The approach was validated through real-world outdoor navigation experiments, achieving superior performance compared to state-of-the-art methods. A video showing an experimental run of the system can be found in https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=i3R5ey5O2yk.

摘要（中文）: 本文提出了一种用于户外应用的无需地图的全局导航方法。该方法结合了条件变分自编码器(CVAEs)生成轨迹的探索能力和轻量级视觉语言模型(VLM)的语义分割能力来选择要执行的轨迹。开放词汇分割用于根据自然语言对生成的轨迹进行评分和选择，并由最先进的局部规划器执行速度指令。所提出方法的一个关键特征是其能够生成大量可变轨迹，并实时选择这些轨迹并进行导航。该方法通过真实世界的户外导航实验进行了验证，与最先进的方法相比，实现了卓越的性能。系统实验运行的视频可在https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=i3R5ey5O2yk找到。

TLDR: This paper introduces Sem-NaVAE, a mapless outdoor navigation system using a conditional variational autoencoder (CVAE) for trajectory generation and a visual language model (VLM) for trajectory selection based on natural language, achieving real-time performance and superior results in outdoor navigation experiments.

简要说明: 这篇论文介绍了Sem-NaVAE，一个使用条件变分自编码器（CVAE）生成轨迹，并使用视觉语言模型（VLM）根据自然语言选择轨迹的无地图户外导航系统。该系统实现了实时性能，并在户外导航实验中取得了优异的成果。

Authors: Gonzalo Olguin, Javier Ruiz-del-Solar

Instance-Guided Unsupervised Domain Adaptation for Robotic Semantic Segmentation

Abstract (English): Semantic segmentation networks, which are essential for robotic perception, often suffer from performance degradation when the visual distribution of the deployment environment differs from that of the source dataset on which they were trained. Unsupervised Domain Adaptation (UDA) addresses this challenge by adapting the network to the robot's target environment without external supervision, leveraging the large amounts of data a robot might naturally collect during long-term operation. In such settings, UDA methods can exploit multi-view consistency across the environment's map to fine-tune the model in an unsupervised fashion and mitigate domain shift. However, these approaches remain sensitive to cross-view instance-level inconsistencies. In this work, we propose a method that starts from a volumetric 3D map to generate multi-view consistent pseudo-labels. We then refine these labels using the zero-shot instance segmentation capabilities of a foundation model, enforcing instance-level coherence. The refined annotations serve as supervision for self-supervised fine-tuning, enabling the robot to adapt its perception system at deployment time. Experiments on real-world data demonstrate that our approach consistently improves performance over state-of-the-art UDA baselines based on multi-view consistency, without requiring any ground-truth labels in the target domain.

摘要（中文）: 语义分割网络对于机器人感知至关重要，但当部署环境的视觉分布与训练所用的源数据集不同时，其性能往往会下降。无监督领域自适应（UDA）通过在没有额外监督的情况下将网络适应于机器人的目标环境来应对这一挑战，利用机器人长期运行中可能自然收集的大量数据。 在这种情况下，UDA方法可以利用整个环境地图中的多视角一致性，以无监督的方式微调模型并减轻领域偏移。 然而，这些方法仍然对跨视角实例级别的不一致性敏感。 在这项工作中，我们提出了一种从体积3D地图开始生成多视角一致伪标签的方法。 然后，我们利用基础模型的零样本实例分割能力来细化这些标签，从而强制执行实例级别的连贯性。 经过细化的标注可以作为自监督微调的监督信号，使机器人能够在部署时调整其感知系统。 在真实世界数据上的实验表明，我们的方法始终优于基于多视角一致性的最先进的 UDA 基线，而无需目标域中的任何真实标签。

TLDR: This paper introduces an instance-guided unsupervised domain adaptation method for robotic semantic segmentation, leveraging multi-view consistency and foundation model-based instance segmentation for label refinement in the target domain.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种用于机器人语义分割的实例引导的无监督领域自适应方法，该方法利用多视图一致性和基于基础模型的实例分割来改进目标域中的标签。

Authors: Michele Antonazzi, Lorenzo Signorelli, Matteo Luperto, Nicola Basilico

David vs. Goliath: Verifiable Agent-to-Agent Jailbreaking via Reinforcement Learning

Abstract (English): The evolution of large language models into autonomous agents introduces adversarial failures that exploit legitimate tool privileges, transforming safety evaluation in tool-augmented environments from a subjective NLP task into an objective control problem. We formalize this threat model as Tag-Along Attacks: a scenario where a tool-less adversary "tags along" on the trusted privileges of a safety-aligned Operator to induce prohibited tool use through conversation alone. To validate this threat, we present Slingshot, a 'cold-start' reinforcement learning framework that autonomously discovers emergent attack vectors, revealing a critical insight: in our setting, learned attacks tend to converge to short, instruction-like syntactic patterns rather than multi-turn persuasion. On held-out extreme-difficulty tasks, Slingshot achieves a 67.0% success rate against a Qwen2.5-32B-Instruct-AWQ Operator (vs. 1.7% baseline), reducing the expected attempts to first success (on solved tasks) from 52.3 to 1.3. Crucially, Slingshot transfers zero-shot to several model families, including closed-source models like Gemini 2.5 Flash (56.0% attack success rate) and defensive-fine-tuned open-source models like Meta-SecAlign-8B (39.2% attack success rate). Our work establishes Tag-Along Attacks as a first-class, verifiable threat model and shows that effective agentic attacks can be elicited from off-the-shelf open-weight models through environment interaction alone.

摘要（中文）: 大型语言模型演变为自主智能体引入了对抗性故障，这些故障利用了合法的工具权限，将工具增强环境中的安全评估从主观的自然语言处理任务转变为客观的控制问题。我们将这种威胁模型形式化为“搭便车攻击”（Tag-Along Attacks）：一种无工具的攻击者“搭便车”于安全对齐的操作员的信任权限，仅通过对话诱导产生被禁止的工具使用场景。为了验证这种威胁，我们提出了“弹弓”（Slingshot），一个“冷启动”强化学习框架，能够自主发现涌现的攻击向量，从而揭示一个关键的见解：在我们的设置中，学习到的攻击倾向于收敛为简短的、类似指令的句法模式，而不是多轮说服。在保留的高难度极端任务中，“弹弓”针对 Qwen2.5-32B-Instruct-AWQ 操作员取得了 67.0% 的成功率（基线为 1.7%），并将首次成功所需的预期尝试次数（在已解决的任务上）从 52.3 次降低到 1.3 次。至关重要的是，“弹弓”能够零样本迁移到多个模型系列，包括诸如 Gemini 2.5 Flash（56.0% 的攻击成功率）的闭源模型，以及诸如 Meta-SecAlign-8B（39.2% 的攻击成功率）的防御性微调开源模型。我们的工作确立了“搭便车攻击”作为一个一流的、可验证的威胁模型，并表明，通过仅环境交互，可以从现成的开源权重模型中引出有效的智能体攻击。

TLDR: This paper introduces 'Tag-Along Attacks,' a novel threat model where a tool-less agent jailbreaks a tool-augmented LLM agent via reinforcement learning. The findings reveal that short, instruction-like patterns are effective attack vectors, transferable across various models, including closed-source ones.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种新的威胁模型“Tag-Along Attacks”，其中一个无工具的代理通过强化学习攻击一个工具增强的 LLM 代理。研究结果表明，简短的指令式模式是有效的攻击向量，并且可以跨多种模型迁移，包括闭源模型。

Authors: Samuel Nellessen, Tal Kachman

Infinite-World: Scaling Interactive World Models to 1000-Frame Horizons via Pose-Free Hierarchical Memory

Abstract (English): We propose Infinite-World, a robust interactive world model capable of maintaining coherent visual memory over 1000+ frames in complex real-world environments. While existing world models can be efficiently optimized on synthetic data with perfect ground-truth, they lack an effective training paradigm for real-world videos due to noisy pose estimations and the scarcity of viewpoint revisits. To bridge this gap, we first introduce a Hierarchical Pose-free Memory Compressor (HPMC) that recursively distills historical latents into a fixed-budget representation. By jointly optimizing the compressor with the generative backbone, HPMC enables the model to autonomously anchor generations in the distant past with bounded computational cost, eliminating the need for explicit geometric priors. Second, we propose an Uncertainty-aware Action Labeling module that discretizes continuous motion into a tri-state logic. This strategy maximizes the utilization of raw video data while shielding the deterministic action space from being corrupted by noisy trajectories, ensuring robust action-response learning. Furthermore, guided by insights from a pilot toy study, we employ a Revisit-Dense Finetuning Strategy using a compact, 30-minute dataset to efficiently activate the model's long-range loop-closure capabilities. Extensive experiments, including objective metrics and user studies, demonstrate that Infinite-World achieves superior performance in visual quality, action controllability, and spatial consistency.

摘要（中文）: 我们提出了无限世界（Infinite-World），一个强大的交互式世界模型，能够在复杂现实世界环境中维持在1000+帧以上的一致视觉记忆。虽然现有的世界模型可以在具有完美真值的合成数据上高效优化，但由于嘈杂的姿态估计和视角重访的稀缺性，它们缺乏针对现实世界视频的有效训练范式。为了弥合这一差距，我们首先引入了一种分层、无姿态的记忆压缩器（HPMC），它可以递归地将历史潜在特征提炼成固定预算的表示。通过将压缩器与生成骨干网络联合优化，HPMC使模型能够以有界的计算成本自主地将生成锚定在遥远的过去，从而消除了对显式几何先验的需求。其次，我们提出了一种不确定性感知动作标注模块，该模块将连续运动离散化为三态逻辑。该策略最大限度地利用原始视频数据，同时保护确定性动作空间免受嘈杂轨迹的破坏，确保稳健的动作-响应学习。此外，在初步玩具研究的启发下，我们采用了一种重访密集微调策略，使用一个紧凑的30分钟数据集来高效激活模型远距离环路闭合的能力。包括客观指标和用户研究在内的大量实验表明，无限世界在视觉质量、动作可控性和空间一致性方面都取得了卓越的性能。

TLDR: The paper introduces Infinite-World, a world model that maintains coherent visual memory over 1000+ frames in real-world environments using a hierarchical pose-free memory compressor and uncertainty-aware action labeling to overcome challenges like noisy pose estimations and scarcity of revisit viewpoints.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种名为 Infinite-World 的世界模型，该模型通过使用分层无姿态记忆压缩器和不确定性感知动作标记，在真实世界环境中维持 1000+ 帧的连贯视觉记忆，克服了诸如嘈杂的姿态估计和稀疏重访视点等挑战。

Authors: Ruiqi Wu, Xuanhua He, Meng Cheng, Tianyu Yang, Yong Zhang, Zhuoliang Kang, Xunliang Cai, Xiaoming Wei, Chunle Guo, Chongyi Li, Ming-Ming Cheng

Context Learning for Multi-Agent Discussion

Abstract (English): Multi-Agent Discussion (MAD) has garnered increasing attention very recently, where multiple LLM instances collaboratively solve problems via structured discussion. However, we find that current MAD methods easily suffer from discussion inconsistency, LLMs fail to reach a coherent solution, due to the misalignment between their individual contexts.In this paper, we introduce a multi-LLM context learning method (M2CL) that learns a context generator for each agent, capable of dynamically generating context instructions per discussion round via automatic information organization and refinement. Specifically, inspired by our theoretical insights on the context instruction, M2CL train the generators to control context coherence and output discrepancies via a carefully crafted self-adaptive mechanism.It enables LLMs to avoid premature convergence on majority noise and progressively reach the correct consensus. We evaluate M2CL on challenging tasks, including academic reasoning, embodied tasks, and mobile control. The results show that the performance of M2CL significantly surpasses existing methods by 20%--50%, while enjoying favorable transferability and computational efficiency.

摘要（中文）: 多智能体讨论（MAD）最近受到了越来越多的关注，其中多个LLM实例通过结构化的讨论协作解决问题。然而，我们发现当前的MAD方法容易受到讨论不一致性的影响，LLM由于个体语境之间的不匹配，难以达成连贯的解决方案。在本文中，我们提出了一种多LLM语境学习方法（M2CL），该方法为每个智能体学习一个语境生成器，能够通过自动信息组织和提炼，在每轮讨论中动态地生成语境指令。具体来说，受到我们对语境指令的理论见解的启发，M2CL训练生成器通过精心设计的自适应机制来控制语境一致性和输出差异，使LLM能够避免对主要噪声的过早收敛，并逐步达成正确的共识。我们在具有挑战性的任务上评估了M2CL，包括学术推理、具身任务和移动控制。结果表明，M2CL的性能显著优于现有方法20%--50%，同时具有良好的可迁移性和计算效率。

TLDR: The paper introduces M2CL, a multi-LLM context learning method that dynamically generates context instructions for agents in multi-agent discussions, improving consistency and consensus-reaching, and achieving significant performance gains across various tasks.

Authors: Xingyuan Hua, Sheng Yue, Xinyi Li, Yizhe Zhao, Jinrui Zhang, Ju Ren

Kimi K2.5: Visual Agentic Intelligence

Abstract (English): We introduce Kimi K2.5, an open-source multimodal agentic model designed to advance general agentic intelligence. K2.5 emphasizes the joint optimization of text and vision so that two modalities enhance each other. This includes a series of techniques such as joint text-vision pre-training, zero-vision SFT, and joint text-vision reinforcement learning. Building on this multimodal foundation, K2.5 introduces Agent Swarm, a self-directed parallel agent orchestration framework that dynamically decomposes complex tasks into heterogeneous sub-problems and executes them concurrently. Extensive evaluations show that Kimi K2.5 achieves state-of-the-art results across various domains including coding, vision, reasoning, and agentic tasks. Agent Swarm also reduces latency by up to $4.5\times$ over single-agent baselines. We release the post-trained Kimi K2.5 model checkpoint to facilitate future research and real-world applications of agentic intelligence.

摘要（中文）: 我们推出了Kimi K2.5，一个开源的多模态自主模型，旨在推进通用自主智能的发展。K2.5强调文本和视觉的联合优化，使两种模态相互增强。这包括一系列技术，如联合文本-视觉预训练、零视觉SFT以及联合文本-视觉强化学习。基于此多模态基础，K2.5引入了Agent Swarm，一个自导向的并行代理编排框架，能够动态地将复杂任务分解为异构的子问题并并发执行。广泛的评估表明，Kimi K2.5在包括编码、视觉、推理和自主任务等多个领域取得了最先进的结果。Agent Swarm相比于单代理基线，还将延迟降低了高达4.5倍。我们发布了经过后训练的Kimi K2.5模型检查点，以促进自主智能的未来研究和实际应用。

TLDR: The paper introduces Kimi K2.5, an open-source multimodal agentic model with Agent Swarm, achieving state-of-the-art results across coding, vision, reasoning, and agentic tasks, with reduced latency.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了 Kimi K2.5，一个开源的多模态智能体模型，它包括 Agent Swarm 框架，并在编码、视觉、推理和智能体任务中实现了最先进的结果，并降低了延迟。

TIDE: Trajectory-based Diagnostic Evaluation of Test-Time Improvement in LLM Agents

Abstract (English): Recent advances in autonomous LLM agents demonstrate their ability to improve performance through iterative interaction with the environment. We define this paradigm as Test-Time Improvement (TTI). However, the mechanisms under how and why TTI succeed or fail remain poorly understood, and existing evaluation metrics fail to capture their task optimization efficiency, behavior adaptation after erroneous actions, and the specific utility of working memory for task completion. To address these gaps, we propose Test-time Improvement Diagnostic Evaluation (TIDE), an agent-agnostic and environment-agnostic framework that decomposes TTI into three comprehensive and interconnected dimensions. The framework measures (1) the overall temporal dynamics of task completion and (2) identifies whether performance is primarily constrained by recursive looping behaviors or (3) by burdensome accumulated memory. Through extensive experiments across diverse agents and environments, TIDE highlights that improving agent performance requires more than scaling internal reasoning, calling for explicitly optimizing the interaction dynamics between the agent and the environment.

摘要（中文）: 自主LLM智能体近年来的进展表明，它们可以通过与环境的迭代互动来提高性能。我们将这种范式定义为测试时改进（TTI）。然而，对于TTI成功或失败的机制和原因，我们仍然知之甚少，并且现有的评估指标未能捕捉到它们在任务优化效率、错误行为后的行为适应性以及工作记忆对任务完成的具体效用。为了弥补这些差距，我们提出了测试时改进诊断评估（TIDE），这是一个与智能体无关且与环境无关的框架，它将TTI分解为三个全面且相互关联的维度。该框架测量（1）任务完成的整体时间动态，并（2）识别性能是否主要受到递归循环行为的限制，或者（3）受到繁重累积记忆的限制。通过跨多种智能体和环境的大量实验，TIDE强调，提高智能体性能需要的不仅仅是扩展内部推理，还需要明确优化智能体与环境之间的互动动态。

TLDR: The paper introduces TIDE, a framework for evaluating the test-time improvement of LLM agents by analyzing task completion dynamics, looping behaviors, and memory usage, revealing that performance gains require optimizing agent-environment interaction beyond simply scaling internal reasoning.

简要说明: 该论文提出了TIDE，一个用于评估LLM Agent在测试时性能提升的框架，通过分析任务完成动态、循环行为和内存使用情况，揭示了性能提升需要优化 Agent 与环境的交互，而不仅仅是扩展内部推理能力。

Authors: Hang Yan, Xinyu Che, Fangzhi Xu, Qiushi Sun, Zichen Ding, Kanzhi Cheng, Jian Zhang, Tao Qin, Jun Liu, Qika Lin

Probabilistic Performance Guarantees for Multi-Task Reinforcement Learning

Abstract (English): Multi-task reinforcement learning trains generalist policies that can execute multiple tasks. While recent years have seen significant progress, existing approaches rarely provide formal performance guarantees, which are indispensable when deploying policies in safety-critical settings. We present an approach for computing high-confidence guarantees on the performance of a multi-task policy on tasks not seen during training. Concretely, we introduce a new generalisation bound that composes (i) per-task lower confidence bounds from finitely many rollouts with (ii) task-level generalisation from finitely many sampled tasks, yielding a high-confidence guarantee for new tasks drawn from the same arbitrary and unknown distribution. Across state-of-the-art multi-task RL methods, we show that the guarantees are theoretically sound and informative at realistic sample sizes.

摘要（中文）: 多任务强化学习训练可以执行多项任务的通用策略。虽然近年来取得了显著进展，但现有方法很少提供正式的性能保证，这对于在安全关键型环境中部署策略至关重要。我们提出了一种计算多任务策略在训练期间未见过的任务上的性能的高置信度保证的方法。具体而言，我们引入了一种新的泛化界限，它将（i）来自有限多次轨迹 rollouts 的每次任务的置信下界与（ii）来自有限多个采样任务的任务级泛化相结合，从而为从相同任意和未知分布中抽取的新任务提供高置信度保证。在最先进的多任务强化学习方法中，我们表明这些保证在理论上是合理的，并且在实际样本量下是有信息量的。

TLDR: This paper introduces a method for computing high-confidence performance guarantees for multi-task reinforcement learning policies, even on unseen tasks, by combining per-task lower confidence bounds with task-level generalization bounds.

简要说明: 该论文提出了一种为多任务强化学习策略计算高置信度性能保证的方法，即使是在未见过的任务上，通过结合每个任务的置信下限和任务级别的泛化界限。

Authors: Yannik Schnitzer, Mathias Jackermeier, Alessandro Abate, David Parker

See2Refine: Vision-Language Feedback Improves LLM-Based eHMI Action Designers

Abstract (English): Automated vehicles lack natural communication channels with other road users, making external Human-Machine Interfaces (eHMIs) essential for conveying intent and maintaining trust in shared environments. However, most eHMI studies rely on developer-crafted message-action pairs, which are difficult to adapt to diverse and dynamic traffic contexts. A promising alternative is to use Large Language Models (LLMs) as action designers that generate context-conditioned eHMI actions, yet such designers lack perceptual verification and typically depend on fixed prompts or costly human-annotated feedback for improvement. We present See2Refine, a human-free, closed-loop framework that uses vision-language model (VLM) perceptual evaluation as automated visual feedback to improve an LLM-based eHMI action designer. Given a driving context and a candidate eHMI action, the VLM evaluates the perceived appropriateness of the action, and this feedback is used to iteratively revise the designer's outputs, enabling systematic refinement without human supervision. We evaluate our framework across three eHMI modalities (lightbar, eyes, and arm) and multiple LLM model sizes. Across settings, our framework consistently outperforms prompt-only LLM designers and manually specified baselines in both VLM-based metrics and human-subject evaluations. Results further indicate that the improvements generalize across modalities and that VLM evaluations are well aligned with human preferences, supporting the robustness and effectiveness of See2Refine for scalable action design.

摘要（中文）: 自动驾驶车辆缺乏与其它道路使用者的自然沟通渠道，这使得外部人机界面(eHMI) 对于传递意图以及在共享环境中维持信任至关重要。然而，大多数eHMI研究依赖于开发者设计的消息-动作对，这些难以适应多样化和动态的交通环境。一个有前景的替代方案是使用大型语言模型(LLMs) 作为动作设计者，生成与上下文相关的eHMI动作；然而，此类设计者缺乏感知验证，并且通常依赖于固定的提示或昂贵的人工标注反馈来进行改进。我们提出了See2Refine，一个无人干预的闭环框架，该框架使用视觉语言模型(VLM) 感知评估作为自动视觉反馈来改进基于LLM的eHMI动作设计者。给定一个驾驶环境和一个候选的eHMI动作，VLM评估该动作的感知适当性，并使用该反馈迭代地修订设计者的输出，从而实现无需人工监督的系统化改进。我们评估了我们的框架在三种eHMI模态（灯条、眼睛和手臂）以及多种LLM模型尺寸上的表现。在各种设置中，我们的框架在基于VLM的指标和人类受试者评估中均始终优于仅使用提示的LLM设计者和手动指定的基线。结果进一步表明，改进具有跨模态的泛化性，并且VLM评估与人类偏好高度一致，这支持了See2Refine在可扩展动作设计方面的鲁棒性和有效性。

TLDR: The paper introduces See2Refine, a closed-loop framework using vision-language model (VLM) perceptual evaluation as feedback to improve LLM-based eHMI action designers for automated vehicles, achieving performance improvements without human supervision.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一个名为See2Refine的闭环框架，该框架使用视觉-语言模型（VLM）的感知评估作为反馈，以改进基于LLM的自动驾驶车辆外部人机界面(eHMI)动作设计器，无需人工干预即可实现性能提升。

Authors: Ding Xia, Xinyue Gui, Mark Colley, Fan Gao, Zhongyi Zhou, Dongyuan Li, Renhe Jiang, Takeo Igarashi

Rethinking the Role of Entropy in Optimizing Tool-Use Behaviors for Large Language Model Agents

Abstract (English): Tool-using agents based on Large Language Models (LLMs) excel in tasks such as mathematical reasoning and multi-hop question answering. However, in long trajectories, agents often trigger excessive and low-quality tool calls, increasing latency and degrading inference performance, making managing tool-use behavior challenging. In this work, we conduct entropy-based pilot experiments and observe a strong positive correlation between entropy reduction and high-quality tool calls. Building on this finding, we propose using entropy reduction as a supervisory signal and design two reward strategies to address the differing needs of optimizing tool-use behavior. Sparse outcome rewards provide coarse, trajectory-level guidance to improve efficiency, while dense process rewards offer fine-grained supervision to enhance performance. Experiments across diverse domains show that both reward designs improve tool-use behavior: the former reduces tool calls by 72.07% compared to the average of baselines, while the latter improves performance by 22.27%. These results position entropy reduction as a key mechanism for enhancing tool-use behavior, enabling agents to be more adaptive in real-world applications.

摘要（中文）: 基于大型语言模型（LLM）的工具型Agent在数学推理和多跳问答等任务中表现出色。然而，在长轨迹中，Agent常常触发过多且低质量的工具调用，从而增加延迟并降低推理性能，使得工具使用行为的管理极具挑战性。在这项工作中，我们进行了基于熵的先导性实验，并观察到熵减少与高质量工具调用之间存在显著的正相关关系。基于此发现，我们提出将熵减少用作监督信号，并设计了两种奖励策略来应对优化工具使用行为的不同需求。稀疏结果奖励提供了粗略的、轨迹级别的指导以提高效率，而密集过程奖励则提供了细粒度的监督以增强性能。跨多个领域的实验表明，两种奖励设计均改善了工具使用行为：前者与基线的平均水平相比，减少了72.07%的工具调用；后者提高了22.27%的性能。这些结果表明，熵减少是增强工具使用行为的关键机制，使Agent能够在实际应用中更具适应性。

TLDR: This paper explores using entropy reduction as a supervisory signal to improve the tool-use behavior of LLM agents, showing significant improvements in efficiency and performance through sparse and dense reward strategies.

简要说明: 本文探索使用熵减作为监督信号来改善LLM代理的工具使用行为，通过稀疏和密集奖励策略，在效率和性能方面均实现了显著提升。

Authors: Zeping Li, Hongru Wang, Yiwen Zhao, Guanhua Chen, Yixia Li, Keyang Chen, Yixin Cao, Guangnan Ye, Hongfeng Chai, Mengdi Wang, Zhenfei Yin

Beyond RAG for Agent Memory: Retrieval by Decoupling and Aggregation

Abstract (English): Agent memory systems often adopt the standard Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) pipeline, yet its underlying assumptions differ in this setting. RAG targets large, heterogeneous corpora where retrieved passages are diverse, whereas agent memory is a bounded, coherent dialogue stream with highly correlated spans that are often duplicates. Under this shift, fixed top-$k$ similarity retrieval tends to return redundant context, and post-hoc pruning can delete temporally linked prerequisites needed for correct reasoning. We argue retrieval should move beyond similarity matching and instead operate over latent components, following decoupling to aggregation: disentangle memories into semantic components, organise them into a hierarchy, and use this structure to drive retrieval. We propose xMemory, which builds a hierarchy of intact units and maintains a searchable yet faithful high-level node organisation via a sparsity--semantics objective that guides memory split and merge. At inference, xMemory retrieves top-down, selecting a compact, diverse set of themes and semantics for multi-fact queries, and expanding to episodes and raw messages only when it reduces the reader's uncertainty. Experiments on LoCoMo and PerLTQA across the three latest LLMs show consistent gains in answer quality and token efficiency.

摘要（中文）: 智能体记忆系统通常采用标准的检索增强生成（RAG）流程，但其基本假设在这种场景下有所不同。RAG针对的是大型、异构的语料库，其中检索到的段落是多样化的，而智能体记忆是有限的、连贯的对话流，具有高度相关的跨度，并且往往是重复的。在这种转变下，固定的 Top-$k$ 相似性检索倾向于返回冗余的上下文，而后验剪枝可能会删除正确推理所需的在时间上相关联的先决条件。我们认为，检索应该超越相似性匹配，转而基于潜在的组件进行操作，遵循解耦到聚合的模式：将记忆解耦为语义组件，将其组织成一个层次结构，并利用这种结构来驱动检索。我们提出 xMemory，它构建了一个完整的单元层次结构，并通过稀疏性-语义目标来保持可搜索但忠实的高层节点组织，该目标指导记忆的拆分和合并。在推理时，xMemory 自上而下地检索，选择一组紧凑、多样的主题和语义用于多事实查询，并且仅当它能减少阅读者的不确定性时才扩展到情节和原始消息。在 LoCoMo 和 PerLTQA 上对三个最新的 LLM 进行的实验表明，答案质量和 Token 效率都得到了持续的提升。

TLDR: The paper introduces xMemory, a novel agent memory system that moves beyond standard RAG by hierarchically organizing memories into semantic components for more efficient and relevant retrieval, demonstrating improved performance and token efficiency with LLMs.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种新的智能体记忆系统xMemory，它通过将记忆分层组织成语义组件，超越了标准的RAG，实现了更高效和相关的检索，并展示了与LLM一起使用时性能和token效率的提高。
