Authors: Zhanghao Hu, Qinglin Zhu, Hanqi Yan, Yulan He, Lin Gui

SAME: Stabilized Mixture-of-Experts for Multimodal Continual Instruction Tuning

Abstract (English): Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) achieve strong performance through instruction tuning, but real-world deployment requires them to continually expand their capabilities, making Multimodal Continual Instruction Tuning (MCIT) essential. Recent methods leverage sparse expert routing to promote task specialization, but we find that the expert routing process suffers from drift as the data distribution evolves. For example, a grounding query that previously activated localization experts may instead be routed to irrelevant experts after learning OCR tasks. Meanwhile, the grounding-related experts can be overwritten by new tasks and lose their original functionality. Such failure reflects two problems: router drift, where expert selection becomes inconsistent over time, and expert drift, where shared experts are overwritten across tasks. Therefore, we propose StAbilized Mixture-of-Experts (SAME) for MCIT. To address router drift, SAME stabilizes expert selection by decomposing routing dynamics into orthogonal subspaces and updating only task-relevant directions. To mitigate expert drift, we regulate expert updates via curvature-aware scaling using historical input covariance in a rehearsal-free manner. SAME also introduces adaptive expert activation to freeze selected experts during training, reducing redundant computation and cross-task interference. Extensive experiments demonstrate its SOTA performance.

摘要（中文）: 多模态大型语言模型(MLLMs)通过指令调优取得了强大的性能，但实际部署需要它们不断扩展能力，这使得多模态持续指令调优(MCIT)至关重要。最近的方法利用稀疏专家路由来促进任务专业化，但我们发现，随着数据分布的演变，专家路由过程会受到漂移的影响。例如，一个先前激活定位专家的基础查询，在学习了OCR任务后，可能会被路由到不相关的专家。同时，与基础相关的专家可能被新任务覆盖并丢失其原始功能。这种失败反映了两个问题：路由器漂移，即专家选择随时间推移变得不一致；以及专家漂移，即共享专家在不同任务中被覆盖。因此，我们提出了用于MCIT的稳定化混合专家(SAME)。为了解决路由器漂移问题，SAME通过将路由动态分解为正交子空间并仅更新任务相关方向来稳定专家选择。为了减轻专家漂移，我们以无排练的方式，利用历史输入协方差，通过曲率感知缩放来调节专家更新。SAME还引入了自适应专家激活，以在训练期间冻结选定的专家，从而减少冗余计算和跨任务干扰。大量实验证明了其SOTA性能。

TLDR: The paper introduces SAME, a stabilized mixture-of-experts approach for multimodal continual instruction tuning to address router drift and expert drift problems, achieving SOTA performance. It stabilizes expert selection and regulates expert updates in a rehearsal-free manner.

简要说明: 该论文提出了SAME，一种用于多模态持续指令调整的稳定混合专家方法，旨在解决路由器漂移和专家漂移问题，并实现了SOTA性能。它稳定了专家选择，并以无排练的方式调节专家更新。

Relevance: (8/10)
Novelty: (8/10)
Clarity: (9/10)

Authors: Zhen-Hao Xie, Jun-Tao Tang, Yu-Cheng Shi, Han-Jia Ye, De-Chuan Zhan, Da-Wei Zhou

Small Generalizable Prompt Predictive Models Can Steer Efficient RL Post-Training of Large Reasoning Models

Abstract (English): Reinforcement learning enhances the reasoning capabilities of large language models but often involves high computational costs due to rollout-intensive optimization. Online prompt selection presents a plausible solution by prioritizing informative prompts to improve training efficiency. However, current methods either depend on costly, exact evaluations or construct prompt-specific predictive models lacking generalization across prompts. This study introduces Generalizable Predictive Prompt Selection (GPS), which performs Bayesian inference towards prompt difficulty using a lightweight generative model trained on the shared optimization history. Intermediate-difficulty prioritization and history-anchored diversity are incorporated into the batch acquisition principle to select informative prompt batches. The small predictive model also generalizes at test-time for efficient computational allocation. Experiments across varied reasoning benchmarks indicate GPS's substantial improvements in training efficiency, final performance, and test-time efficiency over superior baseline methods.

摘要（中文）: 强化学习能够提升大型语言模型的推理能力，但由于优化过程需要大量的 rollout，通常涉及高昂的计算成本。在线提示词选择提供了一个可行的解决方案，通过优先选择包含信息的提示词来提高训练效率。然而，当前的方法要么依赖于代价高昂的精确评估，要么构建缺乏跨提示词泛化能力的特定于提示词的预测模型。本研究引入了可泛化的预测提示词选择（GPS），该方法利用在共享优化历史数据上训练的轻量级生成模型，对提示词难度进行贝叶斯推断。中间难度优先和历史锚定多样性被纳入批量获取原则，以选择信息丰富的提示词批次。该小型预测模型还可在测试时进行泛化，实现高效的计算资源分配。在多个不同的推理基准测试上的实验表明，与优秀的基线方法相比，GPS 在训练效率、最终性能和测试时效率方面均实现了显著提升。

TLDR: This paper introduces Generalizable Predictive Prompt Selection (GPS) to improve the training efficiency of reinforcement learning for large language models by prioritizing informative prompts using a lightweight, generalizable predictive model.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种名为Generalizable Predictive Prompt Selection (GPS) 的方法，通过使用轻量级的、可泛化的预测模型来优先选择信息量大的提示，从而提高大型语言模型强化学习的训练效率。

Authors: Yun Qu, Qi Wang, Yixiu Mao, Heming Zou, Yuhang Jiang, Weijie Liu, Clive Bai, Kai Yang, Yangkun Chen, Saiyong Yang, Xiangyang Ji

Zero-Shot Off-Policy Learning

Abstract (English): Off-policy learning methods seek to derive an optimal policy directly from a fixed dataset of prior interactions. This objective presents significant challenges, primarily due to the inherent distributional shift and value function overestimation bias. These issues become even more noticeable in zero-shot reinforcement learning, where an agent trained on reward-free data must adapt to new tasks at test time without additional training. In this work, we address the off-policy problem in a zero-shot setting by discovering a theoretical connection of successor measures to stationary density ratios. Using this insight, our algorithm can infer optimal importance sampling ratios, effectively performing a stationary distribution correction with an optimal policy for any task on the fly. We benchmark our method in motion tracking tasks on SMPL Humanoid, continuous control on ExoRL, and for the long-horizon OGBench tasks. Our technique seamlessly integrates into forward-backward representation frameworks and enables fast-adaptation to new tasks in a training-free regime. More broadly, this work bridges off-policy learning and zero-shot adaptation, offering benefits to both research areas.

摘要（中文）: 离线学习方法旨在直接从先前交互的固定数据集中推导出最优策略。这一目标带来诸多挑战，主要源于固有的分布偏移和价值函数高估偏差。这些问题在零样本强化学习中变得更加显著，在零样本强化学习中，智能体在无奖励数据上训练后，必须在测试时适应新任务，而无需额外训练。在这项工作中，我们通过发现后继测度与稳态密度比之间的理论联系，解决了零样本环境下的离线学习问题。利用这一洞察，我们的算法可以推断出最优的重要性采样比率，从而有效地执行稳态分布校正，并为任何任务提供即时最优策略。我们在 SMPL Humanoid 上的运动跟踪任务、ExoRL 上的连续控制任务以及长时程 OGBench 任务中对我们的方法进行了基准测试。我们的技术无缝集成到前向-后向表征框架中，并能够在无训练模式下快速适应新任务。更广泛地说，这项工作将离线学习和零样本适应联系起来，为两个研究领域都带来了益处。

TLDR: This paper introduces a zero-shot off-policy learning method that leverages successor measures to infer optimal importance sampling ratios for fast adaptation to new tasks without retraining, demonstrating strong performance across diverse benchmarks.

简要说明: 该论文提出了一种零样本离策略学习方法，利用后继测度推断最佳重要性采样比率，无需重新训练即可快速适应新任务，并在多个基准测试中表现出强大的性能。

Authors: Arip Asadulaev, Maksim Bobrin, Salem Lahlou, Dmitry Dylov, Fakhri Karray, Martin Takac

VLM-Guided Experience Replay

Abstract (English): Recent advances in Large Language Models (LLMs) and Vision-Language Models (VLMs) have enabled powerful semantic and multimodal reasoning capabilities, creating new opportunities to enhance sample efficiency, high-level planning, and interpretability in reinforcement learning (RL). While prior work has integrated LLMs and VLMs into various components of RL, the replay buffer, a core component for storing and reusing experiences, remains unexplored. We propose addressing this gap by leveraging VLMs to guide the prioritization of experiences in the replay buffer. Our key idea is to use a frozen, pre-trained VLM (requiring no fine-tuning) as an automated evaluator to identify and prioritize promising sub-trajectories from the agent's experiences. Across scenarios, including game-playing and robotics, spanning both discrete and continuous domains, agents trained with our proposed prioritization method achieve 11-52% higher average success rates and improve sample efficiency by 19-45% compared to previous approaches. https://esharony.me/projects/vlm-rb/

摘要（中文）: 大型语言模型(LLMs)和视觉语言模型(VLMs)的最新进展赋能了强大的语义和多模态推理能力，为增强强化学习(RL)的样本效率、高层规划和可解释性创造了新的机遇。虽然先前的工作已将LLMs和VLMs整合到RL的各个组成部分中，但回放缓冲区（一个用于存储和重用经验的核心组件）仍未得到探索。我们提出通过利用VLMs来指导回放缓冲区中经验的优先级排序来解决这个空白。我们的核心思想是使用一个冻结的、预训练的VLM（无需微调）作为自动评估器，以识别和优先排序来自智能体经验的有前景的子轨迹。在包括游戏和机器人等场景中，涵盖离散和连续域，通过我们提出的优先级排序方法训练的智能体，相比于以往方法，实现了平均成功率提高11-52%，并提高了19-45%的样本效率。

TLDR: This paper proposes using a pre-trained VLM to prioritize experiences in the replay buffer for reinforcement learning, showing significant performance improvements in game-playing and robotics across discrete and continuous domains.

Authors: Elad Sharony, Tom Jurgenson, Orr Krupnik, Dotan Di Castro, Shie Mannor

ROMA: Recursive Open Meta-Agent Framework for Long-Horizon Multi-Agent Systems

Abstract (English): Current agentic frameworks underperform on long-horizon tasks. As reasoning depth increases, sequential orchestration becomes brittle, context windows impose hard limits that degrade performance, and opaque execution traces make failures difficult to localize or debug. We introduce ROMA (Recursive Open Meta-Agents), a domain-agnostic framework that addresses these limitations through recursive task decomposition and structured aggregation. ROMA decomposes goals into dependency-aware subtask trees that can be executed in parallel, while aggregation compresses and validates intermediate results to control context growth. Our framework standardizes agent construction around four modular roles --Atomizer (which decides whether a task should be decomposed), Planner, Executor, and Aggregator -- which cleanly separate orchestration from model selection and enable transparent, hierarchical execution traces. This design supports heterogeneous multi-agent systems that mix models and tools according to cost, latency, and capability. To adapt ROMA to specific tasks without fine-tuning, we further introduce GEPA$+$, an improved Genetic-Pareto prompt proposer that searches over prompts within ROMA's component hierarchy while preserving interface contracts. We show that ROMA, combined with GEPA+, delivers leading system-level performance on reasoning and long-form generation benchmarks. On SEAL-0, which evaluates reasoning over conflicting web evidence, ROMA instantiated with GLM-4.6 improves accuracy by 9.9\% over Kimi-Researcher. On EQ-Bench, a long-form writing benchmark, ROMA enables DeepSeek-V3 to match the performance of leading closed-source models such as Claude Sonnet 4.5. Our results demonstrate that recursive, modular agent architectures can scale reasoning depth while remaining interpretable, flexible, and model-agnostic.

摘要（中文）: 当前自主代理框架在长程任务上表现不佳。随着推理深度的增加，顺序编排变得脆弱，上下文窗口施加了硬性限制，导致性能下降，而不透明的执行轨迹使得故障难以定位或调试。我们引入ROMA（递归开放元代理），这是一个领域无关的框架，通过递归任务分解和结构化聚合来解决这些限制。ROMA将目标分解为依赖感知的子任务树，可以并行执行，同时聚合压缩和验证中间结果以控制上下文增长。我们的框架围绕四个模块化角色——原子化器（决定是否应该分解任务）、规划器、执行器和聚合器——标准化代理构建，这干净地将编排与模型选择分离，并支持透明的、分层的执行轨迹。这种设计支持异构多代理系统，该系统根据成本、延迟和能力混合模型和工具。为了在不进行微调的情况下使ROMA适应特定任务，我们进一步引入了GEPA$+$, 一种改进的遗传-帕累托提示生成器，可在ROMA的组件层次结构中搜索提示，同时保持接口约定。我们表明，ROMA与GEPA+结合使用，可在推理和长文本生成基准测试中提供领先的系统级性能。在SEAL-0上，该基准测试评估对冲突网络证据的推理，使用GLM-4.6实例化的ROMA比Kimi-Researcher的准确率提高了9.9%。在EQ-Bench（一个长文本写作基准测试）上，ROMA使DeepSeek-V3能够达到领先的闭源模型（如Claude Sonnet 4.5）的性能。我们的结果表明，递归的、模块化的代理架构可以在保持可解释性、灵活性和模型无关性的同时扩展推理深度。

TLDR: The paper introduces ROMA, a recursive meta-agent framework for long-horizon multi-agent systems, achieving state-of-the-art results on reasoning and long-form generation benchmarks by using recursive task decomposition and structured aggregation.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了ROMA，一种用于长时程多智能体系统的递归元智能体框架，通过递归任务分解和结构化聚合，在推理和长格式生成基准测试中取得了最先进的结果。

Authors: Salaheddin Alzu'bi, Baran Nama, Arda Kaz, Anushri Eswaran, Weiyuan Chen, Sarvesh Khetan, Rishab Bala, Tu Vu, Sewoong Oh

Beyond Precision: Training-Inference Mismatch is an Optimization Problem and Simple LR Scheduling Fixes It

Abstract (English): Reinforcement Learning (RL) for training Large Language Models is notoriously unstable. While recent studies attribute this to "training inference mismatch stemming" from inconsistent hybrid engines, standard remedies, such as Importance Sampling, might fail during extended training runs. In this work, we analyze this instability through the lens of optimization, demonstrating that gradient noise and training-inference mismatch escalate in tandem as training progresses. Meanwhile, we find that the mismatch can be effectively suppressed by shrinking the update size. Taken together, we deduce that the mismatch is not merely a static numerical discrepancy, but a dynamic failure coupled with the model's optimization. Based on this insight, we propose a simple yet effective solution: a specialized Learning Rate (LR) scheduler. Instead of pre-defined decay schedule in traditional LR scheduler, our method dynamically triggers LR decay based on response length, which we identify as a reliable early-warning signal for impending instability. Empirical evidence suggests that by reducing the learning rate as gradient noise rises, we can consistently stabilize RL training and keep the training-inference mismatch at a safe level.

摘要（中文）: 强化学习（RL）用于训练大型语言模型时，其不稳定性是出了名的。虽然最近的研究将此归因于源于不一致混合引擎的“训练-推理不匹配”，但标准的补救措施，如重要性采样，可能在长时间的训练过程中失效。在这项工作中，我们通过优化的视角分析了这种不稳定性，证明了梯度噪声和训练-推理不匹配随着训练的进行而同步升级。同时，我们发现可以通过缩小更新步长来有效地抑制不匹配。综上所述，我们推断出不匹配不仅仅是一个静态的数值差异，而是一个与模型优化相结合的动态失效。基于此洞察，我们提出了一种简单而有效的解决方案：一种特殊的学习率（LR）调度器。与传统学习率调度器中预定义的衰减策略不同，我们的方法基于响应长度动态触发学习率衰减，我们将其识别为即将到来的不稳定性的可靠预警信号。经验证据表明，通过在梯度噪声升高时降低学习率，我们可以始终如一地稳定强化学习训练，并将训练-推理不匹配保持在安全水平。

TLDR: This paper analyzes training instability in RL for LLMs as an optimization problem related to training-inference mismatch, proposing a dynamic learning rate scheduler based on response length to stabilize training.

简要说明: 该论文将LLM的RL训练不稳定性分析为一个与训练-推理不匹配相关的优化问题，并提出了一种基于响应长度的动态学习率调度器来稳定训练。

Authors: Yaxiang Zhang, Yingru Li, Jiacai Liu, Jiawei Xu, Ziniu Li, Qian Liu, Haoyuan Li

Fast Autoregressive Video Diffusion and World Models with Temporal Cache Compression and Sparse Attention

Abstract (English): Autoregressive video diffusion models enable streaming generation, opening the door to long-form synthesis, video world models, and interactive neural game engines. However, their core attention layers become a major bottleneck at inference time: as generation progresses, the KV cache grows, causing both increasing latency and escalating GPU memory, which in turn restricts usable temporal context and harms long-range consistency. In this work, we study redundancy in autoregressive video diffusion and identify three persistent sources: near-duplicate cached keys across frames, slowly evolving (largely semantic) queries/keys that make many attention computations redundant, and cross-attention over long prompts where only a small subset of tokens matters per frame. Building on these observations, we propose a unified, training-free attention framework for autoregressive diffusion: TempCache compresses the KV cache via temporal correspondence to bound cache growth; AnnCA accelerates cross-attention by selecting frame-relevant prompt tokens using fast approximate nearest neighbor (ANN) matching; and AnnSA sparsifies self-attention by restricting each query to semantically matched keys, also using a lightweight ANN. Together, these modules reduce attention, compute, and memory and are compatible with existing autoregressive diffusion backbones and world models. Experiments demonstrate up to x5--x10 end-to-end speedups while preserving near-identical visual quality and, crucially, maintaining stable throughput and nearly constant peak GPU memory usage over long rollouts, where prior methods progressively slow down and suffer from increasing memory usage.

摘要（中文）: 自回归视频扩散模型支持流式生成，为长格式合成、视频世界模型和交互式神经游戏引擎打开了大门。然而，它们核心的注意力层在推理时成为主要的瓶颈：随着生成过程的进行，KV缓存不断增长，导致延迟增加和GPU内存消耗加剧，进而限制了可用的时间上下文并损害了长程一致性。在这项工作中，我们研究了自回归视频扩散中的冗余，并识别出三个持续存在的来源：帧之间近乎重复的缓存键、缓慢演化的（主要为语义相关的）查询/键导致大量注意力计算冗余，以及长提示上的交叉注意力，其中每帧只有一小部分token起作用。基于这些观察，我们提出了一种统一的、免训练的自回归扩散注意力框架：TempCache通过时间对应关系压缩KV缓存以限制缓存增长；AnnCA通过使用快速近似最近邻（ANN）匹配选择帧相关的提示token来加速交叉注意力；AnnSA通过将每个查询限制为语义匹配的键来稀疏化自注意力，同样也使用轻量级的ANN。总之，这些模块减少了注意力、计算和内存消耗，并且与现有的自回归扩散骨干网络和世界模型兼容。实验表明，在保持近乎相同的视觉质量的同时，端到端加速高达5到10倍，并且至关重要的是，在长时间的展开过程中保持了稳定的吞吐量和几乎恒定的峰值GPU内存使用量，而先前的方法会逐渐减慢速度并遭受内存使用量增加的困扰。

TLDR: This paper introduces a training-free framework for fast autoregressive video diffusion by compressing the KV cache, accelerating cross-attention, and sparsifying self-attention, enabling long-form video generation with stable throughput and memory usage.

简要说明: 该论文提出了一个无需训练的框架，通过压缩KV缓存、加速交叉注意力和稀疏化自注意力来加速自回归视频扩散，从而实现具有稳定吞吐量和内存使用量的长格式视频生成。

Authors: Dvir Samuel, Issar Tzachor, Matan Levy, Micahel Green, Gal Chechik, Rami Ben-Ari

CoMeT: Collaborative Memory Transformer for Efficient Long Context Modeling

Abstract (English): The quadratic complexity and indefinitely growing key-value (KV) cache of standard Transformers pose a major barrier to long-context processing. To overcome this, we introduce the Collaborative Memory Transformer (CoMeT), a novel architecture that enables LLMs to handle arbitrarily long sequences with constant memory usage and linear time complexity. Designed as an efficient, plug-in module, CoMeT can be integrated into pre-trained models with only minimal fine-tuning. It operates on sequential data chunks, using a dual-memory system to manage context: a temporary memory on a FIFO queue for recent events, and a global memory with a gated update rule for long-range dependencies. These memories then act as a dynamic soft prompt for the next chunk. To enable efficient fine-tuning on extremely long contexts, we introduce a novel layer-level pipeline parallelism strategy. The effectiveness of our approach is remarkable: a model equipped with CoMeT and fine-tuned on 32k contexts can accurately retrieve a passkey from any position within a 1M token sequence. On the SCROLLS benchmark, CoMeT surpasses other efficient methods and achieves performance comparable to a full-attention baseline on summarization tasks. Its practical effectiveness is further validated on real-world agent and user behavior QA tasks. The code is available at: https://anonymous.4open.science/r/comet-B00B/

摘要（中文）: 标准Transformer固有的二次复杂度以及无限增长的键值（KV）缓存是处理长上下文的一个主要障碍。为了克服这一问题，我们引入了协同记忆Transformer（CoMeT），一种新型架构，使 LLM 能够以恒定的内存使用量和线性时间复杂度处理任意长度的序列。CoMeT 被设计为一个高效的、即插即用的模块，只需进行极少的微调即可集成到预训练模型中。它对顺序数据块进行操作，使用双内存系统来管理上下文：一个 FIFO 队列上的临时内存用于近期事件，以及一个具有门控更新规则的全局内存用于远距离依赖关系。这些内存随后充当下一个块的动态软提示。为了在极长上下文中高效地进行微调，我们引入了一种新颖的层级流水线并行策略。我们的方法效果显著：配备 CoMeT 并在 32k 上下文中微调的模型能够从 1M 标记序列中的任何位置准确地检索通行密钥。在 SCROLLS 基准测试中，CoMeT 超越了其他高效方法，并在摘要任务上实现了与全注意力基线相当的性能。其实际有效性在真实世界的代理和用户行为问答任务中得到了进一步验证。代码可在以下网址获取：https://anonymous.4open.science/r/comet-B00B/

TLDR: The paper introduces CoMeT, a novel Transformer architecture designed to handle extremely long sequences with constant memory and linear complexity, validated on long-context retrieval and summarization tasks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了CoMeT，一种新型Transformer架构，旨在处理具有恒定内存和线性复杂度的极长序列，并在长上下文检索和摘要任务中进行了验证。

Authors: Runsong Zhao, Shilei Liu, Jiwei Tang, Langming Liu, Haibin Chen, Weidong Zhang, Yujin Yuan, Tong Xiao, Jingbo Zhu, Wenbo Su, Bo Zheng

Adversarial Reward Auditing for Active Detection and Mitigation of Reward Hacking

Abstract (English): Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) remains vulnerable to reward hacking, where models exploit spurious correlations in learned reward models to achieve high scores while violating human intent. Existing mitigations rely on static defenses that cannot adapt to novel exploitation strategies. We propose Adversarial Reward Auditing (ARA), a framework that reconceptualizes reward hacking as a dynamic, competitive game. ARA operates in two stages: first, a Hacker policy discovers reward model vulnerabilities while an Auditor learns to detect exploitation from latent representations; second, Auditor-Guided RLHF (AG-RLHF) gates reward signals to penalize detected hacking, transforming reward hacking from an unobservable failure into a measurable, controllable signal. Experiments across three hacking scenarios demonstrate that ARA achieves the best alignment-utility tradeoff among all baselines: reducing sycophancy to near-SFT levels while improving helpfulness, decreasing verbosity while achieving the highest ROUGE-L, and suppressing code gaming while improving Pass@1. Beyond single-domain evaluation, we show that reward hacking, detection, and mitigation all generalize across domains -- a Hacker trained on code gaming exhibits increased sycophancy despite no reward for this behavior, and an Auditor trained on one domain effectively suppresses exploitation in others, enabling efficient multi-domain defense with a single model.

摘要（中文）: 从

TLDR: The paper introduces Adversarial Reward Auditing (ARA), a dynamic framework for detecting and mitigating reward hacking in RLHF by framing it as a competitive game between a Hacker and an Auditor, demonstrating improved alignment-utility tradeoff across multiple scenarios and generalization across domains.

Authors: Mohammad Beigi, Ming Jin, Junshan Zhang, Qifan Wang, Lifu Huang

SafePred: A Predictive Guardrail for Computer-Using Agents via World Models

Abstract (English): With the widespread deployment of Computer-using Agents (CUAs) in complex real-world environments, prevalent long-term risks often lead to severe and irreversible consequences. Most existing guardrails for CUAs adopt a reactive approach, constraining agent behavior only within the current observation space. While these guardrails can prevent immediate short-term risks (e.g., clicking on a phishing link), they cannot proactively avoid long-term risks: seemingly reasonable actions can lead to high-risk consequences that emerge with a delay (e.g., cleaning logs leads to future audits being untraceable), which reactive guardrails cannot identify within the current observation space. To address these limitations, we propose a predictive guardrail approach, with the core idea of aligning predicted future risks with current decisions. Based on this approach, we present SafePred, a predictive guardrail framework for CUAs that establishes a risk-to-decision loop to ensure safe agent behavior. SafePred supports two key abilities: (1) Short- and long-term risk prediction: by using safety policies as the basis for risk prediction, SafePred leverages the prediction capability of the world model to generate semantic representations of both short-term and long-term risks, thereby identifying and pruning actions that lead to high-risk states; (2) Decision optimization: translating predicted risks into actionable safe decision guidances through step-level interventions and task-level re-planning. Extensive experiments show that SafePred significantly reduces high-risk behaviors, achieving over 97.6% safety performance and improving task utility by up to 21.4% compared with reactive baselines.

摘要（中文）: 随着计算机用户代理（CUAs）在复杂真实世界环境中的广泛部署，普遍存在的长期风险常常导致严重且不可逆转的后果。目前针对CUAs的大多数安全防护机制都采用被动式方法，仅在当前观察空间内约束代理行为。虽然这些安全防护机制可以防止即时短期风险（例如，点击钓鱼链接），但它们无法主动避免长期风险：看似合理的行动可能导致高风险后果，这些后果会延迟出现（例如，清理日志导致未来的审计无法追溯），而被动式安全防护机制无法在当前观察空间内识别这些风险。为了解决这些局限性，我们提出了一种预测性安全防护机制方法，其核心思想是将预测的未来风险与当前决策对齐。基于此方法，我们提出了SafePred，这是一个用于CUAs的预测性安全防护框架，它建立了风险到决策的闭环，以确保代理的安全行为。SafePred支持两项关键能力：（1）短期和长期风险预测：通过使用安全策略作为风险预测的基础，SafePred利用世界模型的预测能力生成短期和长期风险的语义表示，从而识别并剪除导致高风险状态的行动；（2）决策优化：通过步级干预和任务级重新规划，将预测的风险转化为可操作的安全决策指导。大量实验表明，与被动式基线相比，SafePred显著减少了高风险行为，实现了超过97.6%的安全性能，并将任务效用提高了高达21.4%。

TLDR: SafePred is a predictive guardrail framework for computer-using agents that uses world models to predict both short- and long-term risks, enabling safer decision-making and improved task utility compared to reactive methods.

简要说明: SafePred是一个用于计算机使用代理的预测性护栏框架，它使用世界模型来预测短期和长期风险，与反应式方法相比，能够实现更安全的决策和更高的任务效用。

Authors: Yurun Chen, Zeyi Liao, Ping Yin, Taotao Xie, Keting Yin, Shengyu Zhang

Beyond Mode Elicitation: Diversity-Preserving Reinforcement Learning via Latent Diffusion Reasoner

Abstract (English): Recent reinforcement learning (RL) methods improve LLM reasoning by optimizing discrete Chain-of-Thought (CoT) generation; however, exploration in token space often suffers from diversity collapse as policy entropy decreases due to mode elicitation behavior in discrete RL. To mitigate this issue, we propose Latent Diffusion Reasoning with Reinforcement Learning (LaDi-RL), a framework that conducts exploration directly in a continuous latent space, where latent variables encode semantic-level reasoning trajectories. By modeling exploration via guided diffusion, multi-step denoising distributes stochasticity and preserves multiple coexisting solution modes without mutual suppression. Furthermore, by decoupling latent-space exploration from text-space generation, we show that latent diffusion-based optimization is more effective than text-space policy optimization alone, while a complementary text policy provides additional gains when combined with latent exploration. Experiments on code generation and mathematical reasoning benchmarks demonstrate consistent improvements in both pass@1 and pass@k over discrete RL baselines, with absolute pass@1 gains of +9.4% on code generation and +5.7% on mathematical reasoning, highlighting diffusion-based latent RL as a principled alternative to discrete token-level RL for reasoning.

摘要（中文）: 近期强化学习（RL）方法通过优化离散思维链（CoT）生成来提升大型语言模型（LLM）的推理能力；然而，在Token空间中的探索常常会因策略熵的降低而导致多样性崩塌，这是由离散强化学习中的模式诱导行为引起的。为了缓解这个问题，我们提出了基于强化学习的潜在扩散推理（LaDi-RL），该框架直接在连续潜在空间中进行探索，其中潜在变量编码了语义级别的推理轨迹。通过利用引导扩散对探索过程进行建模，多步去噪过程可以分散随机性，并保留多个共存的解决方案模式，而不会相互抑制。此外，通过将潜在空间探索与文本空间生成解耦，我们表明，基于潜在扩散的优化比单纯的文本空间策略优化更有效，并且当与潜在探索相结合时，互补的文本策略可以带来额外的收益。在代码生成和数学推理基准测试上的实验表明，与离散强化学习基线相比，pass@1和pass@k均取得了持续的改进，其中代码生成的绝对pass@1增益为+9.4%，数学推理的绝对pass@1增益为+5.7%，突出了基于扩散的潜在RL作为一种用于推理的、有原则性的离散Token级别RL替代方案。

TLDR: This paper introduces LaDi-RL, a reinforcement learning framework that uses latent diffusion models to explore reasoning trajectories in a continuous space, improving performance in code generation and mathematical reasoning compared to discrete token-level RL.

简要说明: 该论文提出了LaDi-RL，一种强化学习框架，它使用潜在扩散模型探索连续空间中的推理轨迹，与离散token级RL相比，提高了代码生成和数学推理的性能。

Authors: Haoqiang Kang, Yizhe Zhang, Nikki Lijing Kuang, Yi-An Ma, Lianhui Qin

TRIP-Bench: A Benchmark for Long-Horizon Interactive Agents in Real-World Scenarios

Abstract (English): As LLM-based agents are deployed in increasingly complex real-world settings, existing benchmarks underrepresent key challenges such as enforcing global constraints, coordinating multi-tool reasoning, and adapting to evolving user behavior over long, multi-turn interactions. To bridge this gap, we introduce \textbf{TRIP-Bench}, a long-horizon benchmark grounded in realistic travel-planning scenarios. TRIP-Bench leverages real-world data, offers 18 curated tools and 40+ travel requirements, and supports automated evaluation. It includes splits of varying difficulty; the hard split emphasizes long and ambiguous interactions, style shifts, feasibility changes, and iterative version revision. Dialogues span up to 15 user turns, can involve 150+ tool calls, and may exceed 200k tokens of context. Experiments show that even advanced models achieve at most 50\% success on the easy split, with performance dropping below 10\% on hard subsets. We further propose \textbf{GTPO}, an online multi-turn reinforcement learning method with specialized reward normalization and reward differencing. Applied to Qwen2.5-32B-Instruct, GTPO improves constraint satisfaction and interaction robustness, outperforming Gemini-3-Pro in our evaluation. We expect TRIP-Bench to advance practical long-horizon interactive agents, and GTPO to provide an effective online RL recipe for robust long-horizon training.

摘要（中文）: 随着基于LLM的智能体被部署到日益复杂的现实世界环境中，现有的基准测试低估了诸如实施全局约束、协调多工具推理以及在漫长的多轮交互中适应不断变化的用户行为等关键挑战。为了弥补这一差距，我们推出了\textbf{TRIP-Bench}，这是一个基于真实旅行计划场景的长程基准测试。TRIP-Bench利用真实世界数据，提供18个精心设计的工具和40多个旅行要求，并支持自动评估。它包括不同难度的划分；困难划分侧重于漫长且模糊的交互、风格转变、可行性变化和迭代版本修订。对话跨越最多15个用户轮次，可能涉及150多次工具调用，并且可能超出20万个语料单元的上下文。实验表明，即使是先进模型在简单划分上也最多只能达到50%的成功率，而在困难子集上，性能则降至10%以下。我们进一步提出了\textbf{GTPO}，一种具有专门化的奖励归一化和奖励差分的在线多轮强化学习方法。应用于Qwen2.5-32B-Instruct时，GTPO提高了约束满足度和交互鲁棒性，在我们的评估中优于Gemini-3-Pro。我们期望TRIP-Bench能够促进实际长程交互式智能体的进步，并且GTPO能够为稳健的长程训练提供有效的在线RL配方。

TLDR: The paper introduces TRIP-Bench, a challenging new benchmark for long-horizon interactive agents in realistic travel planning scenarios, and GTPO, a reinforcement learning method that improves performance on this benchmark.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了TRIP-Bench，一个具有挑战性的新基准，用于在现实旅行规划场景中的长时域交互代理，并提出了GTPO，一种强化学习方法，可以提高在此基准上的性能。

Authors: Yuanzhe Shen, Zisu Huang, Zhengyuan Wang, Muzhao Tian, Zhengkang Guo, Chenyang Zhang, Shuaiyu Zhou, Zengjie Hu, Dailin Li, Jingwen Xu, Kaimin Wang, Wenhao Liu, Tianlong Li, Fengpeng Yue, Feng Hong, Cao Liu, Ke Zeng

FlowSteer: Interactive Agentic Workflow Orchestration via End-to-End Reinforcement Learning

Abstract (English): In recent years, a variety of powerful agentic workflows have been applied to solve a wide range of human problems. However, existing workflow orchestration still faces key challenges, including high manual cost, reliance on specific operators/large language models (LLMs), and sparse reward signals. To address these challenges, we propose FlowSteer, an end-to-end reinforcement learning framework that takes a lightweight policy model as the agent and an executable canvas environment, automating workflow orchestration through multi-turn interaction. In this process, the policy model analyzes execution states and selects editing actions, while the canvas executes operators and returns feedback for iterative refinement. Moreover, FlowSteer provides a plug-and-play framework that supports diverse operator libraries and interchangeable LLM backends. To effectively train this interaction paradigm, we propose Canvas Workflow Relative Policy Optimization (CWRPO), which introduces diversity-constrained rewards with conditional release to stabilize learning and suppress shortcut behaviors. Experimental results on twelve datasets show that FlowSteer significantly outperforms baselines across various tasks.

摘要（中文）: 近年来，各种强大的智能体工作流已被应用于解决广泛的人类问题。然而，现有的工作流编排仍然面临诸多关键挑战，包括高昂的人工成本、对特定算子/大型语言模型（LLM）的依赖，以及稀疏的奖励信号。为了解决这些挑战，我们提出了 FlowSteer，一个端到端的强化学习框架，它采用轻量级策略模型作为智能体，以及可执行的画布环境，通过多轮交互自动进行工作流编排。在这个过程中，策略模型分析执行状态并选择编辑动作，而画布执行算子并返回反馈以进行迭代改进。此外，FlowSteer 提供了一个即插即用的框架，支持多样化的算子库和可互换的 LLM 后端。为了有效地训练这种交互范式，我们提出了画布工作流相对策略优化（CWRPO），它引入了具有条件释放的多样性约束奖励，以稳定学习并抑制捷径行为。在十二个数据集上的实验结果表明，FlowSteer 在各种任务中显著优于基线方法。

TLDR: The paper introduces FlowSteer, an end-to-end reinforcement learning framework for agentic workflow orchestration that automates the process with a policy model interacting with an executable canvas environment, achieving superior performance compared to baselines.

简要说明: 该论文介绍FlowSteer，一个端到端的强化学习框架，用于智能体工作流编排。它通过策略模型与可执行画布环境交互来实现自动化，并且在基准测试中表现优异。

Authors: Mingda Zhang, Haoran Luo, Tiesunlong Shen, Qika Lin, Xiaoying Tang, Rui Mao, Erik Cambria

Contribution-aware Token Compression for Efficient Video Understanding via Reinforcement Learning

Abstract (English): Video large language models have demonstrated remarkable capabilities in video understanding tasks. However, the redundancy of video tokens introduces significant computational overhead during inference, limiting their practical deployment. Many compression algorithms are proposed to prioritize retaining features with the highest attention scores to minimize perturbations in attention computations. However, the correlation between attention scores and their actual contribution to correct answers remains ambiguous. To address the above limitation, we propose a novel \textbf{C}ontribution-\textbf{a}ware token \textbf{Co}mpression algorithm for \textbf{VID}eo understanding (\textbf{CaCoVID}) that explicitly optimizes the token selection policy based on the contribution of tokens to correct predictions. First, we introduce a reinforcement learning-based framework that optimizes a policy network to select video token combinations with the greatest contribution to correct predictions. This paradigm shifts the focus from passive token preservation to active discovery of optimal compressed token combinations. Secondly, we propose a combinatorial policy optimization algorithm with online combination space sampling, which dramatically reduces the exploration space for video token combinations and accelerates the convergence speed of policy optimization. Extensive experiments on diverse video understanding benchmarks demonstrate the effectiveness of CaCoVID. Codes will be released.

摘要（中文）: 视频大语言模型在视频理解任务中展现出了卓越的能力。然而，视频令牌的冗余在推理过程中引入了显著的计算开销，限制了它们的实际部署。许多压缩算法被提出，旨在优先保留具有最高注意力得分的特征，以最大程度地减少注意力计算中的扰动。然而，注意力得分与其对正确答案的实际贡献之间的相关性仍然不明确。为了解决上述局限性，我们提出了一种新颖的\textbf{贡献感知}令牌\textbf{压缩}算法，用于\textbf{视频}理解（\textbf{CaCoVID}），该算法显式地基于令牌对正确预测的贡献来优化令牌选择策略。首先，我们引入了一个基于强化学习的框架，该框架优化了一个策略网络，以选择对正确预测具有最大贡献的视频令牌组合。这种范式将重点从被动的令牌保留转移到主动发现最优的压缩令牌组合。其次，我们提出了一种具有在线组合空间采样的组合策略优化算法，该算法显著减少了视频令牌组合的探索空间，并加速了策略优化的收敛速度。在各种视频理解基准测试上进行的大量实验证明了 CaCoVID 的有效性。代码将会发布。

TLDR: The paper proposes CaCoVID, a reinforcement learning-based video token compression algorithm that optimizes for token contribution to correct predictions, addressing the limitations of attention-score based methods and improving efficiency of video understanding models.

Authors: Yinchao Ma, Qiang Zhou, Zhibin Wang, Xianing Chen, Hanqing Yang, Jun Song, Bo Zheng

Reasoning with Autoregressive-Diffusion Collaborative Thoughts

Abstract (English): Autoregressive and diffusion models represent two complementary generative paradigms. Autoregressive models excel at sequential planning and constraint composition, yet struggle with tasks that require explicit spatial or physical grounding. Diffusion models, in contrast, capture rich spatial structure through high-dimensional generation, but lack the stepwise logical control needed to satisfy complex, multi-stage constraints or to reliably identify and correct errors. We introduce Collaborative Thoughts, a unified collaborative framework that enables autoregressive and diffusion models to reason and generate jointly through a closed-loop interaction. In Collaborative Thoughts, autoregressive models perform structured planning and constraint management, diffusion models instantiate these constraints as intermediate visual thoughts, and a vision-based critic module evaluates whether the visual thoughts satisfy the intended structural and physical requirements. This feedback is then used to iteratively refine subsequent planning and generation steps, mitigating error propagation across modalities. Importantly, Collaborative Thoughts uses the same collaborative loop regardless of whether the task is autoregressive question answering or diffusion-based visual generation. Through representative examples, we illustrate how Collaborative Thoughts can improve the reliability of spatial reasoning and the controllability of generation.

摘要（中文）: 自回归模型和扩散模型代表了两种互补的生成范式。自回归模型擅长序列规划和约束组合，但在需要明确空间或物理基础的任务中表现不佳。相比之下，扩散模型通过高维生成捕获丰富的空间结构，但缺乏满足复杂、多阶段约束或可靠地识别和纠正错误所需的逐步逻辑控制。我们引入了“协同思考”（Collaborative Thoughts），一个统一的协同框架，使自回归模型和扩散模型能够通过闭环交互进行联合推理和生成。在“协同思考”中，自回归模型执行结构化规划和约束管理，扩散模型将这些约束实例化为中间视觉思考，而基于视觉的评论模块评估视觉思考是否满足预期的结构和物理要求。然后，此反馈被用于迭代地改进后续的规划和生成步骤，从而减轻跨模态的误差传播。重要的是，“协同思考”使用相同的协同循环，无论任务是自回归问答还是基于扩散的视觉生成。通过具有代表性的例子，我们展示了“协同思考”如何提高空间推理的可靠性和生成的可控性。

TLDR: This paper introduces "Collaborative Thoughts," a framework combining autoregressive and diffusion models to improve spatial reasoning and controllable generation by iteratively refining plans and visual outputs through a feedback loop.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了“协作思维”（Collaborative Thoughts）框架，该框架结合了自回归和扩散模型，通过迭代地改进计划和视觉输出，从而提高空间推理和可控生成的能力。

Authors: Mu Yuan, Liekang Zeng, Guoliang Xing, Lan Zhang, Yunhao Liu

Boosting Maximum Entropy Reinforcement Learning via One-Step Flow Matching

Abstract (English): Diffusion policies are expressive yet incur high inference latency. Flow Matching (FM) enables one-step generation, but integrating it into Maximum Entropy Reinforcement Learning (MaxEnt RL) is challenging: the optimal policy is an intractable energy-based distribution, and the efficient log-likelihood estimation required to balance exploration and exploitation suffers from severe discretization bias. We propose \textbf{F}low-based \textbf{L}og-likelihood-\textbf{A}ware \textbf{M}aximum \textbf{E}ntropy RL (\textbf{FLAME}), a principled framework that addresses these challenges. First, we derive a Q-Reweighted FM objective that bypasses partition function estimation via importance reweighting. Second, we design a decoupled entropy estimator that rigorously corrects bias, which enables efficient exploration and brings the policy closer to the optimal MaxEnt policy. Third, we integrate the MeanFlow formulation to achieve expressive and efficient one-step control. Empirical results on MuJoCo show that FLAME outperforms Gaussian baselines and matches multi-step diffusion policies with significantly lower inference cost. Code is available at https://github.com/lzqw/FLAME.

摘要（中文）: 扩散策略具有表现力，但推理延迟较高。Flow Matching (FM) 能够实现单步生成，但将其集成到最大熵强化学习 (MaxEnt RL) 中具有挑战性：最优策略是一个难以处理的基于能量的分布，并且平衡探索与利用所需的有效对数似然估计会遭受严重离散化偏差的影响。我们提出了基于流的对数似然感知的最大熵强化学习 (FLAME)，这是一个原则性的框架，旨在解决这些挑战。首先，我们推导出一个Q-重权重的FM目标，通过重要性重加权绕过配分函数估计。其次，我们设计了一个解耦的熵估计器，严格地校正偏差，从而实现高效探索，并使策略更接近最优MaxEnt策略。第三，我们集成了MeanFlow公式，以实现富有表现力且高效的单步控制。在MuJoCo上的实验结果表明，FLAME优于高斯基线，并且在推理成本显著降低的情况下，与多步扩散策略相匹配。代码已在 https://github.com/lzqw/FLAME 上提供。

TLDR: The paper introduces FLAME, a novel framework for Maximum Entropy Reinforcement Learning that leverages Flow Matching for efficient one-step policy generation, overcoming challenges related to intractable energy-based distributions and discretization bias, and demonstrating improved performance with reduced inference cost on MuJoCo.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种新的最大熵强化学习框架FLAME，该框架利用流匹配实现高效的单步策略生成，克服了与难以处理的基于能量的分布和离散化偏差相关的挑战，并在MuJoCo上展示了改进的性能和降低的推理成本。

Authors: Zeqiao Li, Yijing Wang, Haoyu Wang, Zheng Li, Zhiqiang Zuo

Autonomous Question Formation for Large Language Model-Driven AI Systems

Abstract (English): Large language model (LLM)-driven AI systems are increasingly important for autonomous decision-making in dynamic and open environments. However, most existing systems rely on predefined tasks and fixed prompts, limiting their ability to autonomously identify what problems should be solved when environmental conditions change. In this paper, we propose a human-simulation-based framework that enables AI systems to autonomously form questions and set tasks by reasoning over their internal states, environmental observations, and interactions with other AI systems. The proposed method treats question formation as a first-class decision process preceding task selection and execution, and integrates internal-driven, environment-aware, and inter-agent-aware prompting scopes to progressively expand cognitive coverage. In addition, the framework supports learning the question-formation process from experience, allowing the system to improve its adaptability and decision quality over time. xperimental results in a multi-agent simulation environment show that environment-aware prompting significantly reduces no-eat events compared with the internal-driven baseline, and inter-agent-aware prompting further reduces cumulative no-eat events by more than 60% over a 20-day simulation, with statistically significant improvements (p < 0.05).

摘要（中文）: 由大型语言模型（LLM）驱动的AI系统在动态和开放环境中自主决策方面日益重要。然而，大多数现有系统依赖于预定义的任务和固定的提示，限制了它们在环境条件变化时自主识别应该解决的问题的能力。在本文中，我们提出了一个基于人类模拟的框架，该框架使AI系统能够通过推理其内部状态、环境观察以及与其他AI系统的交互，自主形成问题并设置任务。所提出的方法将问题形成视为先于任务选择和执行的首要决策过程，并集成了内部驱动、环境感知和跨智能体感知的提示范围，以逐步扩大认知覆盖范围。此外，该框架支持从经验中学习问题形成过程，从而使系统能够随着时间的推移提高其适应性和决策质量。在多智能体仿真环境中进行的实验结果表明，与内部驱动的基线相比，环境感知提示显著减少了未进食事件，而跨智能体感知提示在为期20天的模拟中进一步减少了超过60%的累积未进食事件，且具有统计学意义上的显著改进 (p < 0.05)。

TLDR: This paper proposes a framework for LLM-driven AI systems to autonomously form questions and set tasks based on internal states, environmental observations, and inter-agent interactions, demonstrating improved performance in a multi-agent simulation.

Authors: Hong Su

MAGIC: A Co-Evolving Attacker-Defender Adversarial Game for Robust LLM Safety

Abstract (English): Ensuring robust safety alignment is crucial for Large Language Models (LLMs), yet existing defenses often lag behind evolving adversarial attacks due to their \textbf{reliance on static, pre-collected data distributions}. In this paper, we introduce \textbf{MAGIC}, a novel multi-turn multi-agent reinforcement learning framework that formulates LLM safety alignment as an adversarial asymmetric game. Specifically, an attacker agent learns to iteratively rewrite original queries into deceptive prompts, while a defender agent simultaneously optimizes its policy to recognize and refuse such inputs. This dynamic process triggers a \textbf{co-evolution}, where the attacker's ever-changing strategies continuously uncover long-tail vulnerabilities, driving the defender to generalize to unseen attack patterns. Remarkably, we observe that the attacker, endowed with initial reasoning ability, evolves \textbf{novel, previously unseen combinatorial strategies} through iterative RL training, underscoring our method's substantial potential. Theoretically, we provide insights into a more robust game equilibrium and derive safety guarantees. Extensive experiments validate our framework's effectiveness, demonstrating superior defense success rates without compromising the helpfulness of the model. Our code is available at https://github.com/BattleWen/MAGIC.

摘要（中文）: 确保强大的安全对齐对于大型语言模型（LLMs）至关重要，然而，现有的防御措施往往滞后于不断演变的对抗性攻击，因为它们\textbf{依赖于静态的、预先收集的数据分布}。在本文中，我们提出了\textbf{MAGIC}，一种新颖的多轮多智能体强化学习框架，将LLM的安全对齐构建为一个对抗性的非对称博弈。具体而言，攻击者智能体学习迭代地将原始查询改写为欺骗性提示，而防御者智能体同时优化其策略以识别并拒绝此类输入。这种动态过程触发了\textbf{协同进化}，攻击者不断变化的策略持续揭示长尾漏洞，从而推动防御者泛化到未见过的攻击模式。值得注意的是，我们观察到攻击者，在具备初始推理能力的情况下，通过迭代的强化学习训练进化出\textbf{新颖的、先前未见过的组合策略}，突显了我们方法的巨大潜力。理论上，我们提供了对于更鲁棒的博弈均衡的见解，并推导出了安全保证。大量的实验验证了我们框架的有效性，证明了其卓越的防御成功率，且不损害模型的有用性。我们的代码可在https://github.com/BattleWen/MAGIC获取。

TLDR: The paper introduces MAGIC, a multi-agent reinforcement learning framework for enhancing LLM safety by co-evolving attacker and defender agents to identify and mitigate unseen adversarial attacks, demonstrating improved defense success without sacrificing helpfulness.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了MAGIC，一种多智能体强化学习框架，通过共同进化攻击者和防御者智能体来增强LLM的安全性，以识别和缓解未知的对抗性攻击，展示了在不牺牲模型有用性的前提下提高了防御成功率。

Authors: Xiaoyu Wen, Zhida He, Han Qi, Ziyu Wan, Zhongtian Ma, Ying Wen, Tianhang Zheng, Xingcheng Xu, Chaochao Lu, Qiaosheng Zhang

GOPO: Policy Optimization using Ranked Rewards

Abstract (English): Standard reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) trains a reward model on pairwise preference data and then uses it for policy optimization. However, while reward models are optimized to capture relative preferences, existing policy optimization techniques rely on absolute reward magnitudes during training. In settings where the rewards are non-verifiable such as summarization, instruction following, and chat completion, this misalignment often leads to suboptimal performance. We introduce Group Ordinal Policy Optimization (GOPO), a policy optimization method that uses only the ranking of the rewards and discards their magnitudes. Our rank-based transformation of rewards provides several gains, compared to Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), in settings with non-verifiable rewards: (1) consistently higher training/validation reward trajectories, (2) improved LLM-as-judge evaluations across most intermediate training steps, and (3) reaching a policy of comparable quality in substantially less training steps than GRPO. We demonstrate consistent improvements across a range of tasks and model sizes.

摘要（中文）: 基于人类反馈的标准强化学习 (RLHF) 首先在成对偏好数据上训练奖励模型，然后将其用于策略优化。然而，尽管奖励模型被优化以捕捉相对偏好，但现有的策略优化技术在训练过程中依赖于绝对奖励幅度。在奖励不可验证的场景中，例如摘要生成、指令跟随和聊天完成，这种不一致常常导致次优性能。我们 introduce 了 Group Ordinal Policy Optimization (GOPO)，一种仅使用奖励排序而舍弃其幅度的策略优化方法。与 Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) 相比，我们在不可验证奖励的场景中，基于排序的奖励转换提供了以下几个优势：（1）一致的更高的训练/验证奖励轨迹，（2）跨大多数中间训练步骤的改进的LLM-as-judge 评估，以及（3）以比 GRPO 显著更少的训练步骤达到质量相当的策略。我们证明了在各种任务和模型规模上的持续改进。

TLDR: The paper introduces Group Ordinal Policy Optimization (GOPO), a novel policy optimization method for reinforcement learning from human feedback that utilizes only the ranking of rewards, improving performance in tasks with non-verifiable rewards compared to existing methods.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种新的策略优化方法——群体序数策略优化(GOPO)。该方法仅使用奖励排名，在人类反馈强化学习中，与现有方法相比，在非可验证奖励的任务中提高了性能。

SimGym: Traffic-Grounded Browser Agents for Offline A/B Testing in E-Commerce

Abstract (English): A/B testing remains the gold standard for evaluating e-commerce UI changes, yet it diverts traffic, takes weeks to reach significance, and risks harming user experience. We introduce SimGym, a scalable system for rapid offline A/B testing using traffic-grounded synthetic buyers powered by Large Language Model agents operating in a live browser. SimGym extracts per-shop buyer profiles and intents from production interaction data, identifies distinct behavioral archetypes, and simulates cohort-weighted sessions across control and treatment storefronts. We validate SimGym against real human outcomes from real UI changes on a major e-commerce platform under confounder control. Even without alignment post training, SimGym agents achieve state of the art alignment with observed outcome shifts and reduces experiment cycles from weeks to under an hour , enabling rapid experimentation without exposure to real buyers.

摘要（中文）: A/B测试仍然是评估电商UI变更的金标准，但它会分流流量，需要数周才能达到显著性，并且存在损害用户体验的风险。我们引入SimGym，这是一个可扩展的系统，用于使用流量驱动的合成买家进行快速离线A/B测试。这些买家由运行在实时浏览器中的大型语言模型代理驱动。SimGym从生产交互数据中提取每个店铺的买家画像和意图，识别出不同的行为原型，并模拟跨越控制和处理店铺的队列加权会话。我们在一个大型电商平台上，通过对真实UI变更的真实人类结果进行混淆变量控制，来验证SimGym的有效性。即使在训练后没有进行对齐，SimGym代理也能达到与观察到的结果变化对齐的最新水平，并将实验周期从数周缩短到一小时以内，从而实现无需暴露于真实买家的快速实验。

TLDR: This paper introduces SimGym, a system using LLM agents to simulate e-commerce user behavior in a browser environment for offline A/B testing, significantly reducing experiment time compared to traditional methods.

An Empirical Study of World Model Quantization

Abstract (English): World models learn an internal representation of environment dynamics, enabling agents to simulate and reason about future states within a compact latent space for tasks such as planning, prediction, and inference. However, running world models rely on hevay computational cost and memory footprint, making model quantization essential for efficient deployment. To date, the effects of post-training quantization (PTQ) on world models remain largely unexamined. In this work, we present a systematic empirical study of world model quantization using DINO-WM as a representative case, evaluating diverse PTQ methods under both weight-only and joint weight-activation settings. We conduct extensive experiments on different visual planning tasks across a wide range of bit-widths, quantization granularities, and planning horizons up to 50 iterations. Our results show that quantization effects in world models extend beyond standard accuracy and bit-width trade-offs: group-wise weight quantization can stabilize low-bit rollouts, activation quantization granularity yields inconsistent benefits, and quantization sensitivity is highly asymmetric between encoder and predictor modules. Moreover, aggressive low-bit quantization significantly degrades the alignment between the planning objective and task success, leading to failures that cannot be remedied by additional optimization. These findings reveal distinct quantization-induced failure modes in world model-based planning and provide practical guidance for deploying quantized world models under strict computational constraints. The code will be available at https://github.com/huawei-noah/noah-research/tree/master/QuantWM.

摘要（中文）: 世界模型学习环境动力学的内部表征，使智能体能够在紧凑的潜在空间中模拟和推理未来状态，用于规划、预测和推断等任务。然而，运行世界模型依赖于巨大的计算成本和内存占用，使得模型量化对于高效部署至关重要。 迄今为止，后训练量化（PTQ）对世界模型的影响在很大程度上仍未被研究。在这项工作中，我们以DINO-WM作为代表案例，对世界模型量化进行了系统的经验研究，评估了在仅权重和联合权重-激活设置下的各种PTQ方法。我们对不同的视觉规划任务进行了广泛的实验，涵盖了广泛的位宽、量化粒度和长达50次迭代的规划范围。我们的结果表明，世界模型中的量化效应超越了标准的精度和位宽权衡：分组权重量化可以稳定低比特展开，激活量化粒度产生不一致的收益，且量化敏感性在编码器和预测器模块之间高度不对称。此外，激进的低比特量化会显著降低规划目标和任务成功之间的对齐度，导致额外的优化无法弥补的失败。这些发现揭示了基于世界模型的规划中独特的量化引起的失效模式，并为在严格的计算约束下部署量化的世界模型提供了实用指导。代码将在https://github.com/huawei-noah/noah-research/tree/master/QuantWM 中提供。

TLDR: This paper empirically studies the effects of post-training quantization (PTQ) on world models, revealing distinct quantization-induced failure modes and providing practical guidance for efficient deployment.

UniDriveDreamer: A Single-Stage Multimodal World Model for Autonomous Driving

Abstract (English): World models have demonstrated significant promise for data synthesis in autonomous driving. However, existing methods predominantly concentrate on single-modality generation, typically focusing on either multi-camera video or LiDAR sequence synthesis. In this paper, we propose UniDriveDreamer, a single-stage unified multimodal world model for autonomous driving, which directly generates multimodal future observations without relying on intermediate representations or cascaded modules. Our framework introduces a LiDAR-specific variational autoencoder (VAE) designed to encode input LiDAR sequences, alongside a video VAE for multi-camera images. To ensure cross-modal compatibility and training stability, we propose Unified Latent Anchoring (ULA), which explicitly aligns the latent distributions of the two modalities. The aligned features are fused and processed by a diffusion transformer that jointly models their geometric correspondence and temporal evolution. Additionally, structured scene layout information is projected per modality as a conditioning signal to guide the synthesis. Extensive experiments demonstrate that UniDriveDreamer outperforms previous state-of-the-art methods in both video and LiDAR generation, while also yielding measurable improvements in downstream

摘要（中文）: 世界模型在自动驾驶领域的数据合成方面展现出显著潜力。然而，现有方法主要集中于单模态生成，通常侧重于多摄像头视频或激光雷达序列合成。本文提出UniDriveDreamer，一种用于自动驾驶的单阶段统一多模态世界模型，能够直接生成多模态未来观测值，而无需依赖中间表征或级联模块。我们的框架引入了一个专为激光雷达设计的变分自编码器（VAE），用于编码输入激光雷达序列，以及一个用于多摄像头图像的视频VAE。为了确保跨模态兼容性和训练稳定性，我们提出统一潜在锚定（ULA），显式地对齐两种模态的潜在分布。对齐后的特征被融合，并通过扩散变换器处理，该变换器联合建模其几何对应关系和时间演化。此外，结构化的场景布局信息被投影为每个模态的条件信号，以指导合成。大量实验表明，UniDriveDreamer在视频和激光雷达生成方面均优于以往最先进的方法，同时在下游任务中也产生了可衡量的改进。

Research on World Models Is Not Merely Injecting World Knowledge into Specific Tasks

Abstract (English): World models have emerged as a critical frontier in AI research, aiming to enhance large models by infusing them with physical dynamics and world knowledge. The core objective is to enable agents to understand, predict, and interact with complex environments. However, current research landscape remains fragmented, with approaches predominantly focused on injecting world knowledge into isolated tasks, such as visual prediction, 3D estimation, or symbol grounding, rather than establishing a unified definition or framework. While these task-specific integrations yield performance gains, they often lack the systematic coherence required for holistic world understanding. In this paper, we analyze the limitations of such fragmented approaches and propose a unified design specification for world models. We suggest that a robust world model should not be a loose collection of capabilities but a normative framework that integrally incorporates interaction, perception, symbolic reasoning, and spatial representation. This work aims to provide a structured perspective to guide future research toward more general, robust, and principled models of the world.

摘要（中文）: 世界模型已成为人工智能研究的关键前沿，旨在通过注入物理动力学和世界知识来增强大型模型。其核心目标是使智能体能够理解、预测并与复杂环境交互。然而，当前的研究格局仍然支离破碎，各种方法主要集中于将世界知识注入到孤立的任务中，例如视觉预测、3D估计或符号接地，而非建立统一的定义或框架。虽然这些特定任务的集成带来了性能提升，但它们往往缺乏全面理解世界所需的系统连贯性。在本文中，我们分析了这种碎片化方法的局限性，并提出了世界模型的统一设计规范。我们认为，一个强大的世界模型不应是能力的松散集合，而应是一个规范性框架，它整体性地整合交互、感知、符号推理和空间表示。这项工作旨在提供一个结构化的视角，以指导未来的研究朝着更通用、稳健和有原则的世界模型发展。

TLDR: This paper analyzes the limitations of task-specific world model implementations and proposes a unified design specification that integrally incorporates interaction, perception, symbolic reasoning, and spatial representation for more robust and generalizable world models.

简要说明: 本文分析了特定任务世界模型实现的局限性，并提出了一个统一的设计规范，该规范整合了交互、感知、符号推理和空间表示，以实现更强大和更通用的世界模型。

Authors: Bohan Zeng, Kaixin Zhu, Daili Hua, Bozhou Li, Chengzhuo Tong, Yuran Wang, Xinyi Huang, Yifan Dai, Zixiang Zhang, Yifan Yang, Zhou Liu, Hao Liang, Xiaochen Ma, Ruichuan An, Tianyi Bai, Hongcheng Gao, Junbo Niu, Yang Shi, Xinlong Chen, Yue Ding, Minglei Shi, Kai Zeng, Yiwen Tang, Yuanxing Zhang, Pengfei Wan, Xintao Wang, Wentao Zhang

Self-Supervised Learning from Structural Invariance

Abstract (English): Joint-embedding self-supervised learning (SSL), the key paradigm for unsupervised representation learning from visual data, learns from invariances between semantically-related data pairs. We study the one-to-many mapping problem in SSL, where each datum may be mapped to multiple valid targets. This arises when data pairs come from naturally occurring generative processes, e.g., successive video frames. We show that existing methods struggle to flexibly capture this conditional uncertainty. As a remedy, we introduce a latent variable to account for this uncertainty and derive a variational lower bound on the mutual information between paired embeddings. Our derivation yields a simple regularization term for standard SSL objectives. The resulting method, which we call AdaSSL, applies to both contrastive and distillation-based SSL objectives, and we empirically show its versatility in causal representation learning, fine-grained image understanding, and world modeling on videos.

摘要（中文）: 联合嵌入自监督学习 (SSL) 是从视觉数据中进行无监督表征学习的关键范式，它通过学习语义相关数据对之间的不变性来实现。我们研究了自监督学习中的一对多映射问题，即每个数据点可能被映射到多个有效目标。当数据对来源于自然发生的生成过程时，例如连续的视频帧，就会出现这种情况。我们表明，现有方法难以灵活地捕捉这种条件不确定性。为了解决这个问题，我们引入了一个潜在变量来解释这种不确定性，并推导出了配对嵌入之间互信息的变分下界。我们的推导为标准自监督学习目标提供了一个简单的正则化项。由此产生的方法，我们称之为 AdaSSL，适用于基于对比学习和基于知识蒸馏的自监督学习目标，并且我们通过实验证明了它在因果表征学习、细粒度图像理解和视频世界建模方面的多功能性。

TLDR: The paper introduces AdaSSL, a self-supervised learning method using a latent variable to handle one-to-many mappings in data pairs, leading to improved performance in causal representation learning, fine-grained image understanding, and video world modeling.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了AdaSSL，一种自监督学习方法，它使用潜在变量来处理数据对中的一对多映射问题，从而提高因果表征学习、细粒度图像理解和视频世界建模的性能。

Authors: Yipeng Zhang, Hafez Ghaemi, Jungyoon Lee, Shahab Bakhtiari, Eilif B. Muller, Laurent Charlin

ECHO-2: A Large-Scale Distributed Rollout Framework for Cost-Efficient Reinforcement Learning

Abstract (English): Reinforcement learning (RL) is a critical stage in post-training large language models (LLMs), involving repeated interaction between rollout generation, reward evaluation, and centralized learning. Distributing rollout execution offers opportunities to leverage more cost-efficient inference resources, but introduces challenges in wide-area coordination and policy dissemination. We present ECHO-2, a distributed RL framework for post-training with remote inference workers and non-negligible dissemination latency. ECHO-2 combines centralized learning with distributed rollouts and treats bounded policy staleness as a user-controlled parameter, enabling rollout generation, dissemination, and training to overlap. We introduce an overlap-based capacity model that relates training time, dissemination latency, and rollout throughput, yielding a practical provisioning rule for sustaining learner utilization. To mitigate dissemination bottlenecks and lower cost, ECHO-2 employs peer-assisted pipelined broadcast and cost-aware activation of heterogeneous workers. Experiments on GRPO post-training of 4B and 8B models under real wide-area bandwidth regimes show that ECHO-2 significantly improves cost efficiency while preserving RL reward comparable to strong baselines.

摘要（中文）: 强化学习（RL）是大型语言模型（LLM）后训练的关键阶段，涉及回滚生成、奖励评估和中心化学习之间的重复交互。分布式的回滚执行提供了利用更具成本效益的推理资源的机会，但也带来了广域协调和策略传播方面的挑战。我们提出了ECHO-2，一个用于后训练的分布式RL框架，它采用远程推理工作节点并具有不可忽略的传播延迟。ECHO-2将中心化学习与分布式回滚相结合，并将有界的策略陈旧性视为用户可控的参数，从而使回滚生成、传播和训练能够重叠。我们引入了一种基于重叠的容量模型，该模型将训练时间、传播延迟和回滚吞吐量联系起来，从而产生一种实用的供应规则，以维持学习者的利用率。为了减轻传播瓶颈并降低成本，ECHO-2采用对等辅助的流水线式广播和成本感知的异构工作节点激活。在实际广域带宽条件下对40亿和80亿参数模型的GRPO后训练实验表明，ECHO-2在保持与强基线相当的RL奖励的同时，显著提高了成本效率。

TLDR: ECHO-2 is a distributed RL framework designed to improve cost-efficiency for post-training LLMs by overlapping rollout generation, dissemination, and training, using techniques like peer-assisted broadcast and cost-aware worker activation.

Authors: Jie Xiao, Meng Chen, Qingnan Ren, Song Jingwei, Jiaqi Huang, Yangshen Deng, Chris Tong, Wanyi Chen, Suli Wang, Ziqian Bi, Shuo Lu, Yiqun Duan, Xu Wang, Rymon Yu, Ween Yang, Lynn Ai, Eric Yang, Bill Shi

Self-Consolidation for Self-Evolving Agents

Abstract (English): While large language model (LLM) agents have demonstrated impressive problem-solving capabilities, they typically operate as static systems, lacking the ability to evolve through lifelong interaction. Existing attempts to bridge this gap primarily rely on retrieving successful past trajectories as demonstrations. However, this paradigm faces two critical limitations. First, by focusing solely on success, agents overlook the rich pedagogical value embedded in failed attempts, preventing them from identifying and avoiding recurrent pitfalls. Second, continually accumulating textual experiences not only increases the time consumption during retrieval but also inevitably introduces noise and exhausts the largest context window of current LLMs. To address these challenges, we propose a novel self-evolving framework for LLM agents that introduces a complementary evolution mechanism: First, a contrastive reflection strategy is introduced to explicitly summarize error-prone patterns and capture reusable insights. Second, we propose a self-consolidation mechanism that distills non-parametric textual experience into compact learnable parameters. This enables the agent to internalize extensive historical experience directly into its latent space. Extensive experiments demonstrate the advantages of our method in long-term agent evolution.

摘要（中文）: 大型语言模型（LLM）智能体虽然展现出了令人印象深刻的问题解决能力，但它们通常作为静态系统运行，缺乏通过终身交互进化的能力。现有弥合这一差距的尝试主要依赖于检索成功过去的轨迹作为示范。然而，这种范式面临两个关键限制。首先，通过仅关注成功，智能体忽略了失败尝试中蕴含的丰富教学价值，使其无法识别和避免重复出现的陷阱。其次，不断累积文本经验不仅增加了检索过程中的时间消耗，而且不可避免地引入了噪声并耗尽了当前LLM的最大上下文窗口。为了应对这些挑战，我们提出了一种用于LLM智能体的全新自进化框架，该框架引入了一种互补的进化机制：首先，引入了一种对比反思策略，以明确地总结易错模式并捕捉可重用的见解。其次，我们提出了一种自巩固机制，将非参数文本经验提炼为紧凑的可学习参数。这使得智能体能够将广泛的历史经验直接内化到其潜在空间中。大量实验证明了我们方法在长期智能体进化中的优势。

TLDR: This paper introduces a self-evolving framework for LLM agents that utilizes contrastive reflection on errors and self-consolidation to distill experience into learnable parameters, addressing limitations of retrieval-based approaches.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一个LLM代理的自进化框架，该框架利用对比反思错误和自我巩固将经验提炼成可学习的参数，解决了基于检索的方法的局限性。

Authors: Hongzhuo Yu, Fei Zhu, Guo-Sen Xie, Ling Shao

Grounding Generated Videos in Feasible Plans via World Models

Abstract (English): Large-scale video generative models have shown emerging capabilities as zero-shot visual planners, yet video-generated plans often violate temporal consistency and physical constraints, leading to failures when mapped to executable actions. To address this, we propose Grounding Video Plans with World Models (GVP-WM), a planning method that grounds video-generated plans into feasible action sequences using a learned action-conditioned world model. At test-time, GVP-WM first generates a video plan from initial and goal observations, then projects the video guidance onto the manifold of dynamically feasible latent trajectories via video-guided latent collocation. In particular, we formulate grounding as a goal-conditioned latent-space trajectory optimization problem that jointly optimizes latent states and actions under world-model dynamics, while preserving semantic alignment with the video-generated plan. Empirically, GVP-WM recovers feasible long-horizon plans from zero-shot image-to-video-generated and motion-blurred videos that violate physical constraints, across navigation and manipulation simulation tasks.

摘要（中文）: 大规模视频生成模型已经展现出作为零样本视觉规划器的新兴能力，然而视频生成的规划方案常常违背时间一致性和物理约束，导致映射到可执行动作时出现失败。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了一种利用世界模型对视频规划进行基础化的方法 (GVP-WM)，这是一种规划方法，它使用学习到的、以动作为条件的世界模型将视频生成的规划方案基础化为可行的动作序列。在测试时，GVP-WM 首先根据初始和目标观测生成视频规划，然后通过视频引导的潜在搭配将视频指导投影到动态可行的潜在轨迹流形上。特别是，我们将基础化过程表述为一个以目标为条件的潜在空间轨迹优化问题，该问题在世界模型动力学约束下联合优化潜在状态和动作，同时保持与视频生成规划方案的语义对齐。在经验上，GVP-WM 在导航和操作模拟任务中，可以从违反物理约束的零样本图像到视频生成以及运动模糊视频中恢复可行的长程规划。

TLDR: The paper introduces GVP-WM, a method for grounding video-generated plans into feasible action sequences by using a learned action-conditioned world model to address issues of temporal inconsistency and physical constraint violations common in video-based planners.

Authors: Christos Ziakas, Amir Bar, Alessandra Russo

Grad2Reward: From Sparse Judgment to Dense Rewards for Improving Open-Ended LLM Reasoning

Abstract (English): Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has catalyzed significant breakthroughs in complex LLM reasoning within verifiable domains, such as mathematics and programming. Recent efforts have sought to extend this paradigm to open-ended tasks by employing LLMs-as-a-Judge to provide sequence-level rewards for policy optimization. However, these rewards are inherently sparse, failing to provide the fine-grained supervision necessary for generating complex, long-form trajectories. Furthermore, current work treats the Judge as a black-box oracle, discarding the rich intermediate feedback signals encoded in it. To address these limitations, we introduce Grad2Reward, a novel framework that extracts dense process rewards directly from the Judge's model inference process via a single backward pass. By leveraging gradient-based attribution, Grad2Reward enables precise token-level credit assignment, substantially enhancing training efficiency and reasoning quality. Additionally, Grad2Reward introduces a self-judging mechanism, allowing the policy to improve through its own evaluative signals without training specialized reward models or reliance on superior external Judges. The experiments demonstrate that policies optimized with Grad2Reward achieve outstanding performance across diverse open-ended tasks, affirming its effectiveness and broad generalizability.

摘要（中文）: 基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）已在可验证领域（如数学和编程）内复杂的大语言模型推理方面催化了重大突破。最近的研究致力于通过采用大语言模型作为评判者（LLMs-as-a-Judge）来为开放式任务提供序列级别的奖励，以优化策略。然而，这些奖励本质上是稀疏的，无法提供生成复杂、长形式轨迹所需的细粒度监督。此外，目前的工作将评判者视为黑盒预言机，忽略了其中编码的丰富的中间反馈信号。为了解决这些局限性，我们引入了 Grad2Reward，这是一个新颖的框架，通过单次反向传播，直接从评判者的模型推理过程中提取密集的过程奖励。通过利用基于梯度的归因方法，Grad2Reward 能够实现精确的令牌级别信用分配，从而显著提高训练效率和推理质量。此外，Grad2Reward 引入了一种自我评判机制，允许策略通过其自身的评估信号来改进，而无需训练专门的奖励模型或依赖于更优越的外部评判者。实验表明，使用 Grad2Reward 优化的策略在各种开放式任务中都取得了出色的性能，证实了其有效性和广泛的泛化能力。

TLDR: The paper introduces Grad2Reward, a novel reinforcement learning framework that extracts dense, token-level rewards from LLM judges via gradient-based attribution, improving training efficiency and reasoning quality in open-ended tasks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种名为 Grad2Reward 的新型强化学习框架，它通过基于梯度的归因从 LLM 评估器中提取密集的 token 级别奖励，从而提高开放式任务的训练效率和推理质量。

Authors: Zheng Zhang, Ao Lu, Yuanhao Zeng, Ziwei Shan, Jinjin Guo, Lufei Li, Yexin Li, Kan Ren

What Do Agents Learn from Trajectory-SFT: Semantics or Interfaces?

Abstract (English): Large language models are increasingly evaluated as interactive agents, yet standard agent benchmarks conflate two qualitatively distinct sources of success: semantic tool-use and interface-specific interaction pattern memorization. Because both mechanisms can yield identical task success on the original interface, benchmark scores alone are not identifiable evidence of environment-invariant capability. We propose PIPE, a protocol-level evaluation augmentation for diagnosing interface reliance by minimally rewriting environment interfaces while preserving task semantics and execution behavior. Across 16 environments from AgentBench and AgentGym and a range of open-source and API-based agents, PIPE reveals that trajectory-SFT substantially amplifies interface shortcutting: trained agents degrade sharply under minimal interface rewrites, while non-trajectory-trained models remain largely stable. We further introduce Interface Reliance (IR), a counterbalanced alias-based metric that quantifies preference for training-time interfaces, and show that interface shortcutting exhibits environment-dependent, non-monotonic training dynamics that remain invisible under standard evaluation. Our code is available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/What-Do-Agents-Learn-from-Trajectory-SFT-Semantics-or-Interfaces--0831/.

摘要（中文）: 大型语言模型作为交互式智能体正日益受到评估，然而，标准的智能体基准测试混淆了两种性质上不同的成功来源：语义化的工具使用和特定于界面的交互模式记忆。由于这两种机制都可以在原始界面上产生相同的任务成功，因此仅凭基准测试分数无法识别环境不变能力。我们提出了 PIPE，一种协议层面的评估增强方法，通过在保持任务语义和执行行为的同时，对环境界面进行最小程度的重写，来诊断对界面的依赖性。在来自 AgentBench 和 AgentGym 的 16 个环境以及一系列开源和基于 API 的智能体中，PIPE 表明，轨迹-SFT 显著放大了界面捷径：经过训练的智能体在最小的界面重写下性能急剧下降，而未经轨迹训练的模型则基本保持稳定。我们进一步引入了界面依赖性（IR），这是一种基于平衡别名的指标，用于量化对训练时期界面的偏好，并表明界面捷径表现出环境依赖、非单调的训练动态，而这些在标准评估下是不可见的。我们的代码可在 https://anonymous.4open.science/r/What-Do-Agents-Learn-from-Trajectory-SFT-Semantics-or-Interfaces--0831/ 获得。

TLDR: The paper introduces PIPE, a protocol evaluation method, and Interface Reliance (IR) metric to show that agents trained with trajectory-SFT overly rely on interface shortcuts rather than learning semantics, which is revealed by performance degradation under minimal interface changes.

Authors: Weizheng Gu, Chengze Li, Zhuohao Yu, Mengyuan Sun, Zhibang Yang, Wei Wang, Hongrui Jia, Shikun Zhang, Wei Ye

Non-Uniform Noise-to-Signal Ratio in the REINFORCE Policy-Gradient Estimator

Abstract (English): Policy-gradient methods are widely used in reinforcement learning, yet training often becomes unstable or slows down as learning progresses. We study this phenomenon through the noise-to-signal ratio (NSR) of a policy-gradient estimator, defined as the estimator variance (noise) normalized by the squared norm of the true gradient (signal). Our main result is that, for (i) finite-horizon linear systems with Gaussian policies and linear state-feedback, and (ii) finite-horizon polynomial systems with Gaussian policies and polynomial feedback, the NSR of the REINFORCE estimator can be characterized exactly-either in closed form or via numerical moment-evaluation algorithms-without approximation. For general nonlinear dynamics and expressive policies (including neural policies), we further derive a general upper bound on the variance. These characterizations enable a direct examination of how NSR varies across policy parameters and how it evolves along optimization trajectories (e.g. SGD and Adam). Across a range of examples, we find that the NSR landscape is highly non-uniform and typically increases as the policy approaches an optimum; in some regimes it blows up, which can trigger training instability and policy collapse.

摘要（中文）: 策略梯度方法被广泛应用于强化学习，然而，训练往往随着学习的进行而变得不稳定或速度减慢。我们通过策略梯度估计器的信噪比（NSR）来研究这一现象，信噪比定义为估计器方差（噪声）除以真实梯度平方范数（信号）进行归一化。我们的主要结果是，对于 (i) 具有高斯策略和线性状态反馈的有限视界线性系统，以及 (ii) 具有高斯策略和多项式反馈的有限视界多项式系统，REINFORCE估计器的NSR可以被精确地表征——无论是通过闭式解，还是通过数值矩评估算法——无需近似。对于一般的非线性动力学和表达能力强的策略（包括神经策略），我们进一步推导出方差的一般上限。这些表征能够直接检查NSR如何随策略参数变化，以及它如何沿着优化轨迹（例如SGD和Adam）演变。在一系列示例中，我们发现NSR分布高度不均匀，并且通常随着策略接近最优而增加；在某些情况下，它会爆发，从而可能引发训练不稳定和策略崩溃。

TLDR: This paper analyzes the noise-to-signal ratio (NSR) in REINFORCE, showing it is non-uniform and increases near optima, potentially causing instability. They provide exact characterizations for some system types and variance bounds for others.

简要说明: 该论文分析了REINFORCE算法中的噪声-信号比 (NSR)，表明它不均匀且在最优解附近增加，可能导致不稳定。他们为某些系统类型提供了精确的表征，并为其他系统提供了方差界限。

Authors: Haoyu Han, Heng Yang

Bridging the Sim-to-Real Gap with multipanda ros2: A Real-Time ROS2 Framework for Multimanual Systems

Abstract (English): We present $multipanda\_ros2$, a novel open-source ROS2 architecture for multi-robot control of Franka Robotics robots. Leveraging ros2 control, this framework provides native ROS2 interfaces for controlling any number of robots from a single process. Our core contributions address key challenges in real-time torque control, including interaction control and robot-environment modeling. A central focus of this work is sustaining a 1kHz control frequency, a necessity for real-time control and a minimum frequency required by safety standards. Moreover, we introduce a controllet-feature design pattern that enables controller-switching delays of $\le 2$ ms, facilitating reproducible benchmarking and complex multi-robot interaction scenarios. To bridge the simulation-to-reality (sim2real) gap, we integrate a high-fidelity MuJoCo simulation with quantitative metrics for both kinematic accuracy and dynamic consistency (torques, forces, and control errors). Furthermore, we demonstrate that real-world inertial parameter identification can significantly improve force and torque accuracy, providing a methodology for iterative physics refinement. Our work extends approaches from soft robotics to rigid dual-arm, contact-rich tasks, showcasing a promising method to reduce the sim2real gap and providing a robust, reproducible platform for advanced robotics research.

摘要（中文）: 我们提出了 $multipanda\_ros2$，一种新颖的开源 ROS2 架构，用于对 Franka Robotics 机器人进行多机器人控制。 该框架利用 ros2 control，为从单个进程控制任意数量的机器人提供原生的 ROS2 接口。 我们的核心贡献解决了实时力矩控制中的关键挑战，包括交互控制和机器人-环境建模。 本文的一个中心重点是维持 1kHz 的控制频率，这是实时控制的必要条件，也是安全标准要求的最低频率。 此外，我们引入了一种 controllet-feature 设计模式，该模式能够实现小于等于 2 毫秒的控制器切换延迟，从而促进可复现的基准测试和复杂的多机器人交互场景。 为了弥合仿真到现实 (sim2real) 的差距，我们集成了高保真 MuJoCo 仿真，并提供了运动学精度和动态一致性（力矩、力和控制误差）的量化指标。 此外，我们证明了真实世界中的惯性参数辨识可以显著提高力和力矩的精度，为迭代物理细化提供了一种方法。 我们的工作将软体机器人的方法扩展到了刚性双臂、富接触任务中，展示了一种有希望的方法来减少 sim2real 差距，并为高级机器人研究提供了一个稳健、可复现的平台。

TLDR: The paper introduces a ROS2 framework called `multipanda_ros2` for controlling multiple Franka Emika robots, focusing on real-time torque control, sim-to-real transfer using MuJoCo, and inertial parameter identification for improved accuracy.

Authors: Jon Škerlj, Seongjin Bien, Abdeldjallil Naceri, Sami Haddadin

Synchronized Online Friction Estimation and Adaptive Grasp Control for Robust Gentle Grasp

Abstract (English): We introduce a unified framework for gentle robotic grasping that synergistically couples real-time friction estimation with adaptive grasp control. We propose a new particle filter-based method for real-time estimation of the friction coefficient using vision-based tactile sensors. This estimate is seamlessly integrated into a reactive controller that dynamically modulates grasp force to maintain a stable grip. The two processes operate synchronously in a closed-loop: the controller uses the current best estimate to adjust the force, while new tactile feedback from this action continuously refines the estimation. This creates a highly responsive and robust sensorimotor cycle. The reliability and efficiency of the complete framework are validated through extensive robotic experiments.

摘要（中文）: 我们提出了一种统一的柔性机器人抓取框架，该框架协同整合了实时摩擦力估计和自适应抓取控制。我们提出了一种基于粒子滤波的新方法，利用基于视觉的触觉传感器实时估计摩擦系数。该估计无缝集成到一个反应型控制器中，该控制器动态调节抓取力以维持稳定的抓握。这两个过程在一个闭环中同步运行：控制器使用当前的最佳估计来调整力，而来自该动作的新触觉反馈不断改进估计。这形成了一个高度响应和稳健的感知运动循环。通过大量的机器人实验验证了该完整框架的可靠性和效率。

TLDR: This paper presents a closed-loop framework for gentle robotic grasping, combining real-time friction estimation via a particle filter with adaptive grasp control, validated through robotic experiments.

简要说明: 本文提出了一个用于机器人轻柔抓取的闭环框架，将基于粒子滤波的实时摩擦估计与自适应抓取控制相结合，并通过机器人实验验证。

Authors: Zhenwei Niu, Xiaoyi Chen, Jiayu Hu, Zhaoyang Liu, Xiaozu Ju

Reformulating AI-based Multi-Object Relative State Estimation for Aleatoric Uncertainty-based Outlier Rejection of Partial Measurements

Abstract (English): Precise localization with respect to a set of objects of interest enables mobile robots to perform various tasks. With the rise of edge devices capable of deploying deep neural networks (DNNs) for real-time inference, it stands to reason to use artificial intelligence (AI) for the extraction of object-specific, semantic information from raw image data, such as the object class and the relative six degrees of freedom (6-DoF) pose. However, fusing such AI-based measurements in an Extended Kalman Filter (EKF) requires quantifying the DNNs' uncertainty and outlier rejection capabilities. This paper presents the benefits of reformulating the measurement equation in AI-based, object-relative state estimation. By deriving an EKF using the direct object-relative pose measurement, we can decouple the position and rotation measurements, thus limiting the influence of erroneous rotation measurements and allowing partial measurement rejection. Furthermore, we investigate the performance and consistency improvements for state estimators provided by replacing the fixed measurement covariance matrix of the 6-DoF object-relative pose measurements with the predicted aleatoric uncertainty of the DNN.

摘要（中文）: 针对一组感兴趣对象的精确定位使移动机器人能够执行各种任务。随着能够部署深度神经网络(DNN)进行实时推理的边缘设备的兴起，有理由使用人工智能(AI)从原始图像数据中提取特定于对象、语义信息，例如对象类别和相对六自由度(6-DoF)姿态。然而，在扩展卡尔曼滤波器(EKF)中融合此类基于AI的测量值需要量化DNN的不确定性和离群值剔除能力。 本文介绍了在基于AI的、对象相关的状态估计中重新制定测量方程的优势。通过推导出使用直接对象相关姿态测量的EKF，我们可以解耦位置和旋转测量，从而限制错误旋转测量的影响并允许部分测量剔除。此外，我们研究了通过将6-DoF对象相关姿态测量的固定测量协方差矩阵替换为DNN预测的偶然不确定性，为状态估计器带来的性能和一致性提升。

TLDR: This paper reformulates the measurement equation in AI-based object-relative state estimation to improve the robustness of EKF-based localization by decoupling position and rotation measurements and incorporating aleatoric uncertainty for outlier rejection.

简要说明: 本文重新构建了基于人工智能的物体相对状态估计中的测量方程，通过解耦位置和旋转测量并纳入不确定性来提高基于EKF的定位的鲁棒性，从而提高异常值的拒绝能力。

Authors: Thomas Jantos, Giulio Delama, Stephan Weiss, Jan Steinbrener

Towards Exploratory and Focused Manipulation with Bimanual Active Perception: A New Problem, Benchmark and Strategy

Abstract (English): Recently, active vision has reemerged as an important concept for manipulation, since visual occlusion occurs more frequently when main cameras are mounted on the robot heads. We reflect on the visual occlusion issue and identify its essence as the absence of information useful for task completion. Inspired by this, we come up with the more fundamental problem of Exploratory and Focused Manipulation (EFM). The proposed problem is about actively collecting information to complete challenging manipulation tasks that require exploration or focus. As an initial attempt to address this problem, we establish the EFM-10 benchmark that consists of 4 categories of tasks that align with our definition (10 tasks in total). We further come up with a Bimanual Active Perception (BAP) strategy, which leverages one arm to provide active vision and another arm to provide force sensing while manipulating. Based on this idea, we collect a dataset named BAPData for the tasks in EFM-10. With the dataset, we successfully verify the effectiveness of the BAP strategy in an imitation learning manner. We hope that the EFM-10 benchmark along with the BAP strategy can become a cornerstone that facilitates future research towards this direction. Project website: EFManipulation.github.io.

摘要（中文）: 摘要： 近年来，主动视觉再次成为操控领域的重要概念，因为当主摄像头安装在机器人头部时，视觉遮挡现象更加频繁发生。我们反思视觉遮挡问题，并将其本质确定为缺乏有助于完成任务的信息。受此启发，我们提出了更根本的问题：探索与聚焦操控 (EFM)。所提出的问题是关于主动收集信息以完成需要探索或聚焦的具有挑战性的操控任务。作为解决该问题的初步尝试，我们建立了 EFM-10 基准，它由符合我们定义的 4 个类别的任务（总共 10 个任务）组成。我们进一步提出了一种双臂主动感知 (BAP) 策略，该策略利用一只手臂提供主动视觉，另一只手臂在操控时提供力觉感知。基于这个想法，我们为 EFM-10 中的任务收集了一个名为 BAPData 的数据集。利用该数据集，我们以模仿学习的方式成功验证了 BAP 策略的有效性。我们希望 EFM-10 基准以及 BAP 策略能够成为基石，促进未来朝这个方向的研究。项目网站：EFManipulation.github.io。

TLDR: This paper introduces the Exploratory and Focused Manipulation (EFM) problem, a benchmark (EFM-10), and a Bimanual Active Perception (BAP) strategy, demonstrating its effectiveness via imitation learning.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了探索性和聚焦性操作（EFM）问题，一个基准测试（EFM-10）和一个双臂主动感知（BAP）策略，并通过模仿学习验证了其有效性。

Authors: Yuxin He, Ruihao Zhang, Tianao Shen, Cheng Liu, Qiang Nie

ForSim: Stepwise Forward Simulation for Traffic Policy Fine-Tuning

Abstract (English): As the foundation of closed-loop training and evaluation in autonomous driving, traffic simulation still faces two fundamental challenges: covariate shift introduced by open-loop imitation learning and limited capacity to reflect the multimodal behaviors observed in real-world traffic. Although recent frameworks such as RIFT have partially addressed these issues through group-relative optimization, their forward simulation procedures remain largely non-reactive, leading to unrealistic agent interactions within the virtual domain and ultimately limiting simulation fidelity. To address these issues, we propose ForSim, a stepwise closed-loop forward simulation paradigm. At each virtual timestep, the traffic agent propagates the virtual candidate trajectory that best spatiotemporally matches the reference trajectory through physically grounded motion dynamics, thereby preserving multimodal behavioral diversity while ensuring intra-modality consistency. Other agents are updated with stepwise predictions, yielding coherent and interaction-aware evolution. When incorporated into the RIFT traffic simulation framework, ForSim operates in conjunction with group-relative optimization to fine-tune traffic policy. Extensive experiments confirm that this integration consistently improves safety while maintaining efficiency, realism, and comfort. These results underscore the importance of modeling closed-loop multimodal interactions within forward simulation and enhance the fidelity and reliability of traffic simulation for autonomous driving. Project Page: https://currychen77.github.io/ForSim/

摘要（中文）: 作为自动驾驶闭环训练和评估的基础，交通仿真仍然面临两个根本挑战：开放循环模仿学习引入的协变量偏移，以及反映真实世界交通中观察到的多模态行为的有限能力。尽管最近的框架，例如RIFT，已经通过群组相对优化部分解决了这些问题，但它们的前向仿真过程在很大程度上仍然是非反应性的，导致虚拟领域内不切实际的智能体交互，最终限制了仿真保真度。为了解决这些问题，我们提出了ForSim，一种逐步闭环前向仿真范式。在每个虚拟时间步，交通智能体通过物理上合理的运动动力学传播最能在时空上匹配参考轨迹的虚拟候选轨迹，从而在保证模态内一致性的同时，保留多模态行为的多样性。其他智能体通过逐步预测进行更新，从而产生连贯且具有交互感知的演化。当集成到RIFT交通仿真框架中时，ForSim与群组相对优化协同工作，以微调交通策略。 广泛的实验证实，这种集成在保持效率、真实性和舒适性的同时，始终如一地提高了安全性。这些结果强调了在前向仿真中建模闭环多模态交互的重要性，并提高了自动驾驶交通仿真的保真度和可靠性。项目主页：https://currychen77.github.io/ForSim/

TLDR: The paper introduces ForSim, a stepwise closed-loop forward simulation paradigm that enhances traffic simulation fidelity by improving agent interactions and preserving multimodal behavioral diversity, leading to safer and more realistic autonomous driving simulations.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了ForSim，一种逐步闭环前向仿真范例，通过改进智能体交互并保留多模态行为多样性来提高交通仿真保真度，从而实现更安全、更真实的自动驾驶仿真。
