Authors: Keyu Chen, Wenchao Sun, Hao Cheng, Zheng Fu, Sifa Zheng

Multi-Task Learning for Robot Perception with Imbalanced Data

Abstract (English): Multi-task problem solving has been shown to improve the accuracy of the individual tasks, which is an important feature for robots, as they have a limited resource. However, when the number of labels for each task is not equal, namely imbalanced data exist, a problem may arise due to insufficient number of samples, and labeling is not very easy for mobile robots in every environment. We propose a method that can learn tasks even in the absence of the ground truth labels for some of the tasks. We also provide a detailed analysis of the proposed method. An interesting finding is related to the interaction of the tasks. We show a methodology to find out which tasks can improve the performance of other tasks. We investigate this by training the teacher network with the task outputs such as depth as inputs. We further provide empirical evidence when trained with a small amount of data. We use semantic segmentation and depth estimation tasks on different datasets, NYUDv2 and Cityscapes.

摘要（中文）: 多任务问题求解已被证明可以提高各个任务的准确性，这对于资源有限的机器人来说是一个重要的特性。然而，当每个任务的标签数量不相等，即存在数据不平衡时，可能会由于样本数量不足而出现问题，并且对于移动机器人在每个环境中进行标注并不容易。我们提出了一种即使在某些任务缺乏真值标签的情况下也能学习任务的方法。我们还对所提出的方法进行了详细的分析。一个有趣的发现与任务的交互作用有关。我们展示了一种方法，可以找出哪些任务可以提高其他任务的性能。我们通过训练教师网络并将任务输出（如深度）作为输入来进行研究。我们进一步提供了在少量数据上训练时的经验证据。我们在不同的数据集NYUDv2和Cityscapes上使用了语义分割和深度估计任务。

TLDR: The paper proposes a multi-task learning method for robot perception that addresses the issue of imbalanced data by learning tasks even with missing ground truth labels and analyzes task interactions to improve performance, validated with semantic segmentation and depth estimation.

简要说明: 该论文提出了一种用于机器人感知的多任务学习方法，通过即使在缺少部分任务的真实标签情况下也能学习任务，从而解决了数据不平衡的问题，并分析了任务之间的交互以提高性能，通过语义分割和深度估计进行了验证。

Authors: Ozgur Erkent

Vision-only UAV State Estimation for Fast Flights Without External Localization Systems: A2RL Drone Racing Finalist Approach

Abstract (English): Fast flights with aggressive maneuvers in cluttered GNSS-denied environments require fast, reliable, and accurate UAV state estimation. In this paper, we present an approach for onboard state estimation of a high-speed UAV using a monocular RGB camera and an IMU. Our approach fuses data from Visual-Inertial Odometry (VIO), an onboard landmark-based camera measurement system, and an IMU to produce an accurate state estimate. Using onboard measurement data, we estimate and compensate for VIO drift through a novel mathematical drift model. State-of-the-art approaches often rely on more complex hardware (e.g., stereo cameras or rangefinders) and use uncorrected drifting VIO velocities, orientation, and angular rates, leading to errors during fast maneuvers. In contrast, our method corrects all VIO states (position, orientation, linear and angular velocity), resulting in accurate state estimation even during rapid and dynamic motion. Our approach was thoroughly validated through 1600 simulations and numerous real-world experiments. Furthermore, we applied the proposed method in the A2RL Drone Racing Challenge 2025, where our team advanced to the final four out of 210 teams and earned a medal.

摘要（中文）: 在复杂、无GNSS环境中进行快速飞行和高难度机动需要快速、可靠和精确的无人机状态估计。在本文中，我们提出了一种利用单目RGB相机和IMU实现高速无人机机载状态估计的方法。我们的方法融合了视觉惯性里程计(VIO)、基于机载地标的相机测量系统和IMU的数据，以产生精确的状态估计。通过使用机载测量数据，我们采用一种新颖的数学漂移模型来估计并补偿VIO漂移。目前最先进的方法通常依赖于更复杂的硬件（例如，立体相机或测距仪），并使用未经校正的漂移VIO速度、姿态和角速率，这会导致快速机动期间出现误差。相比之下，我们的方法校正了所有VIO状态（位置、姿态、线速度和角速度），从而即使在快速和动态运动期间也能实现精确的状态估计。我们的方法通过1600次仿真和大量现实世界实验得到了充分验证。此外，我们将所提出的方法应用于A2RL Drone Racing Challenge 2025，我们的团队从210支队伍中脱颖而出，晋级前四名并获得奖牌。

TLDR: This paper presents a vision-only state estimation method for UAVs that corrects VIO drift, enabling accurate navigation in GNSS-denied environments, validated through simulations and real-world experiments, and demonstrated by a finalist performance in the A2RL Drone Racing Challenge.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种仅使用视觉的无人机状态估计方法，通过校正视觉惯性里程计（VIO）漂移，实现了在无GNSS环境中精确导航。该方法通过模拟和真实实验验证，并在A2RL无人机竞速挑战赛中得到验证，其团队进入了决赛。

Authors: Filip Novák, Matěj Petrlík, Matej Novosad, Parakh M. Gupta, Robert Pěnička, Martin Saska

Real-Time Loop Closure Detection in Visual SLAM via NetVLAD and Faiss

Abstract (English): Loop closure detection (LCD) is a core component of simultaneous localization and mapping (SLAM): it identifies revisited places and enables pose-graph constraints that correct accumulated drift. Classic bag-of-words approaches such as DBoW are efficient but often degrade under appearance change and perceptual aliasing. In parallel, deep learning-based visual place recognition (VPR) descriptors (e.g., NetVLAD and Transformer-based models) offer stronger robustness, but their computational cost is often viewed as a barrier to real-time SLAM. In this paper, we empirically evaluate NetVLAD as an LCD module and compare it against DBoW on the KITTI dataset. We introduce a Fine-Grained Top-K precision-recall curve that better reflects LCD settings where a query may have zero or multiple valid matches. With Faiss-accelerated nearestneighbor search, NetVLAD achieves real-time query speed while improving accuracy and robustness over DBoW, making it a practical drop-in alternative for LCD in SLAM.

摘要（中文）: 回环检测 (LCD) 是同步定位与地图构建 (SLAM) 的核心组成部分：它能够识别重新访问的地点，并建立位姿图约束以校正累积的漂移。 经典的词袋 (bag-of-words) 方法，例如 DBoW，效率很高，但经常在外观变化和感知混淆的情况下性能下降。 与此同时，基于深度学习的视觉场景识别 (VPR) 描述符（例如，NetVLAD 和基于 Transformer 的模型）提供了更强的鲁棒性，但其计算成本通常被认为是实时 SLAM 的障碍。 在本文中，我们实证评估了 NetVLAD 作为 LCD 模块，并将其与 KITTI 数据集上的 DBoW 进行了比较。 我们引入了一种细粒度的 Top-K 精度-召回曲线，它能够更好地反映 LCD 设置，其中查询可能具有零个或多个有效匹配项。 借助 Faiss 加速的最近邻搜索，NetVLAD 实现了实时查询速度，同时提高了精度和鲁棒性，胜过 DBoW，使其成为 SLAM 中 LCD 的一个实用的即插即用替代方案。

TLDR: This paper demonstrates that NetVLAD, when accelerated with Faiss, can achieve real-time and improved accuracy for loop closure detection in visual SLAM compared to DBoW, making it a viable drop-in replacement.

简要说明: 本文证明，通过Faiss加速的NetVLAD在视觉SLAM中可以实现实时且更准确的闭环检测，优于DBoW，使其成为一个可行的即插即用替代方案。

Authors: Enguang Fan

AdaptNC: Adaptive Nonconformity Scores for Uncertainty-Aware Autonomous Systems in Dynamic Environments

Abstract (English): Rigorous uncertainty quantification is essential for the safe deployment of autonomous systems in unconstrained environments. Conformal Prediction (CP) provides a distribution-free framework for this task, yet its standard formulations rely on exchangeability assumptions that are violated by the distribution shifts inherent in real-world robotics. Existing online CP methods maintain target coverage by adaptively scaling the conformal threshold, but typically employ a static nonconformity score function. We show that this fixed geometry leads to highly conservative, volume-inefficient prediction regions when environments undergo structural shifts. To address this, we propose \textbf{AdaptNC}, a framework for the joint online adaptation of both the nonconformity score parameters and the conformal threshold. AdaptNC leverages an adaptive reweighting scheme to optimize score functions, and introduces a replay buffer mechanism to mitigate the coverage instability that occurs during score transitions. We evaluate AdaptNC on diverse robotic benchmarks involving multi-agent policy changes, environmental changes and sensor degradation. Our results demonstrate that AdaptNC significantly reduces prediction region volume compared to state-of-the-art threshold-only baselines while maintaining target coverage levels.

摘要（中文）: 严格的不确定性量化对于在非约束环境中安全部署自主系统至关重要。共形预测（CP）为此任务提供了一个无分布的框架，但其标准公式依赖于可交换性假设，而真实世界机器人技术中固有的分布偏移会违反这些假设。现有的在线CP方法通过自适应地调整共形阈值来维持目标覆盖率，但通常采用静态的非共形性评分函数。我们表明，当环境发生结构性转变时，这种固定的几何结构会导致高度保守、体积效率低下的预测区域。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了 \textbf{AdaptNC}，一个用于非共形性评分参数和共形阈值联合在线自适应的框架。AdaptNC利用自适应重加权方案来优化评分函数，并引入回放缓冲区机制来缓解评分转换期间发生的覆盖率不稳定。我们在涉及多智能体策略变化、环境变化和传感器退化的各种机器人基准测试中评估了AdaptNC。我们的结果表明，AdaptNC与最先进的仅阈值基线相比，显著减少了预测区域体积，同时保持了目标覆盖率水平。

TLDR: The paper proposes AdaptNC, a framework for adapting both nonconformity score parameters and the conformal threshold in conformal prediction to improve prediction region efficiency in dynamic robotic environments with distribution shifts.

简要说明: 该论文提出了 AdaptNC，一个用于在共形预测中自适应非一致性评分参数和共形阈值的框架，旨在提高具有分布偏移的动态机器人环境中预测区域的效率。

Authors: Renukanandan Tumu, Aditya Singh, Rahul Mangharam

Generating Physically Sound Designs from Text and a Set of Physical Constraints

Abstract (English): We present TIDES, a text informed design approach for generating physically sound designs based on a textual description and a set of physical constraints. TIDES jointly optimizes structural (topology) and visual properties. A pre-trained text-image model is used to measure the design's visual alignment with a text prompt and a differentiable physics simulator is used to measure its physical performance. We evaluate TIDES on a series of structural optimization problems operating under different load and support conditions, at different resolutions, and experimentally in the lab by performing the 3-point bending test on 2D beam designs that are extruded and 3D printed. We find that it can jointly optimize the two objectives and return designs that satisfy engineering design requirements (compliance and density) while utilizing features specified by text.

摘要（中文）: 我们提出TIDES，一种基于文本的设计方法，用于根据文本描述和一组物理约束生成物理上合理的结构设计。TIDES联合优化结构（拓扑）和视觉属性。我们使用预训练的文本-图像模型来衡量设计与文本提示的视觉对齐程度，并使用可微物理模拟器来衡量其物理性能。我们在不同载荷和支撑条件下、不同分辨率的一系列结构优化问题中评估TIDES，并通过对挤出和3D打印的二维梁设计进行三点弯曲试验，在实验室中进行实验。我们发现TIDES能够联合优化这两个目标，并返回满足工程设计要求（柔度和密度）并利用文本指定特征的设计。

TLDR: The paper introduces TIDES, a method that uses a pre-trained text-image model and a differentiable physics simulator to generate physically sound designs from text descriptions and physical constraints. It jointly optimizes structural integrity and visual aesthetics.

Authors: Gregory Barber, Todd C. Henry, Mulugeta A. Haile

ECHO: Entropy-Confidence Hybrid Optimization for Test-Time Reinforcement Learning

Abstract (English): Test-time reinforcement learning generates multiple candidate answers via repeated rollouts and performs online updates using pseudo-labels constructed by majority voting. To reduce overhead and improve exploration, prior work introduces tree structured rollouts, which share reasoning prefixes and branch at key nodes to improve sampling efficiency. However, this paradigm still faces two challenges: (1) high entropy branching can trigger rollout collapse, where the branching budget concentrates on a few trajectories with consecutive high-entropy segments, rapidly reducing the number of effective branches; (2) early pseudo-labels are noisy and biased, which can induce self-reinforcing overfitting, causing the policy to sharpen prematurely and suppress exploration. To address these issues, we propose Entropy Confidence Hybrid Group Relative Policy Optimization (ECHO). During rollout, ECHO jointly leverages local entropy and group level confidence to adaptively control branch width, and further introduces online confidence-based pruning to terminate persistently low confidence branches, avoiding high entropy traps and mitigating collapse. During policy updates, ECHO employs confidence adaptive clipping and an entropy confidence hybrid advantage shaping approach to enhance training robustness and mitigate early stage bias. Experiments demonstrate that ECHO achieves consistent gains on multiple mathematical and visual reasoning benchmarks, and generalizes more effectively under a limited rollout budget.

摘要（中文）: 测试时强化学习通过重复展开生成多个候选答案，并使用多数投票构建的伪标签进行在线更新。为了减少开销并改善探索，先前的工作引入了树形结构的展开，该结构共享推理前缀并在关键节点分支，从而提高采样效率。然而，这种范式仍然面临两个挑战：（1）高熵分支会触发rollout崩溃，其中分支预算集中在少数具有连续高熵片段的轨迹上，迅速减少有效分支的数量；（2）早期的伪标签具有噪声和偏差，这会诱导自我增强的过拟合，导致策略过早锐化并抑制探索。为了解决这些问题，我们提出熵置信度混合群组相对策略优化（ECHO）。在展开过程中，ECHO联合利用局部熵和群组级别的置信度来自适应地控制分支宽度，并进一步引入在线的基于置信度的剪枝来终止持续低置信度的分支，避免高熵陷阱并缓解崩溃。在策略更新期间，ECHO采用置信度自适应裁剪和熵置信度混合优势整形方法，以增强训练的鲁棒性并减轻早期阶段的偏差。实验表明，ECHO在多个数学和视觉推理基准测试上实现了持续的收益，并在有限的展开预算下更有效地泛化。

TLDR: The paper introduces ECHO, an entropy-confidence hybrid optimization method for test-time reinforcement learning that addresses issues of rollout collapse and noisy pseudo-labels, leading to improved performance and generalization with a limited rollout budget.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了ECHO，一种用于测试时强化学习的熵-置信度混合优化方法。它解决了 rollout 崩溃和噪声伪标签的问题，从而在有限的 rollout 预算下提高了性能和泛化能力。

Authors: Chu Zhao, Enneng Yang, Yuting Liu, Jianzhe Zhao, Guibing Guo

DCoPilot: Generative AI-Empowered Policy Adaptation for Dynamic Data Center Operations

Abstract (English): Modern data centers (DCs) hosting artificial intelligence (AI)-dedicated devices operate at high power densities with rapidly varying workloads, making minute-level adaptation essential for safe and energy-efficient operation. However, manually designing piecewise deep reinforcement learning (DRL) agents cannot keep pace with frequent dynamics shifts and service-level agreement (SLA) changes of an evolving DC. This specification-to-policy lag causes a lack of timely, effective control policies, which may lead to service outages. To bridge the gap, we present DCoPilot, a hybrid framework for generative control policies in dynamic DC operation. DCoPilot synergizes two distinct generative paradigms, i.e., a large language model (LLM) that performs symbolic generation of structured reward forms, and a hypernetwork that conducts parametric generation of policy weights. DCoPilot operates through three coordinated phases: (i) simulation scale-up, which stress-tests reward candidates across diverse simulation-ready (SimReady) scenes; (ii) meta policy distillation, where a hypernetwork is trained to output policy weights conditioned on SLA and scene embeddings; and (iii) online adaptation, enabling zero-shot policy generation in response to updated specifications. Evaluated across five control task families spanning diverse DC components, DCoPilot achieves near-zero constraint violations and outperforms all baselines across specification variations. Ablation studies validate the effectiveness of LLM-based unified reward generation in enabling stable hypernetwork convergence.

摘要（中文）: 现代数据中心(DC)托管着人工智能(AI)专用设备，在高功率密度下运行，且工作负载快速变化，因此需要分钟级的适应性以确保安全和节能运行。然而，手动设计分段式深度强化学习(DRL)智能体无法跟上不断演进的DC中频繁的动态变化和服务级别协议(SLA)变更。这种规范到策略的滞后导致缺乏及时有效的控制策略，进而可能导致服务中断。为了弥合这一差距，我们提出了DCoPilot，一个用于动态DC运行中生成式控制策略的混合框架。DCoPilot协同了两种不同的生成范式，即执行结构化奖励形式符号生成的大型语言模型(LLM)，以及执行策略权重参数生成的超网络。DCoPilot通过三个协调阶段运行：（i）仿真规模化，对各种仿真就绪(SimReady)场景中的奖励候选者进行压力测试；（ii）元策略蒸馏，训练超网络，使其输出以SLA和场景嵌入为条件的策略权重；（iii）在线适应，实现响应更新的规范的零样本策略生成。DCoPilot在涵盖各种DC组件的五个控制任务系列中进行评估，实现了接近于零的约束违例，并且在规范变化方面优于所有基线。消融研究验证了基于LLM的统一奖励生成在实现稳定超网络收敛方面的有效性。

TLDR: DCoPilot is a framework using LLMs and hypernetworks to generate control policies for dynamic data center operations, adapting to changing workloads and SLAs with near-zero constraint violations.

简要说明: DCoPilot是一个利用大型语言模型和超网络为动态数据中心运营生成控制策略的框架，它能够适应不断变化的工作负载和服务水平协议，且约束违规接近于零。

Authors: Minghao Li, Ruihang Wang, Rui Tan, Yonggang Wen

FORLER: Federated Offline Reinforcement Learning with Q-Ensemble and Actor Rectification

Abstract (English): In Internet-of-Things systems, federated learning has advanced online reinforcement learning (RL) by enabling parallel policy training without sharing raw data. However, interacting with real environments online can be risky and costly, motivating offline federated RL (FRL), where local devices learn from fixed datasets. Despite its promise, offline FRL may break down under low-quality, heterogeneous data. Offline RL tends to get stuck in local optima, and in FRL, one device's suboptimal policy can degrade the aggregated model, i.e., policy pollution. We present FORLER, combining Q-ensemble aggregation on the server with actor rectification on devices. The server robustly merges device Q-functions to curb policy pollution and shift heavy computation off resource-constrained hardware without compromising privacy. Locally, actor rectification enriches policy gradients via a zeroth-order search for high-Q actions plus a bespoke regularizer that nudges the policy toward them. A $δ$-periodic strategy further reduces local computation. We theoretically provide safe policy improvement performance guarantees. Extensive experiments show FORLER consistently outperforms strong baselines under varying data quality and heterogeneity.

摘要（中文）: 在物联网系统中，联邦学习通过无需共享原始数据即可进行并行策略训练，从而推动了在线强化学习（RL）的发展。然而，与真实环境进行在线交互可能具有风险且成本高昂，因此促使了离线联邦RL（FRL）的出现，其中本地设备从固定的数据集进行学习。尽管离线FRL前景广阔，但它可能会在低质量、异构数据的情况下失效。离线RL容易陷入局部最优，而在FRL中，一个设备的次优策略可能会降低聚合模型的性能，即策略污染。我们提出了FORLER，它将服务器上的Q-集成聚合与设备上的行动者修正相结合。服务器稳健地合并设备Q函数，以抑制策略污染，并将大量计算转移到资源受限的硬件之外，同时又不损害隐私。在本地，行动者修正通过对高Q动作的零阶搜索以及将策略推向这些动作的定制正则化器来丰富策略梯度。一个δ周期策略进一步减少了本地计算。我们在理论上提供了安全策略改进的性能保证。大量实验表明，FORLER在不同数据质量和异构性下始终优于强大的基线方法。

TLDR: This paper introduces FORLER, a federated offline reinforcement learning method that uses Q-ensemble aggregation on the server and actor rectification on devices to address the problem of policy pollution in heterogeneous data, with theoretical performance guarantees and strong empirical results.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了FORLER，一种联邦离线强化学习方法，它利用服务器上的Q-集成聚合和设备上的actor校正来解决异构数据中的策略污染问题，并具有理论性能保证和强大的实验结果。

Authors: Nan Qiao, Sheng Yue

Constrained Process Maps for Multi-Agent Generative AI Workflows

Abstract (English): Large language model (LLM)-based agents are increasingly used to perform complex, multi-step workflows in regulated settings such as compliance and due diligence. However, many agentic architectures rely primarily on prompt engineering of a single agent, making it difficult to observe or compare how models handle uncertainty and coordination across interconnected decision stages and with human oversight. We introduce a multi-agent system formalized as a finite-horizon Markov Decision Process (MDP) with a directed acyclic structure. Each agent corresponds to a specific role or decision stage (e.g., content, business, or legal review in a compliance workflow), with predefined transitions representing task escalation or completion. Epistemic uncertainty is quantified at the agent level using Monte Carlo estimation, while system-level uncertainty is captured by the MDP's termination in either an automated labeled state or a human-review state. We illustrate the approach through a case study in AI safety evaluation for self-harm detection, implemented as a multi-agent compliance system. Results demonstrate improvements over a single-agent baseline, including up to a 19\% increase in accuracy, up to an 85x reduction in required human review, and, in some configurations, reduced processing time.

摘要（中文）: 基于大型语言模型 (LLM) 的智能体越来越多地被用于在合规和尽职调查等受监管的环境中执行复杂的、多步骤的工作流程。然而，许多智能体架构主要依赖于单个智能体的提示工程，这使得观察或比较模型如何处理不确定性以及如何在相互关联的决策阶段之间以及在人工监督下进行协调变得困难。我们引入了一个多智能体系统，并将其形式化为一个具有有向无环结构的有限视界马尔可夫决策过程 (MDP)。每个智能体对应于一个特定的角色或决策阶段 (例如，合规工作流程中的内容、业务或法律审核)，具有预定义的转移，表示任务升级或完成。认知不确定性在智能体层面使用蒙特卡洛估计进行量化，而系统层面的不确定性则通过 MDP 在自动化标记状态或人工审核状态下的终止来捕获。我们通过一个针对自残检测的 AI 安全评估的案例研究来演示该方法，该案例研究被实施为一个多智能体合规系统。结果表明，与单智能体基线相比，性能有所提升，包括准确率提高高达 19%，所需人工审核次数减少高达 85 倍，并且在某些配置下，处理时间也缩短了。

TLDR: The paper introduces a multi-agent system formalized as an MDP for complex workflows in regulated settings, demonstrating improved accuracy and reduced human review in an AI safety evaluation case study compared to a single-agent baseline.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种多智能体系统，该系统被形式化为MDP，用于受监管环境中的复杂工作流程。通过AI安全评估案例研究表明，与单智能体基线相比，该系统提高了准确性，并减少了人工审查。

Authors: Ananya Joshi, Michael Rudow

Entropy-Guided Data-Efficient Training for Multimodal Reasoning Reward Models

Abstract (English): Multimodal reward models are crucial for aligning multimodal large language models with human preferences. Recent works have incorporated reasoning capabilities into these models, achieving promising results. However, training these models suffers from two critical challenges: (1) the inherent noise in preference datasets, which degrades model performance, and (2) the inefficiency of conventional training methods, which ignore the differences in sample difficulty. In this paper, we identify a strong correlation between response entropy and accuracy, indicating that entropy can serve as a reliable and unsupervised proxy for annotation noise and sample difficulty. Based on this insight, we propose a novel Entropy-Guided Training (EGT) approach for multimodal reasoning reward models, which combines two strategies: (1) entropy-guided data curation to mitigate the impact of unreliable samples, and (2) an entropy-guided training strategy that progressively introduces more complex examples. Extensive experiments across three benchmarks show that the EGT-trained model consistently outperforms state-of-the-art multimodal reward models.

摘要（中文）: 多模态奖励模型对于对齐多模态大型语言模型与人类偏好至关重要。最近的研究已经将推理能力融入到这些模型中，取得了可喜的成果。然而，训练这些模型面临着两个关键挑战：（1）偏好数据集中固有的噪声，这会降低模型性能；以及（2）传统训练方法的低效性，这些方法忽略了样本难度的差异。在本文中，我们发现响应熵和准确率之间存在很强的相关性，表明熵可以作为标注噪声和样本难度的可靠且无监督的代理。基于这一洞察，我们提出了一种新颖的熵引导训练（EGT）方法，用于多模态推理奖励模型，该方法结合了两种策略：（1）熵引导的数据清洗，以减轻不可靠样本的影响；以及（2）一种熵引导的训练策略，逐步引入更复杂的示例。在三个基准测试上的大量实验表明，EGT训练的模型始终优于最先进的多模态奖励模型。

TLDR: This paper introduces Entropy-Guided Training (EGT) to improve multimodal reasoning reward models by using entropy as a proxy for data noise and sample difficulty, leading to more data-efficient training and better performance.

简要说明: 该论文提出了一种熵引导训练(EGT)方法，通过使用熵作为数据噪声和样本难度的代理，改进多模态推理奖励模型，从而实现更高效的数据训练和更好的性能。

Authors: Shidong Yang, Tongwen Huang, Hao Wen, Yong Wang, Li Chen, Xiangxiang Chu

Synesthesia of Vehicles: Tactile Data Synthesis from Visual Inputs

Abstract (English): Autonomous vehicles (AVs) rely on multi-modal fusion for safety, but current visual and optical sensors fail to detect road-induced excitations which are critical for vehicles' dynamic control. Inspired by human synesthesia, we propose the Synesthesia of Vehicles (SoV), a novel framework to predict tactile excitations from visual inputs for autonomous vehicles. We develop a cross-modal spatiotemporal alignment method to address temporal and spatial disparities. Furthermore, a visual-tactile synesthetic (VTSyn) generative model using latent diffusion is proposed for unsupervised high-quality tactile data synthesis. A real-vehicle perception system collected a multi-modal dataset across diverse road and lighting conditions. Extensive experiments show that VTSyn outperforms existing models in temporal, frequency, and classification performance, enhancing AV safety through proactive tactile perception.

摘要（中文）: 自动驾驶汽车（AVs）的安全依赖于多模态融合，但目前的光学和视觉传感器无法检测路面引起的激励，而这些激励对于车辆的动态控制至关重要。受人类联觉的启发，我们提出车辆联觉（SoV），一种新颖的框架，旨在从视觉输入预测自动驾驶车辆的触觉激励。我们开发了一种跨模态时空对齐方法来解决时间和空间差异。此外，还提出了一种使用潜在扩散的视觉-触觉联觉（VTSyn）生成模型，用于无监督的高质量触觉数据合成。真实车辆感知系统收集了涵盖各种路面和光照条件的多模态数据集。大量实验表明，VTSyn在时间、频率和分类性能方面均优于现有模型，通过前瞻性的触觉感知增强了自动驾驶汽车的安全性。

TLDR: This paper introduces Synesthesia of Vehicles (SoV), a framework using latent diffusion to predict tactile excitations from visual inputs for autonomous vehicles, improving safety by proactively perceiving road conditions.

Authors: Rui Wang, Yaoguang Cao, Yuyi Chen, Jianyi Xu, Zhuoyang Li, Jiachen Shang, Shichun Yang

Beyond Dense States: Elevating Sparse Transcoders to Active Operators for Latent Reasoning

Abstract (English): Latent reasoning compresses the chain-of-thought (CoT) into continuous hidden states, yet existing methods rely on dense latent transitions that remain difficult to interpret and control. Meanwhile, sparse representation models uncover human-interpretable semantic features but remain largely confined to post-hoc analysis. We reconcile this tension by proposing LSTR (Latent Sparse Transcoder Reasoning), a latent reasoning framework that elevates functional sparse transcoders into active reasoning operators to perform multi-step computation through sparse semantic transitions. At its core, LSTR employs a Latent Transition Transcoder (LTT) with a residual skip architecture that decouples linear manifold transport from sparse semantic updates, enabling controllable semantic resolution via explicit sparsity constraints. Extensive experiments show that LSTR preserves reasoning accuracy and compression efficiency while substantially improving interpretability over dense latent baselines. Causal interventions and trajectory analyses further demonstrate that these sparse features act as both interpretable and causally effective operators in the reasoning process.

摘要（中文）: 潜在推理将思维链（CoT）压缩为连续的隐藏状态，但现有方法依赖于难以解释和控制的密集潜在转换。与此同时，稀疏表示模型揭示了人类可解释的语义特征，但主要局限于事后分析。我们通过提出LSTR（潜在稀疏转码器推理）来调和这种矛盾，LSTR是一种潜在推理框架，它将功能性稀疏转码器提升为主动推理算子，通过稀疏语义转换为执行多步骤计算。LSTR 的核心是采用具有残差跳跃结构的潜在转换转码器（LTT），它将线性流形传输与稀疏语义更新解耦，从而能够通过显式稀疏性约束实现可控的语义分辨率。大量实验表明，LSTR 在保持推理精度和压缩效率的同时，显著提高了对密集潜在基线的可解释性。因果干预和轨迹分析进一步表明，这些稀疏特征在推理过程中充当了可解释且具有因果效应的算子。

TLDR: This paper introduces LSTR, a latent reasoning framework using sparse transcoders as active reasoning operators, improving interpretability and control over dense latent state methods while maintaining accuracy and compression efficiency.

简要说明: 本文介绍了LSTR，一种使用稀疏转码器作为主动推理算子的潜在推理框架，在保持准确性和压缩效率的同时，提高了对密集潜在状态方法的可解释性和控制性。

Authors: Yadong Wang, Haodong Chen, Yu Tian, Chuanxing Geng, Dong Liang, Xiang Chen

FreshMem: Brain-Inspired Frequency-Space Hybrid Memory for Streaming Video Understanding

Abstract (English): Transitioning Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) from offline to online streaming video understanding is essential for continuous perception. However, existing methods lack flexible adaptivity, leading to irreversible detail loss and context fragmentation. To resolve this, we propose FreshMem, a Frequency-Space Hybrid Memory network inspired by the brain's logarithmic perception and memory consolidation. FreshMem reconciles short-term fidelity with long-term coherence through two synergistic modules: Multi-scale Frequency Memory (MFM), which projects overflowing frames into representative frequency coefficients, complemented by residual details to reconstruct a global historical "gist"; and Space Thumbnail Memory (STM), which discretizes the continuous stream into episodic clusters by employing an adaptive compression strategy to distill them into high-density space thumbnails. Extensive experiments show that FreshMem significantly boosts the Qwen2-VL baseline, yielding gains of 5.20%, 4.52%, and 2.34% on StreamingBench, OV-Bench, and OVO-Bench, respectively. As a training-free solution, FreshMem outperforms several fully fine-tuned methods, offering a highly efficient paradigm for long-horizon streaming video understanding.

摘要（中文）: 将多模态大型语言模型（MLLM）从离线过渡到在线流媒体视频理解对于持续感知至关重要。然而，现有方法缺乏灵活的适应性，导致不可逆转的细节丢失和上下文碎片化。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了FreshMem，一种受大脑对数感知和记忆巩固启发的频域-空间混合记忆网络。FreshMem通过两个协同模块协调短期保真度和长期连贯性：多尺度频率记忆（MFM），将溢出的帧投影到代表性的频率系数，并辅以残差细节以重建全局历史“梗概”；以及空间缩略图记忆（STM），通过采用自适应压缩策略将连续流离散化为情节集群，将其提炼成高密度空间缩略图。大量实验表明，FreshMem显著提升了Qwen2-VL基线，在StreamingBench、OV-Bench和OVO-Bench上分别取得了5.20%、4.52%和2.34%的增益。作为一个无需训练的解决方案，FreshMem优于几种完全微调的方法，为长时程流媒体视频理解提供了一种高效的范式。

TLDR: FreshMem is a novel, training-free memory architecture designed to enhance streaming video understanding in MLLMs by combining frequency and space-based memory representations, achieving significant performance gains over baselines.

简要说明: FreshMem 是一种新颖的、免训练的内存架构，旨在通过结合频率和空间内存表示来增强 MLLM 中的流视频理解，并且在基线上实现了显著的性能提升。

Authors: Kangcong Li, Peng Ye, Lin Zhang, Chao Wang, Huafeng Qin, Tao Chen

TABX: A High-Throughput Sandbox Battle Simulator for Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning

Abstract (English): The design of environments plays a critical role in shaping the development and evaluation of cooperative multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) algorithms. While existing benchmarks highlight critical challenges, they often lack the modularity required to design custom evaluation scenarios. We introduce the Totally Accelerated Battle Simulator in JAX (TABX), a high-throughput sandbox designed for reconfigurable multi-agent tasks. TABX provides granular control over environmental parameters, permitting a systematic investigation into emergent agent behaviors and algorithmic trade-offs across a diverse spectrum of task complexities. Leveraging JAX for hardware-accelerated execution on GPUs, TABX enables massive parallelization and significantly reduces computational overhead. By providing a fast, extensible, and easily customized framework, TABX facilitates the study of MARL agents in complex structured domains and serves as a scalable foundation for future research. Our code is available at: https://anonymous.4open.science/r/TABX-00CA.

摘要（中文）: 环境设计在塑造协作多智能体强化学习 (MARL) 算法的发展和评估中起着至关重要的作用。虽然现有的基准测试突出了关键挑战，但它们通常缺乏设计自定义评估场景所需的模块化。我们引入了基于 JAX 的完全加速战斗模拟器 (TABX)，这是一个为可重配置多智能体任务设计的高吞吐量沙盒。TABX 提供了对环境参数的精细控制，从而可以对各种任务复杂度下涌现的智能体行为和算法权衡进行系统研究。TABX 利用 JAX 在 GPU 上进行硬件加速执行，可实现大规模并行化并显著降低计算开销。通过提供一个快速、可扩展且易于定制的框架，TABX 促进了对 MARL 智能体在复杂结构化域中的研究，并为未来的研究提供了一个可扩展的基础。我们的代码可在以下网址获取：https://anonymous.4open.science/r/TABX-00CA。

Authors: Hayeong Lee, JunHyeok Oh, Byung-Jun Lee

SUSD: Structured Unsupervised Skill Discovery through State Factorization

Abstract (English): Unsupervised Skill Discovery (USD) aims to autonomously learn a diverse set of skills without relying on extrinsic rewards. One of the most common USD approaches is to maximize the Mutual Information (MI) between skill latent variables and states. However, MI-based methods tend to favor simple, static skills due to their invariance properties, limiting the discovery of dynamic, task-relevant behaviors. Distance-Maximizing Skill Discovery (DSD) promotes more dynamic skills by leveraging state-space distances, yet still fall short in encouraging comprehensive skill sets that engage all controllable factors or entities in the environment. In this work, we introduce SUSD, a novel framework that harnesses the compositional structure of environments by factorizing the state space into independent components (e.g., objects or controllable entities). SUSD allocates distinct skill variables to different factors, enabling more fine-grained control on the skill discovery process. A dynamic model also tracks learning across factors, adaptively steering the agent's focus toward underexplored factors. This structured approach not only promotes the discovery of richer and more diverse skills, but also yields a factorized skill representation that enables fine-grained and disentangled control over individual entities which facilitates efficient training of compositional downstream tasks via Hierarchical Reinforcement Learning (HRL). Our experimental results across three environments, with factors ranging from 1 to 10, demonstrate that our method can discover diverse and complex skills without supervision, significantly outperforming existing unsupervised skill discovery methods in factorized and complex environments. Code is publicly available at: https://github.com/hadi-hosseini/SUSD.

摘要（中文）: 无监督技能发现 (USD) 旨在自主学习一组多样化的技能，而无需依赖外部奖励。最常见的 USD 方法之一是最大化技能潜在变量和状态之间的互信息 (MI)。然而，基于 MI 的方法由于其不变性特性，往往偏好简单、静态的技能，从而限制了动态的、与任务相关的行为的发现。距离最大化技能发现 (DSD) 通过利用状态空间距离来促进更动态的技能，但在鼓励涵盖环境中所有可控因素或实体的综合技能集方面仍然不足。在这项工作中，我们引入了 SUSD，这是一个新颖的框架，通过将状态空间分解为独立的component（例如，对象或可控实体）来利用环境的组合结构。 SUSD 将不同的技能变量分配给不同的因素，从而能够对技能发现过程进行更细粒度的控制。一个动态模型也跟踪跨因素的学习情况，自适应地引导智能体的注意力集中到未充分探索的因素上。这种结构化的方法不仅促进了更丰富、更多样化技能的发现，而且还产生了一种分解的技能表示，从而可以对各个实体进行细粒度和解耦的控制，从而可以通过分层强化学习 (HRL) 有效地训练组合式下游任务。我们在三个环境（因素范围从 1 到 10）中的实验结果表明，我们的方法可以在没有监督的情况下发现多样化且复杂的技能，在分解和复杂的环境中显著优于现有的无监督技能发现方法。代码已在以下网址公开提供：https://github.com/hadi-hosseini/SUSD。

TLDR: The paper introduces SUSD, a novel unsupervised skill discovery framework that factorizes the state space to learn diverse and controllable skills, outperforming existing methods in environments with compositional structure. It enables fine-grained control and facilitates efficient hierarchical reinforcement learning.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种名为SUSD的新型无监督技能发现框架，它通过分解状态空间来学习多样化且可控的技能，在具有组合结构的环境中优于现有方法。它实现了细粒度控制，并促进了高效的分层强化学习。

Authors: Seyed Mohammad Hadi Hosseini, Mahdieh Soleymani Baghshah

Adaptive Rollout Allocation for Online Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards

Abstract (English): Sampling efficiency is a key bottleneck in reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards. Existing group-based policy optimization methods, such as GRPO, allocate a fixed number of rollouts for all training prompts. This uniform allocation implicitly treats all prompts as equally informative, and could lead to inefficient computational budget usage and impede training progress. We introduce VIP, a Variance-Informed Predictive allocation strategy that allocates a given rollout budget to the prompts in the incumbent batch to minimize the expected gradient variance of the policy update. At each iteration, VIP uses a lightweight Gaussian process model to predict per-prompt success probabilities based on recent rollouts. These probability predictions are translated into variance estimates, which are then fed into a convex optimization problem to determine the optimal rollout allocations under a hard compute budget constraint. Empirical results show that VIP consistently improves sampling efficiency and achieves higher performance than uniform or heuristic allocation strategies in multiple benchmarks.

摘要（中文）: 强化学习与可验证奖励中的采样效率是一个关键瓶颈。现有的基于群体的策略优化方法，例如GRPO，为所有训练提示分配固定数量的 rollout。这种均匀分配隐式地将所有提示视为具有相同的信息量，可能导致计算预算使用效率低下，并阻碍训练进度。我们提出了 VIP，一种方差知情的预测分配策略，它将给定的 rollout 预算分配给当前批次中的提示，以最小化策略更新的预期梯度方差。在每次迭代中，VIP 使用轻量级高斯过程模型，根据最近的 rollout 预测每个提示的成功概率。这些概率预测被转化为方差估计，然后被输入到一个凸优化问题中，以确定在严格的计算预算约束下的最优 rollout 分配。经验结果表明，在多个基准测试中，VIP 始终能提高采样效率，并实现优于均匀或启发式分配策略的更高性能。

TLDR: This paper introduces VIP, a variance-informed rollout allocation strategy for reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards, improving sampling efficiency by intelligently allocating rollouts based on predicted success probabilities. It outperforms uniform and heuristic allocation methods.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种名为VIP的方差感知 rollout 分配策略，用于具有可验证奖励的强化学习，通过基于预测的成功概率智能地分配rollout来提高采样效率。该方法优于均匀分配和启发式分配方法。

Authors: Hieu Trung Nguyen, Bao Nguyen, Wenao Ma, Yuzhi Zhao, Ruifeng She, Viet Anh Nguyen

The Multiple Ticket Hypothesis: Random Sparse Subnetworks Suffice for RLVR

Abstract (English): The Lottery Ticket Hypothesis demonstrated that sparse subnetworks can match full-model performance, suggesting parameter redundancy. Meanwhile, in Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR), recent work has shown that updates concentrate on a sparse subset of parameters, which further lends evidence to this underlying redundancy. We study the simplest possible way to exploit this redundancy: training only a randomly selected subset of parameters at extreme sparsities. Empirically, we find that training just 1\% of parameters matches or exceeds full-parameter RLVR finetuning across 3 models and 2 task domains. Moreover, different random masks show minimal overlap ($\leq 0.005$ Jaccard similarity) and yet all succeed, suggesting pretrained models contain many viable sparse subnetworks rather than one privileged set. We term this the Multiple Ticket Hypothesis. We explain this phenomenon through the implicit per-step KL constraint in RLVR, which restricts updates to a low-dimensional subspace, enabling arbitrary sparse masks to succeed.

摘要（中文）: 彩票假设证明了稀疏子网络可以媲美完整模型性能，暗示了参数冗余。同时，在可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）中，最近的研究表明更新集中在参数的一个稀疏子集上，进一步佐证了这种潜在的冗余性。我们研究了利用这种冗余性的最简单可能的方式：以极端的稀疏度仅训练随机选择的参数子集。实验结果表明，仅训练1%的参数在3个模型和2个任务领域中，就能够达到或超过完整参数RLVR微调的性能。此外，不同的随机掩码显示出极小的重叠（杰卡德相似度$\leq 0.005$），但都成功了，这表明预训练模型包含许多可行的稀疏子网络，而不是一个特权集合。我们称之为多重彩票假设。我们通过RLVR中隐式的每步KL散度约束来解释这种现象，该约束将更新限制在一个低维子空间内，从而使任意稀疏掩码都能成功。

TLDR: This paper introduces the 'Multiple Ticket Hypothesis' for Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR), showing that numerous random sparse subnetworks (e.g., 1% of parameters) can achieve full-parameter performance, suggesting redundancy in pretrained models.

简要说明: 本文提出了针对可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）的“多重彩票假说”，表明许多随机稀疏子网络（例如，1%的参数）能够实现全参数模型的性能，暗示了预训练模型中的冗余。

Authors: Israel Adewuyi, Solomon Okibe, Vladmir Ivanov

Making Avatars Interact: Towards Text-Driven Human-Object Interaction for Controllable Talking Avatars

Abstract (English): Generating talking avatars is a fundamental task in video generation. Although existing methods can generate full-body talking avatars with simple human motion, extending this task to grounded human-object interaction (GHOI) remains an open challenge, requiring the avatar to perform text-aligned interactions with surrounding objects. This challenge stems from the need for environmental perception and the control-quality dilemma in GHOI generation. To address this, we propose a novel dual-stream framework, InteractAvatar, which decouples perception and planning from video synthesis for grounded human-object interaction. Leveraging detection to enhance environmental perception, we introduce a Perception and Interaction Module (PIM) to generate text-aligned interaction motions. Additionally, an Audio-Interaction Aware Generation Module (AIM) is proposed to synthesize vivid talking avatars performing object interactions. With a specially designed motion-to-video aligner, PIM and AIM share a similar network structure and enable parallel co-generation of motions and plausible videos, effectively mitigating the control-quality dilemma. Finally, we establish a benchmark, GroundedInter, for evaluating GHOI video generation. Extensive experiments and comparisons demonstrate the effectiveness of our method in generating grounded human-object interactions for talking avatars. Project page: https://interactavatar.github.io

摘要（中文）: 生成会说话的头像 (talking avatars) 是视频生成中的一项基本任务。 尽管现有方法可以生成具有简单人体动作的全身会说话头像，但将此任务扩展到基于环境的人与物体交互 (GHOI) 仍然是一个开放的挑战，这要求头像执行与周围物体文本对齐的交互。 这一挑战源于对环境感知的需求以及 GHOI 生成中的控制质量困境。 为了解决这个问题，我们提出了一种新颖的双流框架 InteractAvatar，它将感知和规划与视频合成分离，以实现基于环境的人与物体交互。 利用检测来增强环境感知，我们引入了一个感知与交互模块 (PIM) 来生成文本对齐的交互动作。 此外，还提出了一个感知音频-交互生成模块 (AIM) 来合成执行物体交互的生动会说话头像。 通过专门设计的运动到视频对齐器，PIM 和 AIM 共享相似的网络结构，并能够并行协同生成运动和合理的视频，从而有效地缓解了控制质量困境。 最后，我们建立了一个基准测试 GroundedInter，用于评估 GHOI 视频生成。 大量的实验和比较表明了我们的方法在为会说话头像生成基于环境的人与物体交互方面的有效性。 项目主页：https://interactavatar.github.io

Authors: Youliang Zhang, Zhengguang Zhou, Zhentao Yu, Ziyao Huang, Teng Hu, Sen Liang, Guozhen Zhang, Ziqiao Peng, Shunkai Li, Yi Chen, Zixiang Zhou, Yuan Zhou, Qinglin Lu, Xiu Li

Cross-Paradigm Evaluation of Gaze-Based Semantic Object Identification for Intelligent Vehicles

Abstract (English): Understanding where drivers direct their visual attention during driving, as characterized by gaze behavior, is critical for developing next-generation advanced driver-assistance systems and improving road safety. This paper tackles this challenge as a semantic identification task from the road scenes captured by a vehicle's front-view camera. Specifically, the collocation of gaze points with object semantics is investigated using three distinct vision-based approaches: direct object detection (YOLOv13), segmentation-assisted classification (SAM2 paired with EfficientNetV2 versus YOLOv13), and query-based Vision-Language Models, VLMs (Qwen2.5-VL-7b versus Qwen2.5-VL-32b). The results demonstrate that the direct object detection (YOLOv13) and Qwen2.5-VL-32b significantly outperform other approaches, achieving Macro F1-Scores over 0.84. The large VLM (Qwen2.5-VL-32b), in particular, exhibited superior robustness and performance for identifying small, safety-critical objects such as traffic lights, especially in adverse nighttime conditions. Conversely, the segmentation-assisted paradigm suffers from a "part-versus-whole" semantic gap that led to large failure in recall. The results reveal a fundamental trade-off between the real-time efficiency of traditional detectors and the richer contextual understanding and robustness offered by large VLMs. These findings provide critical insights and practical guidance for the design of future human-aware intelligent driver monitoring systems.

摘要（中文）: 理解驾驶员在驾驶过程中视觉注意力集中的位置（以注视行为为特征），对于开发下一代高级驾驶辅助系统和提高道路安全至关重要。本文将此挑战视为一项语义识别任务，目标是从车辆前视摄像头捕捉到的道路场景中进行识别。具体而言，本文使用三种不同的基于视觉的方法研究了注视点与对象语义的搭配关系：直接对象检测 (YOLOv13)、分割辅助分类（SAM2 搭配 EfficientNetV2 与 YOLOv13）以及基于查询的视觉-语言模型（VLMs）（Qwen2.5-VL-7b 与 Qwen2.5-VL-32b）。结果表明，直接对象检测 (YOLOv13) 和 Qwen2.5-VL-32b 明显优于其他方法，实现了超过 0.84 的宏平均F1分数。特别是，大型VLM（Qwen2.5-VL-32b）在识别小型、安全关键对象（如交通信号灯），尤其是在不利的夜间条件下，表现出卓越的鲁棒性和性能。相反，分割辅助范式受到“部分与整体”语义鸿沟的影响，导致召回率的大幅下降。结果揭示了传统检测器的实时效率与大型VLM提供的更丰富的上下文理解和鲁棒性之间的根本权衡。这些发现为未来以人为本的智能驾驶员监控系统的设计提供了关键的见解和实践指导。

Authors: Penghao Deng, Jidong J. Yang, Jiachen Bian

Enhancing Indoor Occupancy Prediction via Sparse Query-Based Multi-Level Consistent Knowledge Distillation

Abstract (English): Occupancy prediction provides critical geometric and semantic understanding for robotics but faces efficiency-accuracy trade-offs. Current dense methods suffer computational waste on empty voxels, while sparse query-based approaches lack robustness in diverse and complex indoor scenes. In this paper, we propose DiScene, a novel sparse query-based framework that leverages multi-level distillation to achieve efficient and robust occupancy prediction. In particular, our method incorporates two key innovations: (1) a Multi-level Consistent Knowledge Distillation strategy, which transfers hierarchical representations from large teacher models to lightweight students through coordinated alignment across four levels, including encoder-level feature alignment, query-level feature matching, prior-level spatial guidance, and anchor-level high-confidence knowledge transfer and (2) a Teacher-Guided Initialization policy, employing optimized parameter warm-up to accelerate model convergence. Validated on the Occ-Scannet benchmark, DiScene achieves 23.2 FPS without depth priors while outperforming our baseline method, OPUS, by 36.1% and even better than the depth-enhanced version, OPUS†. With depth integration, DiScene† attains new SOTA performance, surpassing EmbodiedOcc by 3.7% with 1.62$\times$ faster inference speed. Furthermore, experiments on the Occ3D-nuScenes benchmark and in-the-wild scenarios demonstrate the versatility of our approach in various environments. Code and models can be accessed at https://github.com/getterupper/DiScene.

摘要（中文）: 占用预测为机器人技术提供了关键的几何和语义理解，但面临着效率与准确性的权衡。当前的密集方法在空体素上存在计算浪费，而稀疏的基于查询的方法在多样和复杂的室内场景中缺乏鲁棒性。在本文中，我们提出了一种新颖的基于稀疏查询的框架DiScene，该框架利用多层蒸馏来实现高效且鲁棒的占用预测。具体而言，我们的方法包含两个关键创新：（1）一种多层一致性知识蒸馏策略，该策略通过在四个层级上的协同对齐，将来自大型教师模型的层级表示传递到轻量级学生模型，包括编码器层级的特征对齐、查询层级的特征匹配、先验层级的空间引导和锚点的置信度高的知识迁移；（2）一种教师引导的初始化策略，采用优化的参数预热来加速模型收敛。在Occ-Scannet基准上的验证表明，DiScene在没有深度先验的情况下实现了23.2 FPS，同时性能优于我们的基线方法OPUS 36.1%，甚至优于深度增强版本OPUS†。通过深度融合，DiScene†获得了新的SOTA性能，超越EmbodiedOcc 3.7%，且推理速度快1.62倍。此外，在Occ3D-nuScenes基准测试和真实场景中的实验证明了我们方法在各种环境中的通用性。代码和模型可在https://github.com/getterupper/DiScene访问。

TLDR: The paper introduces DiScene, a sparse query-based occupancy prediction framework utilizing multi-level knowledge distillation and teacher-guided initialization, achieving state-of-the-art performance and higher efficiency on occupancy prediction benchmarks.

Authors: Xiang Li, Yupeng Zheng, Pengfei Li, Yilun Chen, Ya-Qin Zhang, Wenchao Ding

Segment to Focus: Guiding Latent Action Models in the Presence of Distractors

Abstract (English): Latent Action Models (LAMs) learn to extract action-relevant representations solely from raw observations, enabling reinforcement learning from unlabelled videos and significantly scaling available training data. However, LAMs face a critical challenge in disentangling action-relevant features from action-correlated noise (e.g., background motion). Failing to filter these distractors causes LAMs to capture spurious correlations and build sub-optimal latent action spaces. In this paper, we introduce MaskLAM -- a lightweight modification to LAM training to mitigate this issue by incorporating visual agent segmentation. MaskLAM utilises segmentation masks from pretrained foundation models to weight the LAM reconstruction loss, thereby prioritising salient information over background elements while requiring no architectural modifications. We demonstrate the effectiveness of our method on continuous-control MuJoCo tasks, modified with action-correlated background noise. Our approach yields up to a 4x increase in accrued rewards compared to standard baselines and a 3x improvement in the latent action quality, as evidenced by linear probe evaluation.

摘要（中文）: 潜在动作模型(LAMs)学会仅从原始观测中提取与动作相关的表征，从而实现从未标记视频中的强化学习，并显著扩展可用的训练数据。然而，LAMs面临着一个关键挑战：将与动作相关的特征从与动作相关的噪声（例如，背景运动）中解耦。无法过滤这些干扰因素会导致LAMs捕获虚假相关性并构建次优的潜在动作空间。在本文中，我们提出MaskLAM——一种针对LAM训练的轻量级修改，通过纳入视觉agent分割来缓解此问题。MaskLAM利用来自预训练基础模型的分割掩码来加权LAM重建损失，从而在无需架构修改的情况下优先考虑显著信息而非背景元素。我们证明了我们的方法在连续控制的MuJoCo任务上的有效性，这些任务被加入了与动作相关的背景噪声。与标准基线相比，我们的方法产生了高达4倍的累积奖励增益，以及3倍的潜在动作质量提升，如线性探针评估所证明。

TLDR: The paper introduces MaskLAM, a modification to Latent Action Models that uses agent segmentation masks to prioritize action-relevant features and filter out background noise, leading to improved performance on continuous control tasks with distractors.

Authors: Hamza Adnan, Matthew T. Jackson, Alexey Zakharov

CIEC: Coupling Implicit and Explicit Cues for Multimodal Weakly Supervised Manipulation Localization

Abstract (English): To mitigate the threat of misinformation, multimodal manipulation localization has garnered growing attention. Consider that current methods rely on costly and time-consuming fine-grained annotations, such as patch/token-level annotations. This paper proposes a novel framework named Coupling Implicit and Explicit Cues (CIEC), which aims to achieve multimodal weakly-supervised manipulation localization for image-text pairs utilizing only coarse-grained image/sentence-level annotations. It comprises two branches, image-based and text-based weakly-supervised localization. For the former, we devise the Textual-guidance Refine Patch Selection (TRPS) module. It integrates forgery cues from both visual and textual perspectives to lock onto suspicious regions aided by spatial priors. Followed by the background silencing and spatial contrast constraints to suppress interference from irrelevant areas. For the latter, we devise the Visual-deviation Calibrated Token Grounding (VCTG) module. It focuses on meaningful content words and leverages relative visual bias to assist token localization. Followed by the asymmetric sparse and semantic consistency constraints to mitigate label noise and ensure reliability. Extensive experiments demonstrate the effectiveness of our CIEC, yielding results comparable to fully supervised methods on several evaluation metrics.

摘要（中文）: 为应对虚假信息的威胁，多模态篡改定位受到越来越多的关注。然而，当前方法依赖于代价高昂且耗时的细粒度标注，例如图像块/令牌级别的标注。本文提出了一种名为耦合隐式和显式线索（CIEC）的新型框架，旨在仅利用粗粒度的图像/句子级别标注，实现图像-文本对的多模态弱监督篡改定位。该框架包含两个分支：基于图像和基于文本的弱监督定位。对于前者，我们设计了文本引导的精细化图像块选择（TRPS）模块。它整合了来自视觉和文本视角的伪造线索，并在空间先验的辅助下锁定可疑区域。随后，通过背景抑制和空间对比度约束来抑制来自无关区域的干扰。对于后者，我们设计了视觉偏差校准的令牌定位（VCTG）模块。它关注有意义的内容词，并利用相对视觉偏差来辅助令牌定位。随后，通过非对称稀疏性和语义一致性约束来减轻标签噪声并确保可靠性。 广泛的实验表明了我们CIEC的有效性，在多个评估指标上取得了与完全监督方法相当的结果。

TLDR: The paper introduces CIEC, a novel weakly-supervised multimodal manipulation localization framework for image-text pairs using only coarse-grained annotations. It achieves comparable performance to fully supervised methods.

简要说明: 该论文提出了CIEC，一种新颖的弱监督多模态操纵定位框架，仅使用粗粒度标注来处理图像-文本对。它实现了与完全监督方法相当的性能。

Efficient Cross-Country Data Acquisition Strategy for ADAS via Street-View Imagery

Abstract (English): Deploying ADAS and ADS across countries remains challenging due to differences in legislation, traffic infrastructure, and visual conventions, which introduce domain shifts that degrade perception performance. Traditional cross-country data collection relies on extensive on-road driving, making it costly and inefficient to identify representative locations. To address this, we propose a street-view-guided data acquisition strategy that leverages publicly available imagery to identify places of interest (POI). Two POI scoring methods are introduced: a KNN-based feature distance approach using a vision foundation model, and a visual-attribution approach using a vision-language model. To enable repeatable evaluation, we adopt a collect-detect protocol and construct a co-located dataset by pairing the Zenseact Open Dataset with Mapillary street-view images. Experiments on traffic sign detection, a task particularly sensitive to cross-country variations in sign appearance, show that our approach achieves performance comparable to random sampling while using only half of the target-domain data. We further provide cost estimations for full-country analysis, demonstrating that large-scale street-view processing remains economically feasible. These results highlight the potential of street-view-guided data acquisition for efficient and cost-effective cross-country model adaptation.

摘要（中文）: 由于各国在法规、交通基础设施和视觉习惯方面的差异，跨国部署ADAS和ADS仍然面临挑战，这些差异引入的领域偏移会降低感知性能。传统的跨国数据采集依赖于大量的道路驾驶，使得识别具有代表性的地点既昂贵又低效。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了一种街景引导的数据获取策略，该策略利用公开可用的图像来识别感兴趣的地点（POI）。我们引入了两种POI评分方法：一种是基于视觉基础模型的使用KNN的特征距离方法，另一种是使用视觉-语言模型的视觉归因方法。为了实现可重复的评估，我们采用了一种收集-检测协议，并通过将Zenseact开放数据集与Mapillary街景图像配对，构建了一个共址数据集。在交通标志检测（一项对交通标志外观的跨国差异特别敏感的任务）上的实验表明，我们的方法在仅使用一半目标域数据的情况下，实现了与随机采样相当的性能。我们进一步提供了针对全国范围分析的成本估算，表明大规模街景处理在经济上仍然可行。这些结果突出了街景引导的数据获取在高效且经济的跨国模型适配方面的潜力。

Authors: Yin Wu, Daniel Slieter, Carl Esselborn, Ahmed Abouelazm, Tsung Yuan Tseng, J. Marius Zöllner

MagicFuse: Single Image Fusion for Visual and Semantic Reinforcement

Abstract (English): This paper focuses on a highly practical scenario: how to continue benefiting from the advantages of multi-modal image fusion under harsh conditions when only visible imaging sensors are available. To achieve this goal, we propose a novel concept of single-image fusion, which extends conventional data-level fusion to the knowledge level. Specifically, we develop MagicFuse, a novel single image fusion framework capable of deriving a comprehensive cross-spectral scene representation from a single low-quality visible image. MagicFuse first introduces an intra-spectral knowledge reinforcement branch and a cross-spectral knowledge generation branch based on the diffusion models. They mine scene information obscured in the visible spectrum and learn thermal radiation distribution patterns transferred to the infrared spectrum, respectively. Building on them, we design a multi-domain knowledge fusion branch that integrates the probabilistic noise from the diffusion streams of these two branches, from which a cross-spectral scene representation can be obtained through successive sampling. Then, we impose both visual and semantic constraints to ensure that this scene representation can satisfy human observation while supporting downstream semantic decision-making. Extensive experiments show that our MagicFuse achieves visual and semantic representation performance comparable to or even better than state-of-the-art fusion methods with multi-modal inputs, despite relying solely on a single degraded visible image.

摘要（中文）: 本文关注一个极具实用性的场景：当仅有可见光成像传感器可用时，如何在恶劣条件下继续受益于多模态图像融合的优势。为实现这一目标，我们提出一种新颖的单图像融合概念，将传统数据级融合扩展到知识层面。具体而言，我们开发了MagicFuse，这是一个新颖的单图像融合框架，能够从单一低质量可见光图像中推导出全面的跨光谱场景表征。MagicFuse首先引入了基于扩散模型的同光谱知识强化分支和跨光谱知识生成分支。它们分别挖掘可见光谱中隐藏的场景信息，并学习传递到红外光谱的热辐射分布模式。在此基础上，我们设计了一个多域知识融合分支，该分支集成了这两个分支扩散流中的概率噪声，从中可以通过连续采样获得跨光谱场景表征。然后，我们施加视觉和语义约束，以确保该场景表征既能满足人类观察，又能支持下游语义决策。大量实验表明，尽管仅依赖于单一降质的可见光图像，但我们的MagicFuse在视觉和语义表征性能上，达到了甚至优于最先进的具有多模态输入融合方法的效果。

TLDR: The paper introduces MagicFuse, a single-image fusion framework that generates cross-spectral scene representations from a single, low-quality visible image, using diffusion models and knowledge reinforcement to match or exceed multi-modal fusion performance.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种名为 MagicFuse 的单图像融合框架，它仅使用单个低质量可见图像生成跨光谱场景表示，通过扩散模型和知识增强，达到甚至超过多模态融合的性能。

Authors: Hao Zhang, Yanping Zha, Zizhuo Li, Meiqi Gong, Jiayi Ma

FastPhysGS: Accelerating Physics-based Dynamic 3DGS Simulation via Interior Completion and Adaptive Optimization

Abstract (English): Extending 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) to 4D physical simulation remains challenging. Based on the Material Point Method (MPM), existing methods either rely on manual parameter tuning or distill dynamics from video diffusion models, limiting the generalization and optimization efficiency. Recent attempts using LLMs/VLMs suffer from a text/image-to-3D perceptual gap, yielding unstable physics behavior. In addition, they often ignore the surface structure of 3DGS, leading to implausible motion. We propose FastPhysGS, a fast and robust framework for physics-based dynamic 3DGS simulation:(1) Instance-aware Particle Filling (IPF) with Monte Carlo Importance Sampling (MCIS) to efficiently populate interior particles while preserving geometric fidelity; (2) Bidirectional Graph Decoupling Optimization (BGDO), an adaptive strategy that rapidly optimizes material parameters predicted from a VLM. Experiments show FastPhysGS achieves high-fidelity physical simulation in 1 minute using only 7 GB runtime memory, outperforming prior works with broad potential applications.

摘要（中文）: 将3D高斯溅射(3DGS)扩展到4D物理模拟仍然具有挑战性。基于物质点方法(MPM)，现有方法要么依赖于手动参数调整，要么从视频扩散模型中提取动力学，从而限制了泛化能力和优化效率。最近使用LLM/VLM的尝试存在文本/图像到3D的感知差距，导致不稳定的物理行为。此外，它们常常忽略3DGS的表面结构，导致不合理的运动。我们提出了FastPhysGS，一个快速而稳健的基于物理的动态3DGS模拟框架：(1) 采用蒙特卡洛重要性采样(MCIS)的实例感知粒子填充(IPF)技术，以有效地填充内部粒子，同时保持几何逼真度；(2) 双向图解耦优化(BGDO)，一种自适应策略，可快速优化从VLM预测的材料参数。实验表明，FastPhysGS仅使用7GB运行内存在1分钟内即可实现高保真物理模拟，优于现有工作，具有广泛的潜在应用。

TLDR: FastPhysGS enables fast physics-based dynamic 3D Gaussian splatting simulation by efficiently populating interior particles and adaptively optimizing material parameters predicted from a VLM.

简要说明: FastPhysGS通过有效地填充内部粒子和自适应地优化来自VLM的材料参数预测，实现了快速的基于物理的动态3D高斯溅射模拟。

Authors: Yikun Ma, Yiqing Li, Jingwen Ye, Zhongkai Wu, Weidong Zhang, Lin Gao, Zhi Jin

SMTrack: State-Aware Mamba for Efficient Temporal Modeling in Visual Tracking

Abstract (English): Visual tracking aims to automatically estimate the state of a target object in a video sequence, which is challenging especially in dynamic scenarios. Thus, numerous methods are proposed to introduce temporal cues to enhance tracking robustness. However, conventional CNN and Transformer architectures exhibit inherent limitations in modeling long-range temporal dependencies in visual tracking, often necessitating either complex customized modules or substantial computational costs to integrate temporal cues. Inspired by the success of the state space model, we propose a novel temporal modeling paradigm for visual tracking, termed State-aware Mamba Tracker (SMTrack), providing a neat pipeline for training and tracking without needing customized modules or substantial computational costs to build long-range temporal dependencies. It enjoys several merits. First, we propose a novel selective state-aware space model with state-wise parameters to capture more diverse temporal cues for robust tracking. Second, SMTrack facilitates long-range temporal interactions with linear computational complexity during training. Third, SMTrack enables each frame to interact with previously tracked frames via hidden state propagation and updating, which releases computational costs of handling temporal cues during tracking. Extensive experimental results demonstrate that SMTrack achieves promising performance with low computational costs.

摘要（中文）: 视觉跟踪旨在自动估计视频序列中目标对象的状态，尤其在动态场景中极具挑战性。 因此，人们提出了许多方法来引入时间线索以增强跟踪的鲁棒性。 然而，传统的 CNN 和 Transformer 架构在视觉跟踪中建模远距离时间依赖性方面表现出内在的局限性，通常需要复杂的定制模块或大量的计算成本来整合时间线索。 受状态空间模型成功的启发，我们提出了一种用于视觉跟踪的新型时间建模范式，称为状态感知 Mamba 跟踪器 (SMTrack)，它提供了一个简洁的训练和跟踪流程，无需定制模块或大量的计算成本来构建远距离时间依赖性。 它具有以下优点。 首先，我们提出了一种新型的选择性状态感知空间模型，该模型具有状态相关的参数，用于捕获更多样化的时间线索以实现鲁棒跟踪。 其次，SMTrack 在训练期间以线性计算复杂度促进远距离时间交互。 第三，SMTrack 允许每一帧通过隐藏状态的传播和更新与先前跟踪的帧进行交互，从而释放了在跟踪期间处理时间线索的计算成本。 广泛的实验结果表明，SMTrack 以较低的计算成本实现了令人满意的性能。

TLDR: The paper introduces SMTrack, a visual tracking method using a state-aware Mamba architecture for efficient long-range temporal modeling, achieving promising performance with low computational costs.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种名为SMTrack的视觉跟踪方法，它使用状态感知的Mamba架构来进行高效的远距离时序建模，并在低计算成本下实现了良好的性能。

Authors: Yinchao Ma, Dengqing Yang, Zhangyu He, Wenfei Yang, Tianzhu Zhang

UV-M3TL: A Unified and Versatile Multimodal Multi-Task Learning Framework for Assistive Driving Perception

Abstract (English): Advanced Driver Assistance Systems (ADAS) need to understand human driver behavior while perceiving their navigation context, but jointly learning these heterogeneous tasks would cause inter-task negative transfer and impair system performance. Here, we propose a Unified and Versatile Multimodal Multi-Task Learning (UV-M3TL) framework to simultaneously recognize driver behavior, driver emotion, vehicle behavior, and traffic context, while mitigating inter-task negative transfer. Our framework incorporates two core components: dual-branch spatial channel multimodal embedding (DB-SCME) and adaptive feature-decoupled multi-task loss (AFD-Loss). DB-SCME enhances cross-task knowledge transfer while mitigating task conflicts by employing a dual-branch structure to explicitly model salient task-shared and task-specific features. AFD-Loss improves the stability of joint optimization while guiding the model to learn diverse multi-task representations by introducing an adaptive weighting mechanism based on learning dynamics and feature decoupling constraints. We evaluate our method on the AIDE dataset, and the experimental results demonstrate that UV-M3TL achieves state-of-the-art performance across all four tasks. To further prove the versatility, we evaluate UV-M3TL on additional public multi-task perception benchmarks (BDD100K, CityScapes, NYUD-v2, and PASCAL-Context), where it consistently delivers strong performance across diverse task combinations, attaining state-of-the-art results on most tasks.

摘要（中文）: 高级驾驶辅助系统 (ADAS) 需要在感知导航环境的同时理解人类驾驶员的行为，但联合学习这些异构任务会导致任务间负迁移，并损害系统性能。在此，我们提出了一种统一且通用的多模态多任务学习 (UV-M3TL) 框架，以同时识别驾驶员行为、驾驶员情绪、车辆行为和交通环境，同时减轻任务间负迁移。我们的框架包含两个核心组件：双分支空间通道多模态嵌入 (DB-SCME) 和自适应特征解耦多任务损失 (AFD-Loss)。DB-SCME 通过采用双分支结构显式地建模显著的任务共享和任务特定特征，从而增强跨任务知识迁移，同时减轻任务冲突。AFD-Loss 通过引入基于学习动态和特征解耦约束的自适应加权机制，提高了联合优化的稳定性，同时引导模型学习多样化的多任务表示。我们在 AIDE 数据集上评估了我们的方法，实验结果表明 UV-M3TL 在所有四个任务上都实现了最先进的性能。为了进一步证明其通用性，我们在其他公开的多任务感知基准数据集（BDD100K、CityScapes、NYUD-v2 和 PASCAL-Context）上评估了 UV-M3TL，它在不同的任务组合中始终表现出强大的性能，并在大多数任务上取得了最先进的结果。

TLDR: The paper proposes a Unified and Versatile Multimodal Multi-Task Learning (UV-M3TL) framework for assistive driving perception, achieving SOTA performance on multiple tasks and datasets by mitigating negative transfer between them.

Authors: Wenzhuo Liu, Qiannan Guo, Zhen Wang, Wenshuo Wang, Lei Yang, Yicheng Qiao, Lening Wang, Zhiwei Li, Chen Lv, Shanghang Zhang, Junqiang Xi, Huaping Liu

Split&Splat: Zero-Shot Panoptic Segmentation via Explicit Instance Modeling and 3D Gaussian Splatting

Abstract (English): 3D Gaussian Splatting (GS) enables fast and high-quality scene reconstruction, but it lacks an object-consistent and semantically aware structure. We propose Split&Splat, a framework for panoptic scene reconstruction using 3DGS. Our approach explicitly models object instances. It first propagates instance masks across views using depth, thus producing view-consistent 2D masks. Each object is then reconstructed independently and merged back into the scene while refining its boundaries. Finally, instance-level semantic descriptors are embedded in the reconstructed objects, supporting various applications, including panoptic segmentation, object retrieval, and 3D editing. Unlike existing methods, Split&Splat tackles the problem by first segmenting the scene and then reconstructing each object individually. This design naturally supports downstream tasks and allows Split&Splat to achieve state-of-the-art performance on the ScanNetv2 segmentation benchmark.

摘要（中文）: 3D高斯溅射（GS）能够实现快速且高质量的场景重建，但缺乏对象一致和语义感知的结构。我们提出了Split&Splat，一个使用3DGS进行全景场景重建的框架。我们的方法显式地建模对象实例。它首先使用深度传播跨视图的实例掩码，从而产生视图一致的2D掩码。然后，每个对象被独立重建并合并回场景中，同时细化其边界。最后，实例级别的语义描述符被嵌入到重建的对象中，支持各种应用，包括全景分割、对象检索和3D编辑。与现有方法不同，Split&Splat通过首先分割场景，然后单独重建每个对象来解决问题。这种设计自然地支持下游任务，并使Split&Splat能够在ScanNetv2分割基准上实现最先进的性能。

TLDR: The paper introduces Split&Splat, a novel panoptic scene reconstruction framework using 3D Gaussian Splatting that explicitly models object instances by segmenting the scene first and then reconstructing each object individually, achieving state-of-the-art results on ScanNetv2.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了Split&Splat，一种新颖的基于3D高斯溅射的全景场景重建框架，通过先分割场景然后单独重建每个对象来显式地对对象实例进行建模，并在ScanNetv2上取得了最先进的结果。

Authors: Leonardo Monchieri, Elena Camuffo, Francesco Barbato, Pietro Zanuttigh, Simone Milani

Learning Markov Decision Processes under Fully Bandit Feedback

Abstract (English): A standard assumption in Reinforcement Learning is that the agent observes every visited state-action pair in the associated Markov Decision Process (MDP), along with the per-step rewards. Strong theoretical results are known in this setting, achieving nearly-tight $Θ(\sqrt{T})$-regret bounds. However, such detailed feedback can be unrealistic, and recent research has investigated more restricted settings such as trajectory feedback, where the agent observes all the visited state-action pairs, but only a single \emph{aggregate} reward. In this paper, we consider a far more restrictive ``fully bandit'' feedback model for episodic MDPs, where the agent does not even observe the visited state-action pairs -- it only learns the aggregate reward. We provide the first efficient bandit learning algorithm for episodic MDPs with $\widetilde{O}(\sqrt{T})$ regret. Our regret has an exponential dependence on the horizon length $\H$, which we show is necessary. We also obtain improved nearly-tight regret bounds for ``ordered'' MDPs; these can be used to model classical stochastic optimization problems such as $k$-item prophet inequality and sequential posted pricing. Finally, we evaluate the empirical performance of our algorithm for the setting of $k$-item prophet inequalities; despite the highly restricted feedback, our algorithm's performance is comparable to that of a state-of-art learning algorithm (UCB-VI) with detailed state-action feedback.

摘要（中文）: 强化学习中的一个标准假设是，智能体能够观察到相关马尔可夫决策过程（MDP）中每一个被访问过的状态-动作对，以及每一步的奖励。在这种设定下，已经存在强大的理论结果，获得了几乎紧凑的$Θ(\sqrt{T})$-遗憾界。然而，这种详细的反馈可能是不现实的，最近的研究已经开始探索更受限制的设定，例如轨迹反馈，其中智能体能够观察到所有被访问过的状态-动作对，但仅能获得一个\emph{聚合}奖励。在本文中，我们考虑一个更加严格的“完全bandit”反馈模型用于情景MDP，其中智能体甚至无法观察到被访问过的状态-动作对——它只能学习到聚合奖励。我们为情景MDP提供了第一个高效的bandit学习算法，其遗憾为$\widetilde{O}(\sqrt{T})$。我们的遗憾界对期长度$\H$呈指数依赖关系，我们证明这是必要的。我们还获得了“有序”MDP的改进的近乎紧凑的遗憾界；这些可以用来建模经典的随机优化问题，例如$k$项预言家不等式和连续发布定价。最后，我们评估了我们的算法在$k$项预言家不等式设定下的经验性能；尽管反馈高度受限，我们算法的性能与具有详细状态-动作反馈的最先进学习算法（UCB-VI）的性能相当。

TLDR: This paper presents the first efficient bandit learning algorithm for episodic Markov Decision Processes (MDPs) under fully bandit feedback, achieving $\widetilde{O}(\sqrt{T})$ regret and improved bounds for ordered MDPs. Its empirical performance is comparable to state-of-the-art algorithms with detailed feedback in $k$-item prophet inequalities.

简要说明: 该论文提出了一种针对片段式马尔可夫决策过程（MDPs）在完全bandit反馈下的首个高效bandit学习算法，实现了$\widetilde{O}(\sqrt{T})$的遗憾，并且对于有序MDPs获得了改进的边界。在k-item prophet inequalities问题上，其经验性能与具有详细反馈的最先进算法相当。

Authors: Zhengjia Zhuo, Anupam Gupta, Viswanath Nagarajan

Well-Posed KL-Regularized Control via Wasserstein and Kalman-Wasserstein KL Divergences

Abstract (English): Kullback-Leibler divergence (KL) regularization is widely used in reinforcement learning, but it becomes infinite under support mismatch and can degenerate in low-noise limits. Utilizing a unified information-geometric framework, we introduce (Kalman)-Wasserstein-based KL analogues by replacing the Fisher-Rao geometry in the dynamical formulation of the KL with transport-based geometries, and we derive closed-form values for common distribution families. These divergences remain finite under support mismatch and yield a geometric interpretation of regularization heuristics used in Kalman ensemble methods. We demonstrate the utility of these divergences in KL-regularized optimal control. In the fully tractable setting of linear time-invariant systems with Gaussian process noise, the classical KL reduces to a quadratic control penalty that becomes singular as process noise vanishes. Our variants remove this singularity, yielding well-posed problems. On a double integrator and a cart-pole example, the resulting controls outperform KL-based regularization.

摘要（中文）: Kullback-Leibler散度(KL)正则化在强化学习中被广泛使用，但它在支撑集不匹配的情况下会变为无穷大，并在低噪声极限下可能退化。我们利用统一的信息几何框架，通过将KL动态公式中的Fisher-Rao几何替换为基于传输的几何，引入基于(卡尔曼)-Wasserstein的KL类似物，并推导出了常用分布族的闭式解。这些散度在支撑集不匹配的情况下保持有限，并为卡尔曼集成方法中使用的正则化启发式方法提供了几何解释。我们展示了这些散度在KL正则化最优控制中的效用。 在具有高斯过程噪声的线性时不变系统的完全可处理设置中，经典的KL散度简化为二次控制惩罚，该惩罚随着过程噪声的消失而变得奇异。 我们的变体消除了这种奇异性，从而产生了适定问题。 在双积分器和倒立摆的例子中，所得到的控制性能优于基于KL的正则化。

TLDR: This paper introduces Kalman-Wasserstein KL divergences for KL-regularized reinforcement learning, addressing the singularity issue of classical KL divergence in low-noise limits, and demonstrates improved optimal control performance on benchmark tasks.

简要说明: 本文介绍了基于卡尔曼-Wasserstein的KL散度，用于KL正则化强化学习，解决了经典KL散度在低噪声极限下的奇异性问题，并在基准任务上证明了改进的最优控制性能。

Authors: Viktor Stein, Adwait Datar, Nihat Ay

Position: Beyond Model-Centric Prediction -- Agentic Time Series Forecasting

Abstract (English): Time series forecasting has traditionally been formulated as a model-centric, static, and single-pass prediction problem that maps historical observations to future values. While this paradigm has driven substantial progress, it proves insufficient in adaptive and multi-turn settings where forecasting requires informative feature extraction, reasoning-driven inference, iterative refinement, and continual adaptation over time. In this paper, we argue for agentic time series forecasting (ATSF), which reframes forecasting as an agentic process composed of perception, planning, action, reflection, and memory. Rather than focusing solely on predictive models, ATSF emphasizes organizing forecasting as an agentic workflow that can interact with tools, incorporate feedback from outcomes, and evolve through experience accumulation. We outline three representative implementation paradigms -- workflow-based design, agentic reinforcement learning, and a hybrid agentic workflow paradigm -- and discuss the opportunities and challenges that arise when shifting from model-centric prediction to agentic forecasting. Together, this position aims to establish agentic forecasting as a foundation for future research at the intersection of time series forecasting.

摘要（中文）: 时间序列预测传统上被表述为一种以模型为中心、静态且单次完成的预测问题，即将历史观测值映射到未来值。虽然这种范式推动了显著的进步，但它在自适应和多轮设置中显得不足，因为在这些场景下，预测需要信息丰富的特征提取、推理驱动的推断、迭代优化以及随时间的持续适应。在本文中，我们提出智能体式时间序列预测（ATSF）的概念，将预测重新定义为一个由感知、规划、行动、反思和记忆组成的智能体式过程。ATSF不仅关注预测模型，还强调将预测组织为一个智能体式工作流，该工作流可以与工具交互、整合来自结果的反馈，并通过经验积累不断演进。我们概述了三种具有代表性的实现范式——基于工作流的设计、智能体式强化学习，以及混合智能体式工作流范式——并讨论了从以模型为中心的预测转向智能体式预测时出现的机遇和挑战。总而言之，本文旨在将智能体式预测确立为未来时间序列预测交叉领域研究的基础。

TLDR: The paper proposes a shift from model-centric to agentic time series forecasting (ATSF) using perception, planning, action, reflection, and memory, suggesting new paradigms for future research.

简要说明: 该论文提出了一种从以模型为中心的时间序列预测到以代理为中心的预测 (ATSF) 的转变，使用感知、规划、行动、反思和记忆，为未来的研究提出了新的范式。

Authors: Mingyue Cheng, Xiaoyu Tao, Qi Liu, Ze Guo, Enhong Chen

Optimal Sample Complexity for Single Time-Scale Actor-Critic with Momentum

Abstract (English): We establish an optimal sample complexity of $O(ε^{-2})$ for obtaining an $ε$-optimal global policy using a single-timescale actor-critic (AC) algorithm in infinite-horizon discounted Markov decision processes (MDPs) with finite state-action spaces, improving upon the prior state of the art of $O(ε^{-3})$. Our approach applies STORM (STOchastic Recursive Momentum) to reduce variance in the critic updates. However, because samples are drawn from a nonstationary occupancy measure induced by the evolving policy, variance reduction via STORM alone is insufficient. To address this challenge, we maintain a buffer of small fraction of recent samples and uniformly sample from it for each critic update. Importantly, these mechanisms are compatible with existing deep learning architectures and require only minor modifications, without compromising practical applicability.

摘要（中文）: 我们证明了在具有有限状态-动作空间的无限视界折扣马尔可夫决策过程(MDP)中，使用单时间尺度演员-评论家(AC)算法获得一个$ε$-最优全局策略的最优样本复杂度为$O(ε^{-2})$，优于之前最优的$O(ε^{-3})$结果。 我们的方法应用STORM（随机递归动量）来降低评论家更新中的方差。 然而，由于样本是从由演化策略引起的非平稳占用测度中抽取的，仅通过STORM进行方差缩减是不够的。 为了应对这一挑战，我们维护一个包含一小部分最近样本的缓冲区，并在每次评论家更新时从中均匀采样。 重要的是，这些机制与现有的深度学习架构兼容，并且只需要进行少量修改，而不会影响实际应用性。

TLDR: This paper presents a single time-scale actor-critic algorithm with momentum that achieves an improved sample complexity of O(ε^{-2}) compared to prior art for finding ε-optimal policies in Markov decision processes by using a recent sample buffer to address non-stationary occupancy measures.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种基于动量的单时间尺度Actor-Critic算法，与现有技术相比，该算法在Markov决策过程中寻找ε-最优策略时，实现了改进的O(ε^{-2})样本复杂度。论文通过使用最近样本缓冲区来解决非平稳占用度量问题。

Authors: Navdeep Kumar, Tehila Dahan, Lior Cohen, Ananyabrata Barua, Giorgia Ramponi, Kfir Yehuda Levy, Shie Mannor

Provable Cooperative Multi-Agent Exploration for Reward-Free MDPs

Abstract (English): We study cooperative multi-agent reinforcement learning in the setting of reward-free exploration, where multiple agents jointly explore an unknown MDP in order to learn its dynamics (without observing rewards). We focus on a tabular finite-horizon MDP and adopt a phased learning framework. In each learning phase, multiple agents independently interact with the environment. More specifically, in each learning phase, each agent is assigned a policy, executes it, and observes the resulting trajectory. Our primary goal is to characterize the tradeoff between the number of learning phases and the number of agents, especially when the number of learning phases is small. Our results identify a sharp transition governed by the horizon $H$. When the number of learning phases equals $H$, we present a computationally efficient algorithm that uses only $\tilde{O}(S^6 H^6 A / ε^2)$ agents to obtain an $ε$ approximation of the dynamics (i.e., yields an $ε$-optimal policy for any reward function). We complement our algorithm with a lower bound showing that any algorithm restricted to $ρ< H$ phases requires at least $A^{H/ρ}$ agents to achieve constant accuracy. Thus, we show that it is essential to have an order of $H$ learning phases if we limit the number of agents to be polynomial.

摘要（中文）: 我们研究了无奖励探索情境下的合作多智能体强化学习，其中多个智能体联合探索一个未知的 MDP 以学习其动力学（不观察奖励）。我们聚焦于表格型有限水平 MDP，并采用分阶段学习框架。在每个学习阶段，多个智能体独立地与环境交互。更具体地，在每个学习阶段，每个智能体被分配一个策略，执行该策略并观察产生的轨迹。我们的主要目标是刻画学习阶段数量与智能体数量之间的权衡，尤其是在学习阶段数量较少的情况下。 我们的结果识别出由水平时间步长 $H$ 决定的一个急剧转变。当学习阶段数量等于 $H$ 时，我们提出一种计算高效的算法，该算法仅使用 $\tilde{O}(S^6 H^6 A / ε^2)$ 个智能体就能获得动力学的 $ε$ 近似（即，对于任何奖励函数，产生一个 $ε$-最优策略）。我们用一个下界来补充我们的算法，该下界表明，任何限制在 $ρ < H$ 阶段的算法至少需要 $A^{H/ρ}$ 个智能体才能达到恒定精度。因此，我们表明，如果我们将智能体数量限制为多项式级别，那么拥有 $H$ 数量级的学习阶段是至关重要的。

TLDR: This paper studies multi-agent reinforcement learning in reward-free MDPs, demonstrating a trade-off between the number of learning phases and the number of agents required to learn the environment dynamics. They provide an efficient algorithm requiring a polynomial number of agents when the number of phases equals the horizon and a theoretical lower bound when this condition is not met.

简要说明: 本文研究了无奖励MDPs中的多智能体强化学习，展示了学习阶段的数量与学习环境动态所需的智能体数量之间的权衡。他们提出了一种高效算法，当阶段数等于时间范围时，需要多项式数量的智能体，并在不满足此条件时提供了理论下限。

Authors: Idan Barnea, Orin Levy, Yishay Mansour

Before Autonomy Takes Control: Software Testing in Robotics

Abstract (English): Robotic systems are complex and safety-critical software systems. As such, they need to be tested thoroughly. Unfortunately, robot software is intrinsically hard to test compared to traditional software, mainly since the software needs to closely interact with hardware, account for uncertainty in its operational environment, handle disturbances, and act highly autonomously. However, given the large space in which robots operate, anticipating possible failures when designing tests is challenging. This paper presents a mapping study by considering robotics testing papers and relating them to the software testing theory. We consider 247 robotics testing papers and map them to software testing, discussing the state-of-the-art software testing in robotics with an illustrated example, and discuss current challenges. Forming the basis to introduce both the robotics and software engineering communities to software testing challenges. Finally, we identify open questions and lessons learned.

摘要（中文）: 机器人系统是复杂且安全性至关重要的软件系统，因此需要进行彻底的测试。不幸的是，与传统软件相比，机器人软件本质上更难测试，这主要是因为软件需要与硬件紧密交互，考虑其运行环境中的不确定性，处理扰动，并高度自主地行动。然而，鉴于机器人运行的巨大空间，在设计测试时预测可能的故障极具挑战性。本文通过考虑机器人测试论文并将它们与软件测试理论联系起来，提出了一项映射研究。我们考虑了247篇机器人测试论文并将它们映射到软件测试之上，通过一个示例说明了机器人技术中最新的软件测试技术，并讨论了当前的挑战。这为向机器人和软件工程社区介绍软件测试挑战奠定了基础。最后，我们确定了未解决的问题和经验教训。

TLDR: This paper presents a mapping study of robotics testing papers, relating them to software testing theory to identify challenges and open questions in robotics software testing.

Authors: Nils Chur, Thiago Santos de Moura, Argentina Ortega, Sven Peldszus, Thorsten Berger, Nico Hochgeschwender, Yannic Noller

A Unified Control Architecture for Macro-Micro Manipulation using a Active Remote Center of Compliance for Manufacturing Applications

Abstract (English): Macro-micro manipulators combine a macro manipulator with a large workspace, such as an industrial robot, with a lightweight, high-bandwidth micro manipulator. This enables highly dynamic interaction control while preserving the wide workspace of the robot. Traditionally, position control is assigned to the macro manipulator, while the micro manipulator handles the interaction with the environment, limiting the achievable interaction control bandwidth. To solve this, we propose a novel control architecture that incorporates the macro manipulator into the active interaction control. This leads to a increase in control bandwidth by a factor of 2.1 compared to the state of the art architecture, based on the leader-follower approach and factor 12.5 compared to traditional robot-based force control. Further we propose surrogate models for a more efficient controller design and easy adaptation to hardware changes. We validate our approach by comparing it against the other control schemes in different experiments, like collision with an object, following a force trajectory and industrial assembly tasks.

摘要（中文）: 宏-微操控器结合了具有大工作空间的宏操控器（例如工业机器人）和轻量级、高带宽的微操控器。这使得在保持机器人宽广工作空间的同时，能够实现高度动态的交互控制。传统上，位置控制被分配给宏操控器，而微操控器处理与环境的交互，这限制了可实现的交互控制带宽。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了一种新颖的控制架构，该架构将宏操控器纳入主动交互控制中。与基于主从方法的现有技术架构相比，这使得控制带宽提高了2.1倍，与传统的基于机器人的力控制相比提高了12.5倍。此外，我们提出了替代模型，以便更高效地进行控制器设计并轻松适应硬件更改。我们通过在不同的实验中将其与其他控制方案进行比较来验证我们的方法，例如与物体碰撞、跟随力轨迹和工业装配任务。

TLDR: This paper presents a novel control architecture for macro-micro manipulators using an active Remote Center of Compliance, achieving significant bandwidth improvements in interaction control for manufacturing applications, validated through various experiments.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种使用主动遥控柔顺中心的宏微型机械臂的新型控制架构，在制造应用中实现了交互控制带宽的显着提升，并通过各种实验进行了验证。

Authors: Patrick Frank, Christian Friedrich

Tilt-Ropter: A Novel Hybrid Aerial and Terrestrial Vehicle with Tilt Rotors and Passive Wheels

Abstract (English): In this work, we present Tilt-Ropter, a novel hybrid aerial-terrestrial vehicle (HATV) that combines tilt rotors with passive wheels to achieve energy-efficient multi-mode locomotion. Unlike existing under-actuated HATVs, the fully actuated design of Tilt-Ropter enables decoupled force and torque control, greatly enhancing its mobility and environmental adaptability. A nonlinear model predictive controller (NMPC) is developed to track reference trajectories and handle contact constraints across locomotion modes, while a dedicated control allocation module exploits actuation redundancy to achieve energy-efficient control of actuators. Additionally, to enhance robustness during ground contact, we introduce an external wrench estimation algorithm that estimates environmental interaction forces and torques in real time. The system is validated through both simulation and real-world experiments, including seamless air-ground transitions and trajectory tracking. Results show low tracking errors in both modes and highlight a 92.8% reduction in power consumption during ground locomotion, demonstrating the system's potential for long-duration missions across large-scale and energy-constrained environments.

摘要（中文）: 本文介绍了一种新型的空陆混合飞行器（HATV）Tilt-Ropter，它结合了倾转旋翼和被动轮，实现了节能的多模式运动。与现有的欠驱动HATV不同，Tilt-Ropter的全驱动设计使其能够实现解耦的力和力矩控制，从而大大提高了其机动性和环境适应性。我们开发了一种非线性模型预测控制器（NMPC）来跟踪参考轨迹并处理跨运动模式的接触约束，同时，一个专门的控制分配模块利用驱动冗余来实现对执行器进行节能控制。此外，为了增强地面接触过程中的鲁棒性，我们引入了一种外部wrench估计算法，用于实时估计环境交互作用力和力矩。通过仿真和真实世界的实验验证了该系统，包括无缝的空地转换和轨迹跟踪。结果表明，该系统在两种模式下都具有较低的跟踪误差，并强调了地面运动过程中功耗降低了92.8%，证明了该系统在大型和能源受限环境中执行长时任务的潜力。

TLDR: The paper introduces Tilt-Ropter, a fully actuated hybrid aerial-terrestrial vehicle with tilt rotors and passive wheels, demonstrating energy-efficient locomotion through a novel control system and real-world experiments.

Authors: Ruoyu Wang, Xuchen Liu, Zongzhou Wu, Zixuan Guo, Wendi Ding, Ben M. Chen

Towards Autonomous Instrument Tray Assembly for Sterile Processing Applications

Abstract (English): The Sterile Processing and Distribution (SPD) department is responsible for cleaning, disinfecting, inspecting, and assembling surgical instruments between surgeries. Manual inspection and preparation of instrument trays is a time-consuming, error-prone task, often prone to contamination and instrument breakage. In this work, we present a fully automated robotic system that sorts and structurally packs surgical instruments into sterile trays, focusing on automation of the SPD assembly stage. A custom dataset comprising 31 surgical instruments and 6,975 annotated images was collected to train a hybrid perception pipeline using YOLO12 for detection and a cascaded ResNet-based model for fine-grained classification. The system integrates a calibrated vision module, a 6-DOF Staubli TX2-60L robotic arm with a custom dual electromagnetic gripper, and a rule-based packing algorithm that reduces instrument collisions during transport. The packing framework uses 3D printed dividers and holders to physically isolate instruments, reducing collision and friction during transport. Experimental evaluations show high perception accuracy and statistically significant reduction in tool-to-tool collisions compared to human-assembled trays. This work serves as the scalable first step toward automating SPD workflows, improving safety, and consistency of surgical preparation while reducing SPD processing times.

摘要（中文）: 无菌处理和配送（SPD）部门负责在手术间隙对手术器械进行清洁、消毒、检查和组装。人工检查和准备器械托盘既耗时又容易出错，而且经常容易发生污染和器械损坏。在这项工作中，我们提出了一种全自动机器人系统，用于将手术器械分拣并结构化地装入无菌托盘，重点关注SPD组装阶段的自动化。我们收集了一个包含31种手术器械和6,975个标注图像的定制数据集，用于训练一个混合感知流水线，该流水线使用YOLO12进行检测，并使用基于ResNet的级联模型进行细粒度分类。该系统集成了校准的视觉模块、带有定制双电磁夹具的6自由度Staubli TX2-60L机械臂，以及基于规则的打包算法，该算法可减少运输过程中器械之间的碰撞。打包框架使用3D打印的隔板和支架来物理隔离器械，从而减少运输过程中的碰撞和摩擦。实验评估表明，与人工组装的托盘相比，该系统具有高感知精度，并且工具之间的碰撞在统计学上得到了显著减少。这项工作是实现SPD工作流程自动化、提高手术准备的安全性和一致性，以及缩短SPD处理时间的可扩展第一步。
